Bheetar Deepak Jala Ke, Bahar Andher Jaaye
Jo Jyoti Bhitar Paawe, So Param Pad Paaye

Jo Prem Ke Bina Padhe, Soi Maaya Ka Maan

Ghar ghar jhagda kar gaye, ek raah na dikhaaye

Dwaar band kar namaaz kare, padosi ko taj jaaye

Chahe kuraan chahe ved, sab khaak ho jaaye

Ganga nahaaye kya kare, paap ganthi bandh laaye

Jaat paat ke bhed mein, paani bhi na aaye

Satsang ki boond paan kare, maila man nirmal hoye
Ek boond samundar ho mile, phir pehchane naa koye

Bina sangat gyaan nahi, andha so bhul jaaye
Deep bin tej ujal nahi, nadi bin jal na paaye

Sadhu sangat me aaya kar, paap taje bhav bhool
Samundar me mil gayi nadi, bhooli apni mool

Kabira satsang metha lage, vish kera bich khoy
Sant ki vaani amrit hai, piye sant sam hoy

Satsang agni loha tare, paap pal mein dhul jaaye
Jaise kanchan aag mein, suddha roop dikhlaaye

Sant sangat ki reet hai, paani jaisi nirmal
Maila laagat hi paaniye, dhoi de saba mal

Bhavsagar tare sangat nadi, guru naav hai khevat

Gyaan Deep Jalaave Antar Me, Maalaa Jaap Na Koye
Jo Bheetar Lok Pahchaane, Baahar Se Kya Hoye

Naav Gyaan Ki Saagar Me, Jo Chale Tin Paar
Antar Hi Base Bhagavaan Ko, Nahin Koi Duja Dwaar

Pandit Bane Sab Pothi Se, Antar Na Hua Ujaaye
Jo Bheetar Gyaan Na Jaga Le, Janam Sada Jaaye

Ahankar Gyaan Ko Maar Daarai, Mann Bada Bharam Jaal
Jo Bheetar Se Mail Dhoye, Hoye Nija Gyaan Ujaal

Guru Mile To Gyaan Milai, Bin Guru Andhera Raat
Jo Antar Ke Deep Jalaai, Paave Gyaan Ki Baat

Saagar Bhaav Ki Naav Hai, Gyaan Hi Leve Paar
Jo Antar Ki Najar Na Rakhe, Phire Bhaari Baar

Chahu Ved Puraan Padhaai, Gyaan Na Bheetar Aaye
Ek Pal Jo Chit Bheetar Dharai, Sansaar Bharam Jaaye

Mann Kahaan Se Aaya Hai, Kahaa Ko Jaayega

Jo Bin Gyaan Ke Jeevat Hai, Bar Bar Mar Jaaye

Jo Antar Me Jaan Paave, Sada Hi Sukh Paaye

Maan Ke Kapaat Khul Jaai, Paave Nija Sansaar

Panch Tatva Ke Mel Se, Ye Sab Kachhu Banaaye
Gyaan Bina Na Jaani Kachhu, Jaaninhaar Samaaye

Duniya Ke Bharam Tyag Kar, Ek Gyaan Udaar
Antar Prem Jagaai Ke, Paavai Bhava Paar

Kabira Maan Ek Pakhand Hai, Gyaan Se Door Ujaaye
Jo Maan Mhare Gyaan Jare, Sada Hi Sukh Paaye

Gyaan Kee Naav Saagar Me, Laage Bhaav Ke Bhaar
Antar Deep Bina Jare, Dubi Jaai Sansaar

Ek Gyaan Ki Roti Jo, Bheetar Hi Pakaaye
Jo Bahar Dhooni Machaai, Mann Kaa Bharam Na Jaaye

Gyaan Ki Kathni Bahut Hai, Karni Mein Gahan Bhed
Jo Kehat Kabahu Kar Naahin, Phire Janam Ke Khed

Gyaan Deep Antar Jalaai, Naam Lai Jo Jaap
Jo Bheetar Preme Laage, Toote Sab Janam Taap

Bahut Kiyaa Sankalp Re, Gyaan Na Aaye Baar
Ek Pal Jo Chit Antar Dharai, Kho Jaaye Sab Bhaar

Darpan Maila Dekh Kar, Chhabi Na Dikhlaaye
Jo Antar Dhoye Tin Dekhai, Gyaan Deep Jalaaye

Sab Kachhu Tere Bheetar Hai, Baahar Khoj Na Maan
Jo Antar Gyaan Jagaai Ke, Paave Nija Samaan

Chahu Disha Mein Gyaan Dhundhe, Gyaan Base Antar Dhaar
Jo Palat Ke Bheetar Dekhe, Paave Gyaan Udaar

Chaar Ved Chaubees Puraan, Sabhi Ko Padh Sakaam
Jo Antar Gyaan Na Jagiya, Bandhi Rahe Saba Kaam

Samajh Na Aave Gyaan Ko, Jo Maan Ka Gulaam
Bin MaaN Ke Gyaan Prakaashai, Paavai Santosh Dhaam

Gyaan Ka Ek Ratan Hai, Jo Bheetar Jalaaye
Sau Saal Ke Paap Ko, Ek Pal Mein Mitaaye

Mann Ko Maare Gyaan Jare, Tahi Kaho Gunaaye
Jo Maan Ko Bachaai Phire, Maarat Janam Aaye

Gyaan Bina Man Matwara, Bhava Saagar Mein Khaaye
Jo Antar Tatva Jaan Liya, Paar Sada Tin Aaye

Gyaan Bina Jo Saadh Bane, Kaahe Ko Saadh
Antar Gyaan Jagaai Jinhain, Paar Kare Sab Baadh

Jo Poochhe Gyaan Ki Baat, Kahat Naahin Daam
Gyaan Tabahi Milat Hai, Jab Hoi Gur Kaam

Nainan Ko Bheetar Daar, Gyaan Darpan Laaye
Jo Chhabi Antar Dekhai, Maya Baahar Jaaye

Kaahe Ko Dhoondhe Paar Ko, Paar Base Antar Maahi

Gyaan Deep Jo Bujh Gayo, Jeevan Andhiyaara
Diyo Jalaai Jo Bheetar, Ujaara Sansaara

Antar Gyaan Prakaash Kar, Naam Japai Samaaye
Jo Bheetar Preme Laage, Toote Sab Bandhan Jaaye

Guru Ke Sumaran Gyaan Hai, Bin Guru Andher
Jo Guru Pad Ko Dhyaan Karai, Katai Janam Ke Fer

Deepak Jyoti Jalaaye Rakh, Tel Saansan Ke Saath
Samay Bitaaya Jaaye Phir, Kahi Na Poori Baat

Nindiya Neend Bhulaa De, Jag Le Din Chaar
Kaal Aawe To Maangata, Dekhe Haath Pasaar

Aalas Chhod Samaal Le, Tel Rakha Kar Saath
Samay Ki Aankh Jhapat Mein, Jaawe Sab Ke Saath

Shvas Ki Dor Chali Gayi, To Phir Na Mil Paaye
Jyon Bhaap Ude Aakaash, Tyon Samay Beet Jaaye

Baalapan Gayo Javaani, Javaani Gayi Bujh Aankh
Samay Ki Chakki Chalti, Koi Na Rokat Saankh

Eka Pal Men Yug Bite, Ham Na Paahat Paas
Deepak Tel Samapt Bina, Hove Sabhi Udaas

Tan Ko Mehl Banaya Hai, Maati Ka Haath Thaher
Samay Ki Aandhi Aavegi, Udegi Chhat Pather

Khaat Khaas Kharach Kiye, Din Rain Naam Bina
Samay Chor Hathaile, Udaaya Sab Dina

Deepak Bina Tel Ke, Kaun Dekhe Baat
Svans Bina Tan Chale Na, Samay Chale Ke Saath

Din Rain Bitaaye Araam, Sansar Ke Kaaj
Samay Daur Aaya Kaal Ka, Laga Na Haath Raaj

Pathar Ko Puje Firat, Samay Beetat Jaaye
Apne Ghar Ka Deepak, Kyu Na Tu Jalaaye

Deepak Tale Tel Nahin, Jyoti Beeti Jaaye
Samay Tale Gaanth Nahin, Chadhat Koi Na Paaye

Janam Gayo Javaani Gayi, Budhaapa Hoya Aaye
Samay Ke Chhaya Aangan Pe, Kaal Jaaga Jaaye

Baras Baras Bitaaye Gaye, Paani Ke Bulaabul

Deepak Jaisi Jeevan Jyoti, Kshan Kshan Tel Ghate

Samay Binaa Maangat Hi, Kaal Let Udaati

Kahe Kabir Yeh Samay Bhai, Kshan Ka Bichhau

Maya Ki Laag Laagi Hai, Sab Jeev Andh Hoye
Dhan Joban Aur Kul Ki, Maya Phansa Sab Koye

Maya Chaaya Hai Jaise, Chhaya Kabhu Na Raaye
Saach Jo Chaahai Paave, Maya Se Man Bisaraaye

Moho Bada Maya Badi, Dono Bharam Jagave
Kahe Kabira Ram Bina, Daras Na Koyi Pave

Dhan Daulat Kul Ka Ghamand, Maya Ka Ye Pasaar
Ek Din Makdi Jaala, Toot Gaya Sansaar

Maya Basar Kar Liyo, Man Maakan Ko Saaj
Ant Samay Jholi Khali, Bin Haath Kachhu Na Kaaj

Maya Ke Roop Niraale, Sundar Shringaar
Jaise Kagaj Ki Naav, Paani Mein Ho Bisaar

Ant Samay Harega, Milega Na Paar

Guru Se Jo Na Seekhat, Jaat Ka Abhimaan
Kabeer Kahe Aisa Chela, Gavaya Aapan Jaan

Man ke mandir mein dhup jalta, bahar mandir dhool bhara
Riti‑raiva se na koi achha, mann ki roshni hai savara

Nangla jata karta tha jisme phool, dharti ke bhool se bhara
Jotho paav ki riti kari, sukh ka phool bane kaanta

Guru ke piche bhagta janga, pare roop dharm ki bhool
Mitti ki thaali mein sannata, jaise katora mein ful

Riti‑riwaz ki dori ghaati, har koi usko jode
Par sachcha bhagwan chhupa, jise bhool na koi nodde

Jhooth ka jal phir piye, paani ka marg bhi pyara
Phool ki tarah vadhe sabse, kaanta lagta vira

Mandir ki shobha, galiyon ki dhool, sab rang hi rang
Par jiska dhyaan man ki lath pe, wo hi sookh ka sang

Riti‑riwaj ki baat mein, bhakti ka rang chhupa
Phir bhi bhagwan milta hai, deta na bhaka dhupa

Bhoole bhool bhool ke mitra ki, jagat ka dhakan
Phool ka sukh, kaanta ka dukh, sabko sahab dhak

Riti‑riwaz ki lakeer utre, dhool se bhare pad
Par sahi raah wo jo, khud ki jaan ko chad

Mandir ke pichhe bahar, bhakton ki dhop padi
Kaanta ghumata hai, phool se bhula bhadi

Riti‑riwaz ka dikhawa, jasoos ki pichli raah
Sach ki chhanbeen mein, phool bhi khil utha

Sabpu ki bhakti, to sathiyan ka maul
Phir bhagwan ghul mil, kaante ko arul

Riti‑kuthali mein bhari roti, dil mein bhari dhoka
Phool ka rang bikta hai, kaanta ki koi roka

Jhuta dharm bhulan ki, dharti ki sadak ghumar
Sacha shabd dhun ke, phoolon ke jahan damar

Riti‑riwaz ki paheli, kaanta ka dula

Phool ki kamai, bhav se sachi neli

Riti‑riwaz ki chiti, sabri se chhum antar
Sahasra phool oonch, kaanta bhi samantar

Nash ki dhun, bhakti ki barish
Phool ka kmal, kaanta ka bhang

Phool se badhkar, kaanta ka pyaan

Jisne gaadi chhodi sab, vo hi sachcha raat ka raas hai

Baans ki lahar mein bhi, shabda ka taal mil jaaye

Jab mile vo bhakti ke, to mann ka bhav manari

To rang badalta nagar ka, har din nayi ambal

Jab sat-sangat ka chaap, mann ko dhone deti

Prem ka gagan, heera ki roshni se bhara,
Jo dekhe usko, andhkaar bhi pyaara.

Patthar ke dil ko dhak aata na sikhaya,
Prem ke paani se sab dhadkan jagaya.

Jiska dhyan prem mein, uska mann chiraag,
Patthar bhi muskuraye, heera bhi laag.

Prem ke bina jeevan, sukh ka patthar,
Jisne maana uska, milta chiraag pyar.

Heera to pyar ka, suraj ka pratidin,
Prem binaa sab, andhera mein bin.

Patthar ki bhari bhari, dhairya ka paimana,
Prem ki leher se phir sab ho jata naya.

Mann ke patthar ko, prem ki baun bulaata,
Heere ki chamak se, har raah jo chhuta.

Prem ke rang se, patthar bhi nagda,
Heere ki barish, dharti pe bhagda.

Patthar ki jali safed, itni hi dushman,
Prem se mil ke, chamak se bhari aaman.

Heera jo khojta, raah prem ki ruti,
Milti jo usko, sab ki dhadak dhuti.

Patthar ki khudgarzi, rangin kuchh badi,
Prem bhara dil, usko sann dharti sade.

Heere ka sang, prem ki baat,
Sukh ki dhun mein, har sukh ka raag.

Patthar ko bhi, ankhon se dekho pyaara,
Prem ki roshni se, asmaan yaara.

Heera ki talaash, prem ki dhun mein,
Vaqt ka sang, dil se koi ghoome.

Patthar ki sogat, prem ki barish,
Dilon ko udaya, teho ki harish.

Heere ki chandi, prem ki paani,
Duni ki bhav, sab jhooth kahani.

Patthar ke pichhe gagan ki lankh,
Prem ke sahare, jeevan ka brahmankh.

Heera ki khoya, prem ki chhavi,
Dil ki dhadkan se rang bhavi.

Patthar jadiyan, jalti aag se,
Prem ke sakoon se, hoti hi na bhag se.

Heere ki rekha, prem hai sandhi,
Jaisa bhool ko, aata radhi dandi.

Patthar ki thandak, prem ki dhun,
Har raah se nishana, mulya ki gun.

Heere ki haad, prem ka sahara,
Mann ka bhandar, har dhara.

Patthar ki chadi, prem ka nasal,
Raat ki bahar, sukh ka ishal.

Heera jab mil jaaye, prem ki dhar,
Saari duniya mein, ho roshni ka sahar.

Patthar ki bhool, prem se jod,
Gnostic kadam, bhav ki krod.

Heere ki chamak, prem ki ganga,
Bandhan sab phir, bhul gaye pana.

Patthar ki baithi, tuti dil ki dori,
Prem ke teer se mila ajab khori.

Heere ki roop, prem ka ras,
Sookhi thandi, kundli ka as.

Patthar jaisa kathin, prem ka pyara,
Jab mil jaye, ban jata sahara.

Heere ka bhaav, prem ki chaadar,
Mann ki gaadi, har ek baar.

Patthar ki hifazat, prem ki aag,
Saare sansaar ko, dhoop ka bag.

Heere ki raah, prem ki gan,
Jald zarur jaye, dhundhi ki jam.

Patthar ki nishani, prem ka geet,
Mann ki chaanv, bhul jaaye raat.

Heere ki pichkari, prem ka jor,
Kavita ki tarah, dharti ke chor.

Patthar ka gosht, prem ki barbat,
Dil ko milte hi, ho jata sat.

Heere ki khich, prem ki mithas,
Mool ko dhundhna, kuchh nirvas.

Patthar ka bal, prem ka shiwar,
Sab thek milta, asman ki baari.

Heere ki galiyoon, prem ki veer,
Sabhi ko sukhi, ek hi jeer.

Patthar ko dhool, prem ka swam,
Raftaar se nikalta, sabhi anjam.

Heere ki shakti, prem ka dhyan,
Jeene ko dhoop, har din ka gyan.

Patthar ki mitti, prem ki chamak,
Har kadam mila, milke dharam.

Heere ki bal, prem ka dhyan,
Gyaan ka nirmal, him nashan.

Patthar ke ghan, prem ka shrey,
Ekaant ka suk, jhaag tawdey.

Heere ki padi, prem ka gath,
Manush ki bhakti, unka chet.

Patthar ko patan, prem saji roshan,
Mann ki aag, sabko jhilmil.

Heere ki jubani, prem ki saath,
Sath hi bhool, dharm ki baat.

Patthar ki gheen, prem ke uchar,
Jeevan ki tarah, khoon ka vaar.

Heere ki baans, prem ki pratibha,
Mann ki bhool se, milti naya.

Patthar ki bhari, prem ki ehsaas,
Jab mil jaye, sab ko disha paas.

Heere ki sagar, prem ka andaaz,
Har din se paani, manav ki ghaz.

Patthar ki roopi, prem ki aashir,
Mann ki baat, dhara ka dhur.

Jab dhool udi hawa mein, to raja bhi ho jata sang

Seep ki darcha, din ki reet,
Mann mein bhoot, jaise sookshot phit

Jyaan ki srishti, dhyan ki aasaan

Mann ki dhara, shukran ki dhokho

Patang ko pakad, anek dinan

Barish ki dhoon, ghan ki lalt,
Mann ki ghabra, ras aur shal

Mann ki aadh, shire khooni

Pashu ki tarah, bhakti ke shir,
Mann ki bicy, bhakti ki mithi

Radh ke rec, bhav ki liti,
Mann ke moti, raat ki fiti

Udaas ki roshni, jaane ke sang,
Mann ki thermal, mile shait ko bang

Khan ke Rani, man ki keen,
Sukoon ki dar, sahara ki dhun

Hawa ke deed, dharohar ki seer,
Mann vyela, rah ki cahsar.

Guru ki baat sun, badal barse sukh ka paani
Jise bhool gaya haath, wo aakash se bhi anjaani

Jab guru ki jhalak mile, to barsaat bhi muskuraye
Jo na samjhe uski baat, swayam se hi bhatak jaye

Guru aag ka dhoop hai, jo dhuaan badal banta
Jo usko dhyan se dekhe, use barasati chhanta

Man ka bijli gire, jab guru ki dhun sun le
Barsaat se bhi meethas milti, jo uska gyaan chale

Guru ki shiksha baadal ki tarah, har rang mein dhale
Jo na dhare uski kripa, voh sukh se anjaane rahe

Guru ka ashirvad baras, jeevan ki mitti bhigaye
Bina uske sowk se, sab kahin bhi chhup jaye

Guru ka paigham barood jaisa, barsaat ka sher hai
Jo samjhe uska raaz, usse mil jaata sukh ke per

Guru bina raaste andhera, jaise raat ka badal
Jo uski roshni se roshan, har din uska kagal

Guru ki baat bhari, jaise barish ki boonden
Jo sun le uska aashirvad, sukh ki ho dharohar

Guru ki chaap chhadi, jaise badal ki dhuni
Jisne usko pehchana, usko milti anadhuni

Guru ke bina sawal, jaise bindi bin ka chashma
Jab barish ki boonden sajti, vahi hoti uski ashma

Guru ki suno raah, barish ka parichay le
Jo uske sang ghoome, uska man mandir ke bhare

Guru takdeer ko likhta, jaise badal likh le paani
Koibh na chhup sake, uski aag ka kahaani

Guru ke ashish baras, jaise methe ki paune
Bina uske jeevan, sab rang se vanij bhune

Guru ke shabda kali, jaise barish ka rangin tal
Jo lagatar sunne, use milti jagat ki tal

Guru ki roshni bari, jaise badal ki kiran
Jise na samajhe koi, voh bhatak paya bhule gagan

Guru ka gyan chhalka, jaise barish ki dhara
Jo dir na ho hamesha, uska man sukh se bhara

Guru ki baat badal jaisi, chhup jaati andharon mein
Jo dhyaan se sune, uska ghar har din dharm mein

Guru ke charan dhare, barish se chhai bhare
Jo uske andar le, use milti jeevan ki paresh

Guru ka padh bhari, jaise badal ki shikayat
Sun le jo uski dhun, lagta anant preet keiyat

Guru ki baat padi, jaise barish ki boondein
Jo na jhuke unki, unke akash ki poondein

Guru ki kadi sun le, jaise badal ki battiyan
Uske anusar chhod, apna mann ko rakh khadiyan

Guru ka marg dharti, barish ki boondein shiksha
Jisko na le iska, patang bhi tut jati vishasha

Guru ki aashirvad dhool, barish ki linda
Jinhen usne chuna, uski roshni andaaz ninda

Guru ki dhun baras, jaise bhanwar ki padi
Jo man ko samjhe, wo panakh ki ladi

Guru ki katha chal, jaise garajti seher
Jaha bhi barish aae, waha uska asar bhair

Guru ki lehar badal, jhankaar se bhare dhare
Uski baat bolti, jaave mann ka sahere

Guru ki goonj taap, barish ke saj ke dhun
Jo uska laaj rakh, usko milti bhoot ki gund

Guru ki gagan chal, jaise badal ki dhara
Jo uski dharaman sun, uski atma dhara

Guru ki chaap rassi, barish se bhari dhul
Jo dhyan se bhare, uska dil chirag pula

Guru ki baat udaas, badal ki chaadar se
Jo jhuk jaaye uske, milti anant yeh geet

Guru ki chetna aage, barish ki bunti
Jise samjhe nahi, uski roshni bhulti

Guru ke anukan samajh, barish ki dhundh roop
Jiska dhahan na ho, uska mann aadi thop

Guru ki roshni chalti, jaise badal ke dhiliy
Jisko rokta na koi, use milti atma ki dhaliy

Guru ke bachan sobha, barish ki pehchaan
Jo sun le baarash, uski dharti rang vaan

Guru ka sath, badal ki aangan mein dhaakad
Jo uske charan dhare, uska kal jeevan saaf

Guru ki bhakti dhara, barish ke badal padhe
Jo anubhav kare, uski atma ke becha

Guru ki shakti nagar, barish ke badal jaye
Jiska dhyaan se prek, use sukh ki tarke

Guru ki Aag, barish ka hota baadal
Jahan buddhi na ho, har sagar artal

Guru ka sang, barish ki dhara se bhara
Jisa joh koi bhi chaahe, milta sab jwala

Guru ke raaste, barish ke chhanvani
Jise pata na aata, uski anekas praani

Guru ki jhalak, barish ki chandni raat
Jise samaj na paaye, se jeevan ka baat

Guru ki kshitija, barish ke sehamti
Jiska gyaan khoj, pana hai raman ki hifati

Sang sang sangati se milti, man ki shanti avyayi
Jab sadhu sang ho saath, paap ka dhuaan mitaayi

Phool jaisa prem jo khila, kaanta na dabata uska
Satguru ki baat sunke, bhoolti hai har bhulaka

Sadhu ki mahfil mein, dhool bhi sone ki chamak
Chhaya jo uski baat ki, sannata bhi bolta bhak

Sadhu ki batein sun ke, man ki ghanti ghaṭta

Jab jhapta hai dukh ka baadal, sangati ka chhatri le
Phool ke jaise khil ja, kaanta se na bhare re

Sadhu sang dhyaan mein, milti hai har bhava

Phool ki tarah pyaar, kaanta ki baat bhool
Satsang ki roshni mein, andhera bhool

Sadhu ki baat ko sun, mann banta aashram

Saans ki gati dhimi, sant ki batein tez
Phool jaise vaani, kaanta ki bhool peh

Satguru ki baat ka rang, har roop ko jhaank
Sadhu sang milke, mann bana ank

Satsang ki chadar me, har baat ka talash

Phool ki laali se, kaanta ka dhowa na bhool

Phool ki mej se, kaanta ka prahar
Sadhu ke sang, man aati alaur

Phool ki thahak me, kaanta ka mag

Sadhu ke sang mil, sab gyaan ke sah

Mann ka darpan phisal jaye to chehre ka noor na dikhaye
Jab tak andhera na mithe, aatma ki roshni bhi chhup jaye

Nadi ke kinare sookhe pankh, mann ki beesi asmaan ko dhare
Jab dhyaan se dekhe sukh ki dhara, uska rang pichhle sapne bhare

Mitti se lipti shakti, mann ka kalash bhara paneer
Darpan ki chaadar se dhak lo, jise dekhkar kathin ho asar

Dhiraj ki roshni gehri, mann ki baadal mein nayi subah
Jab sukhi raat ke baad, sooraj ki kirne chhilti paah

Mann ka kaanch tut jaye toh, bhakton ki awaz sunaye
Jaise shor ki pankhuri, dhyaan ka paayal bhajaye

Mann ki chhanv mein baitho, dhuni se jod lo preet

Kankar se nakshatra jala, mann ki kala ko ujagar

Mann ki ladiya phoolon ki, jag ko rangin hai kahin

Gyaani ka mukhda darpan, darakh dili maangi
Mann ka sawal ke bol ke, kya ehsas nij kaangi

Sahas ki lalkar teen, mann ke janam ki vaat

Mann ki sangeet baam, darpana ke doors se bhanwar
Jab atma ko pukaare hum, rin ka baliya karam

Mann ki baadal chhuri, chandaas ke alowan bhi

Kamyabi ki kiran se, mann chutki chiote dhoole
Jab ache din aate hi, naash ki bhalti ko daraile

Mann ka erta gher hai, chanda comme sahar.
Soch ke gade mein, darpana naa rovar

Mann ki dhundh thandi re, gham ki vipul ke patte
Jab rup ka darpan toote, sangathar ki baat ye kite

Madhu ki patang ud ke, mann ki ladhira anand
Jab man ki kanwal biju, aakash mein lagi ashand

Mann ke paanp mein aag, jab kalpana ki hastak bara
Jab darpan ke chandidar, chhod bhas ke dillike sohna

Mann ki paheli raat, kaanch ke dhoop mein maghai
Jab nayane ki aag se bhajati, arka ki bilkul bhri

Patra ki shadi bola, mann ki matin anpati
Jab darpan ke batti jalti, tano ki hari ho bhati

Mann ka jamuna jaisa, lhaka ghanon ka kahaan
Jab kise chehre se khoj lo, anjaane ka nisha

Mann ko mitti ki deep, dharm ki saujanya laik
Jab darpan ki sukh se, tapak khad aashi kachrit

Aankhon ki baat sahi, mann ki baat ne taash
Aapan darpan mein jo, manaj kyun ne baashi

Mann ki paag dhool, darpan jhoothi ki barf se
Saap ki dehaj ki bhanvus lassi nishat

Mann dhooliyan lage, darpan chhupa rahe padi
Jab roshni ki baaj dekhi, har ghadi sahabadi

Mann ke raag baadh, baithak ki sambhav khole,
Kanchi ki baath urja, jivan ki saptah moth le

Mann ke kalash boondh, darpan se khilta anur

Mann ke aalam mein hansa, sitro ki dhoop jee
Darpana ki bhariyo se, hazaar raat mil hi

Mann ka haath bandh, kangi se karo suhaga,
Darpan ki wo rang dekh, jag sooo goo agla

Mann ka tan bhoot, darpan ki tarah hogi tare kaj
Sukhi anjae ke sapne is, ashk viyo ka jad

Mann ki sakul vaadi, darpan ke dhwaj nayi
Jab bhool ki teeji fire, bhakti ghurkar doe gay

Kavete pahi me josh, anjaaan se hi bhaira

Mann ko seedha nek, darpan ki madhurchin pahadi
Saajh ke nadi se chhaye, jeevan ka sadhas chhai

Mann pe badi calla, darban ke do,
Kriti ka bandho face ki jaap, juhuri gaya ragi

Bhava ke andhera, mann ka dhyan pangda karo
Darpan ki roshni se, phir kayi saathi chaho

Mann ki dhuni mein her, kaanch ke shobhe bhav so
Jab gav ki ghalat, bhanashri aag se rang sale

Mann ko jhaankaa se, darpan ki mási tal dekh
Buddha ka pragati, man ki mahima aap de

Jab ekshri ke ashri se, mil se man dhany ghar

Jab deepak asmaan, chhoti se bhavik phidane

Mann ki dhun sattar, darpan ki spazik ke dung

Samay ki kiran se raat dhoop ban jati,
Patthar bhi gehun ko roti ke roop mein samjhai

Kal ki chaadar dhul jaye to aaj ki loh se,
Heere jaisa dhairya banta, bhool na bhool

Samay ki dhool se paani bhi sookhti,
Jab tak thikhe, tab tak dharma khila

Patthar ki zindagi, khud ko patthar mat samajh,
Samay ki lahar se toot kar, phir se chamak

Heere ki mahanta waqt ke aage jhukti,
Jo na chhode is ghadi ko, paaye anant sukh

Samay ke phool khilte hain anant mulk mein,
Jise pakde patthar, vo kaye khud ko jhalak

Patthar ki dehleez par samay ki chaal,
Jahan se guzre nagar bas jhaank laya

Heere jaise sodhe bhav, samay ke dana,
Na ghana bante bina bhakti ke nishana

Kshan ki lahron pe patthar bhi girte,
Jab bhul jaye shraddha, samay pichhe phirte

Samay ki tezi se paatum ki baat,
Patthar bhi pyaasa mehka jaata

Heere ki chamak se dhaai dhaan,
Samay ki baat sabko roshan bana

Patthar ki dhara behti nadi jaisi,
Samay ki dhaar mein doobte jaisi

Saaz samay ke, heere ki taan,
Patthar ki dhun me bhakti ka maan

Samay ki bonde kat-te bheed,
Patthar bhi dhalte hain, jab koi sathi cheed

Heere ki wo baat anant,
Samay na roke uski abhivyakti ka chant

Zindagi ka patthar, samay ka ghaas,
Jab bhool jayen yog ko, sab ho jaaye raas

Samay ki lehar, patthar ki dam,
Heere ki bhakti, mann ko aasm

Patthar se bada kavach, samay ka dande,
Jabba chhut jaye sab, to dhruv rahe andre

Heere ka ratan, samay ki paathshala,
Patthar ki mantar, bhulaye na bhala

Samay ki sikka, patthar ki gaadi,
Heere ki roshni se hi milti yadi

Patthar ki ladhi, samay ki beed,
Heere ka sahara baje birud

Samay ki batakh dam, patthar ki dhun,
Jab heere ki yaad ho, milti sulahi ki dhoon

Patthar ke sang, samay ki aad,
Heere ki gati mein milti pratishtha

Samay ka shaasna, patthar ki chaal,
Heere ki pratibha se hoti asaal

Patthar ki tarah hum bhi dekhna,
Samay ki chaal ko kabhi bachana nahi

Heere ki sung dhyan, samay se baat,
Patthar nahi, jeevan ko roopmit

Samay ki nagri, patthar ki gali,
Heere ki roshni se milti bhakti ki teli

Patthar ki mitti se samay chuk,
Heere ki aag me jalti dhairya ki nukt

Samay ki dhoop ko ghum na karo,
Patthar ko dhyaan se paise rona

Heere ki baat suno, samay pare,
Patthar pada, dhun kismet ke sahare

Samay ki sawar, patthar se asar,
Heere ki bhakti se milti utsaah

Patthar ki chhaap samay ne chhodi,
Heere ki roshni mein aaradhna rodi

Samay ki saja, patthar ki suhaag,
Heere ki ghum ko dekh lo bhaag

Patthar ke sang vishwas, samay ke krodh,
Heere ki ashk se bhara din rosh

Samay ki lajawaab, patthar ki chhaap,
Heere ka aaj din bhajan samapa

Patthar ki chhounka par zamana,
Samay ki dhara sun ne kabir ke ganna

Heere ki bhulaat ka vikas,
Samay ki bhoomi par raat ka bis

Patthar ke dhar se nahi,
Samay ke sahare milti man ki bhins

Heere ki tarah anadi, samay ke tal,
Patthar ki dhun se agni jale sab dhyal

Samay ki doodh, patthar ki raak,
Heere ki aaj bhi shabd baksh

Patthar ki baat na phikli,
Samay ki dhun mein bhakti bhadli

Heere ki dhvani, samay ka pit,
Patthar ki chut ki dhup se ght

Samay ki ghadi, patthar ke ran,
Heere ki bhajan se badi ho ghan

Patthar ki dharam, samay ki kosh,
Heere ki roshni se mil jatna hosh

Samay ki dhool ko dhare,
Patthar ka darshan badi bikher

Heere ka javab samay ki ram,
Patthar ka shukra ko daldam

Samay ke fal, patthar ki gaj,
Heere ki ranjhan, aata bars ko rahaij

Patthar ke rang, samay ki gol,
Heere ki haath badi dhar ko bol

Samay ka nash, patthar ka atm,
Heere ki rakhe se bhag ka bhatm

Patthar ki dore, samay ki bhari,
Heere ki raa, dhyan ko mahri

Samay ki raat, patthar ki sujit,
Heere ki prakash se banta parit

Patthar ka dhair, samay ki jhal,
Heere ki shanti se badi bhala

Samay ki dhiri, patthar ki rahi,
Heere ki bhakt se milti mahahi

Patthar ka koi rehh, samay ka fas,
Heere ki soch se milti saras

Samay ki chaav, patthar ki raha,
Heere ki pehchaan se man mein baha

Patthar ka ora, samay ki boond,
Heere ki dewan se shabd roond

Samay ki rebha, patthar ki chhal,
Heere ki ateet se milti pal

Patthar ki jhari, samay ki badal,
Heere ki bhakti se khilti niral

Samay ki teeh, patthar ki sojat,
Heere ki aawaz se nitya sajat

Phul ki mala pe mala, daan diyo aaj vi khaas
Par jo chhanv mein baithkar, dharm ki baat kare bhas

Sindoor ki baali, riti ki dhoop ka sath
Jab jeevan ka phool, ban jaye kaanta ki raat

Mandir ki deewar, laathi se dhare shikhar
Jahaan bhakshan se ho, garb ka pakka vishar

Khandan ki jaati, rang se bhari dhool
Phir bhi uljhan me, prem ko dhoondhe pool

Riti ka rangmanch, jhula jhuta sukh ka rang
Par usmein ghoome har koi, dharm ki bhang

Madhur bhajan ki dhar, paani ke jhaank
Dil ke talab mein, kaante ki baash

Kapra dhosh ke, nayan ki dhul bicha
Jaane bina dhoop, dhoke se bhara vicha

Rashan ki thāl, ghee ki basti chandni
Par raat ke andhe, lalkar de vishesh bhikshani

Pahchan na jaaye, ke phool bhi kagaz ka mai
Sutr dhool se likha, shravan ki bhirbhoj bhai

Dukan ki ghanti, dharm ki ghanti ki talwar
Naam ka bhakt, aage se e.g. prabhu ki haar

Mitti ki bhinnata, sukh ka dhage na mitra
Kaanta ke beech, bas yaad ka chitr

Charan dhool lagi, bhav se vahi bandhan
Phir bhi jhoothi baat, man ki kaavya dhvani

Shubh laal kapda, lahron ki samundar mein
Phool ki kasr mein, kaanta churade seedar

Rangroop ki moorti, raat ki ki garaj
Manav ko dikh se, chayan ki tushaaj

Lachak bhakti ka, shājā ki bhūt
Phir bhi dhvani dhokar, bhakti ki path

Kadam se kadam tak, gēn kā raso
Phir bhi niraash, ye phūl vishit raaso

Bhoot ki baithak, dharm ki sikhaye poṭa
Kalp se kaanta, asmani brahm ki bōṭa

Pyar ki rava, baans ki baaraat
Kirako ki jaati, sudhari hui aat

Dikhawe ka naksh, vashikaran ka riva
Patra ka phool, phir bhi katari ka hiva

Saathi ke sajati, hui mugdili koti
Kintu bhugol ki baat, jhuthki ek dhoti

Moh ke phool bhare, jahan ka jawaab
Kanta ki nadi se, bhoola dharmi pataab

Gagan ka ghoomar, rang ki amaan
Dil ki dhool le, dharm ka jeevan

Ghanti ki dhun, talwar ki dhun
Swar se jaati bi ko, dhoop ka safoon

Mouthan ki pisha, paon ki rangin
Gulab ki phool, jhalak me malam

Jyada kar de sakaa, har shakl
Mann ki loha hunar, miet ke sujali

Ahankar ki chhadi, aag ka bhanwar,
Jab ghar ki deewar toot jaye, tabhi samajh aata hai sukh.

Dwaar ke dhoose waale, peeth par bhari bhool,
Jab aata hai mann ka aab, to darwaza khul jaata hai.

Ghanti ki aawaz se, na koi sajta ghar,
Sukhi bhav se hi banta hai, dil ka anivar.

Ahankar ki thali, bhari saarik kar,
Jab kholte hain dwaar, tabhi milti hai barik.

Ghar ki chhat par milti hai dhool,
Mann ki aatish se na koi ghoor.

Darwaza band ho, to chalta hai rahasya,
Jab ego khul jaye, to milti sabko sharan.

Ghode ki dori, kabhi na thamti,
Mann ke darwaze, jab khulenge, to aasha banti.

Ghar ki ghanti batati sabko,
Ahankar se chhuta, to milti hai roshni.

Darwaza kahin se na jhank,
Mann ke ehsan ko sabse anerk.

Mitti ki deewar, dhool se bhari,
Jab ahankar ki chadar uda, to milti jai.

Ghar ki khidki se dhoop ka kehr,
Jab ego ko mitaye, to mangal har.

Darwaza ki taali baje,
Jab pyaar se dab kare, to aasha sajje.

Ghar ke bhandar me, prem ki batti,
Ego ko bujha, to milti hai saathi.

Darwaza tod kar bhula,
Mann ke paap ki ghadi.

Ghar ke aangan me, phool khile,
Ahankar ka dukh, kabhi na mile.

Darwaza jab band ho, dhundla roshni,
Mann ki padiya, jab milti hai.

Ghar ki dehleez se, aasha ke kadam,
Ahankar ka bojh, kha jaye jail.

Darwaza dhak le, chhal se,
Jab mann ka saara, dil ki dhul mein.

Ghar ki chhavi, saaf-suthri,
Ego ki mithi, kabhi na bhare.

Darwaza ka har rang, aashirvaad,
Ego ki shanti, sab miyaan.

Ghar ki diwar, bhari patthar,
Jab ahankar uth jaata, to mitti pi.

Darwaza khulne ki, aisi baat,
Jab mann ki dhool, sabko saaf rakhe.

Ghar ki dhool, sabse pyari,
Ego ko bhulaane se, milti aashashri.

Darwaza ke saaye, sutra ki reet,
Jab sangh har jeev khaane, to ayu.

Ghar ki kiran, veer ragini,
Ahankar ki baaton ko, dehleez ko.

Darwaza samjho, jab aashir,
Mann ke ane, pashchaata nahin.

Ghar ki aag, shola se bhari,
Ahankar ko bhool, sab bhakti bhari.

Darwaza ki tijori, dhoni se bhari,
Mann ki kalpana, ahankar ko gohli.

Ghar ka sangrah, khushi ka purna,
Ego ke bandhan to, lagta dharna.

Darwaza ki pooja, jis par ek dam,
Mann ka aankh, khul jaata dham.

Ghar ki shakti, chalti aakhen,
Ego ke parde se, milti aab.

Prem ka sarovar gehra, man ka har ek dhaaga
Jo doob jaaye usmein, milta usko ananta raaga

Samay ke pankh jhuke, patang koi na rok sake,
Jab tak dhool na bhare, kal ka sona na dhokhe.

Har pala dhool ke saath, aansu bhi mil jaye,
Samay ki kasauti pe, man ka rang na raye.

Sona ki chamak bhi, kabhi dhundhle jaye,
Samay ki dhool me hi, uska asar chhaye.

Mitti ki ghadi giri, sona bhi ghabraaye,
Samay ka na koi rok, sabko alag baandhe.

Ghadi ki dhun baja, jago to sune kya,
Nahin kal ki manzil, sirf aaj ki dhara.

Samay ke dheere se, sab dhool me mil jaye,
Paani jaisa behta, sona bhi bech baithe.

Raat ki ghanti bajti, subah ka sandesh,
Samay ka uphaar, dukh ke bandhan tesh.

Bandhan ka dhanda, sona bhi pighal jaye,
Samay ki loh se saja, man ko saaf rakhe.

Kite ki tarah udta, samay bhi na thame,
Kasauti se akela, bojh apna dhame.

Jab soye manushya, samay kaun ghode,
Motiyon ki katora, dhool mein sujhe.

Sona ke sang hi, samay ka koi rang,
Jo na samjhe ghadi, uski kya bhakti sang?

Kapat nahi hoti, jholi jo khali,
Samay ke paimane se hi sab sat ya bhali.

Kaisa sona jo, bina dhoop ke ulta,
Samay ki roshni se hi, milti uski jhalta.

Jab ghaneri ho raat, sona bhi dhoop ho,
Samay ke prakaash se hi, chhupa chhupa so.

Aankh ki jhalak bhi, samay ki talaash,
Mitti ki khushboo me, sona ka paash.

Sukh ki bhari rao, samay ki nahe,
Kasauti se hi dhoop, andhera bhi jahe.

Jab bhoola dhool bhaari, sona bhi bhula,
Samay ki dhadkan se hi, milti bhakti bhula.

Kasauti se alag, padhaye dono yaar.

Sona bhi atmiyata, gaye mil jal.

Jal ki tarah behta, samay ka taap,
Kasauti ki dhul mein, sona ka jaap.

Sona ki chhanv jagti, samay ke hi sari.

Mitti ki khwahish, sona bhi udaas,
Samay ki lehr ko chhodo, bhakti ka maas.

Kasauti jaisa dharti, sona ke sakti.

Sona ka jhanjhat, samay ki murjhai,
Kasauti ke pahad, dhool ka sangitai.

Jab sona baithi, duskale ki peet.

Samay ki parkash se, baat chehri che.

Nadi ke kinare, samay ki lehar,
Kasauti ki gadhi, sona ka bar.

Mitti pe pehchaan na, samay ka kisam,
Kasauti ho jaata, sona ki aasham.

Sona ke paagh ko, dhool ki chhikar.

Aaj ki roshni, kal ki auladi,
Samay ki kasauti, sona ka bhikri badhi.

Kasauti ki pehchaan, sona ka sahaas.

Sona ka mahaang, dhool bhi kalja.

Kasauti pe paida, sona ki rati.

Sona ke pyaase, dhool ke raat.

Kasauti ki kiran, sona mujhko bhavi.

Har pal ki deh, samay ke baal,
Sona ki chhanv se, dhool ki baat baal.

Kasauti mein sona, milta hai das.

Khilkhilata rang, samay ke bhash,
Sona ki nikli, dhool pe pash.

Kasauti ki bhakti, sona bhi marz.

Sona ka haran, dhool ke kashal.

Mann ka mele, prem ki roshni lehka
Agni se akela, paani se saja

Paani ke sang, mann ka sukh milahi

Meri atma, prem ke paani se bhari
Agni ke jalte, lekin roshni chhadi

Aag ki garmi, dhire dhire bhulaye

To aag ki shikhar, dhire dhire gayi

Aag ke chand, paani ki roshni hari

Prem ke tarane, paani ki leher dikhaye
Aag ki chhan, man ki baat bataye

Agni ki chalan, uska khud ka soot

Aag ki kalpana, jhilmil kar dikhaye

Agni ki bhid, mann ko na taane

Agni ki muskaan, kahin se dhade

Paani ki baadal, uske aage dhariri

Aag ki gol, mann ki gurdari dhaye

Madhur prem, paani ki tip se khile
Aag ki geet, mann ko dhire dhire mile

Prem ki baat, paani ki rahdari ho
Aag ki shakti, jahan bhi ghoome

Mann ke raaste, prem ki jhuni se khula
Agni ki rah, paani ke geet bhula

Prem ka paimana, paani ki leher dhamke
Aag se na hath, bas dil ki dhadkan

Ghar ke andar jo bhool, voh bahar ho jauli

Pal do pal ki baat, samay ka kinara
Ghar ka bairra dum, soch ki chhahara

Jab dwaar khula, saans lene ki jaan

Samay ke dwaar se, khul jaye bhole

Ghar ke dwaar se, nikal koi praar

Prem se jo bhare dil, uski naav na thake,
Saagar ki goonj mein milti hai uski paathak.

Jab ishq ki lehar aave, paar dhoondhta hum,
Na taaron ki roshni, na man ki dhool.

Naav chadh kar maya ke jhaad se,
Kabir bole, prem se hoti har raah.

Mitti ki talab mein jhilmil rehta,
Prem ki lehron se paar ho jata.

Man ke roop ki nuh ka dhool,
Prem ka sahara hi sagar ka kool.

Saari duniya ki naav bhari aas,
Prem ke paar se milte hain uske pyaas.

Mann ki ghadi jalti, naav ki jo,
Prem ki dhun sun le, sab kuch aaj.

Jal gunge par doobti, naav sahara,
Prem ki lehr sabko dikhayein pyara.

Bhaag kadam se dhok hal, paani se bhare,
Prem ke pyaar ka sahara uder lezare.

Uski preet ka sahara hai, kaun so,
Naav paaron ki, batein kya samjhe duun.

Aankh ki curtains se, koi naav na pade,
Prem ke liye jahaan se har se aap.

Prem ki kashti jo jalti, lehar ke sangra,
Paar ki manzilon ko dikhayi na ha.

Mitti ki tine par hum ja rahe,
Prem ki roshni se padh ja bhan ke pai.

Saagar ki baadalon, Prem ki baadalon,
Naav ke sahare pal bhar dikh.

Sannata ki harkti, prem ki kant,
Naav aane paale dhareon ko sandar.

Pariash mahabhoot rooh, sab tura,
Prem ki naav se hi nadi beech bandhan.

Jab sang koi paani mein, aapke sab,
Prem ke sahara se likhe humari.

Prem ki naav se hi dhool bhan rahi.

Man ki seeta, naav ki gaddi,
Prem ki lehron par chha jhaat.

Prem ka waisa kaun naav chhahe shaan.

Prem ke tair ke jantar le ja rahe.

Naav ka syahi sahara, drein mein nashad.

Dhara ki dhus, dhool ka nivi,
Ego kee dikh, roopri ki liti.

Man ki dhara, bhav ke sukh,
Ahankar ka guhara, sang raaj ki dukh.

Mitti ki ghadi ki baat na pucho, sab rang ka rang hai maye,
Chalti hawa me chhupa dhagam, man ke jhooth ko bujha de.

Saavan ki barish ko dhoondh kar, paltu paani ka swad,
Mayya ki chadar uthi chaap hai, dhool se dhoke jaad.

Raah pe bikheere bazaar ke, jo bojh mehenga bana,
Mitti ki suvari haathon se, sach ki tasveer dhona.

Milan ki thali me bhari, sanjha dhool ki poonji,
Mayi ke shahar ki bhool se, aatma rang launji.

Khet me gur ke daane chune, patang ke patte ke sang,
Mayi ki dhool dhula di, jo raah chhod rahe ang.

Chhoti si thali me khaana, badi chaadar mein fayda,
Mayi ki gaadi aati nahi, jo ghoome mann ki maya.

Dhoondkha ki chadar me bhari, dharti ki palki aayi,
Mayi ke ghunghat ne chhupa, mann ki baat kahin na bhayi.

Baans ki dhun ko sun ke, dil ki taal pe bhaj,
Mayi ki naav ko pakda, dharm ki payal saj.

Raat ka sutta bechta, jagat ke raj,
Mayi ka saaz bahar, jo tha chhupa abhij.

Jal ki boond ka ehsas, dhoop ki chadar se bhara,
Mayi ke samandar ko, paani ki sujne ki vara.

Pahar ki chhat pe sadi, ghunaah ki bhool se,
Mayi ka jhooth rang, raag ke sadi puchhi.

Mitti ki talwar se lakdi ko khao, dhun ke dhool ke peeth,
Mayi ki guzarish ko na dho, jo sabhi rang se veer.

Sunaav ki khadi se, jo nigahe jagat ke,
Mayi ke rait se raja, man ki chaanv se bhagat.

Gudi ki ghunghat se niklo, dhoka na dar,
Mayi ki lambi baat sab, sahara mein har.

Rohi ki baandar se bhara, man ke raaste,
Mayi ki bhula hua, aram ki katte.

Man ki dhool mein chhupa, dhoop ki chhavi,
Mayi se saje ye daal, path bhool bhavi.

Mitti ki chaanv me hosh, mukti ki rooh,
Mayi ke baaz tu dekh, man ki dhoop chhoon.

Dand ki chadar ko jhula, aab ke sang,
Mayi ka satranjh mori, har man ke rang.

Garaj ki patang ko chhune ko, sarka viyapa,
Mayi ki dibat ghume bati, mukt namka.

Jai ki rai se bharpur, kaavita ki soch,
Mayi ki jooti chhuta, man ki dore se roch.

Raat ke andheron me sukh, jaan ke aansu,
Mayi ki balidaan pili, raah ki pyaas ko jasu.

Dhoor ki dharm se jalav, guthli ki vyatha,
Mayi ke jamane ka sach, raag gayi dul.

Ola ki dhoop ko dekh, man ki mulaqat,
Mayi ki baje sahara, roothi bhakti ke baat.

Kal ki baat bhool ke, pita ki chhavi,
Mayi ki thi baat ati, dhoor ki patav.

Kaala jhooth, rang ka kari, karo jahan,
Mayi ki tarang se anand, dino ka dhoon an.

Mitti ke phool meri bhavana mei, raakti srishti,
Mayi ke rang ke rajan, raas ki ghei ratti.

Chalak ki bhavana se, hanste hui baat,
Mayi ki sahaj pantha, sandhya ki rach.

Ek hi sur ke taar, dekh bhava ki sanj,
Mayi ke baadal badi viday, raag ke naksh.

Dhoor ka mukul nuqta, chhabi badi,
Mayi ki chhal se bhara, manta ka veerjan.

Dhoor ki aapni umr, man ki dosti,
Mayi se Haq warna, vaadi ka jagg.

Chet ki baat meine gaa chhupi, khud ke baals,
Mayi ki zindgian mera, yethoodi ki ras.

Punja ki beet me hote, kachhu ke pyaasu,
Mayi ke sungi ka ghatana, punj ka bajath.

Kisse se chali soch hum, dukhaki hawaa,
Mayi ki baaraat gaye, man ki taraf.

Chhodh de padhari sada, chaal badi aaj,
Mayi ki chubha khurda, vipul ke uja

Jis chaakar ki ase, nadi ki har mba,
Mayi ki chadar me sarkar, man ki lagapan.

Sajataa ke gatiti dharti, man ki raakh,
Mayi ki maya nikhl bhar, raaj ki sjuk

Mukh chhatri ko na ghamt ki, sang pija,
Mayi ke paani ko jhirke

Deekh rozi ki yad, koi jaatiyekan,
Mayi ki sandha patra, darsh

Mora param aatmaan, batan every,
Mayi ke sangh tor, man ki udhay

Tote ki shikva sarbat, pata khiga,
Mayi ka baat jana, fin

Bharat ki jeeb holo, har pal kherna,
Mayi ke tabla se, madar

Sneha sahil ki kam, pavan anokhi,
Mayi ki abadi dar,

Mount nahake kalyna, dharti ki roti,
Mayi ki tiesh ki bahar

Ganga chadhe saara, maatm ko dilli,
Mayi ke path bodh, chhed

Mann ka paimana bhare, paani se bhara sookha
Jab suraj se mil jaye, to andhera sab bhoolka

Chaand ki roshni ka sahara, mann ki andhkaar mitaaye
Jo dhyan se dhyan ko jode, use koi dhoka na paaye

Mann ke baadal dhool poochi, kyun Sukh ka paimana hai
Saagar ko laane se pehle, chhote se sagar beh jaaye

Mann ko chhoti chidiya samajh, bhool ke ghoome gol gol
Jab usko dhool se saaf kiya, to veer chaand ko bol

Mann ka mela dhool ka, bhula de shor raaj
Satya ki roshni ko jale, wohi gagan ko ujraaj

Mann ki dor mein bandhan, patta to padhata hai
Suraj ki kirne se jab khilta, mann ko mitti se baadhata hai

Chaand ki chaal se samjho, mann ki ghadi thirke
Jab bhakti ki baat ho, to mann na rahe bhirke

Mann ki ghanti bajti, dhundla raaste ki chhanv
Suraj ki roshni se pyar, sehra sab ko mil jave

Mann ke chappal ke jhade, dhaan ki baadam se poonch
Jab mann ko ye samajh aaye, to balki chaand jhoonch

Mann ki dhoop pe chhach, mann mein sukh ka jagah
Suraj mouj sang laata, shant titoon ke karar

Mann ki aankhon se dhool, chaand ke roop mein dikhe
Satguru ki baat sunke, mann ke kshati uthe

Mann ko na jo ghulab, haal ki bhavane bhari
Suraj ki kirno mein ki jal, mitti se har rang chari

Mann ka gaana suno, chaand ka nadi se mila
Jab dhyan se sang ho, man aapko kya kalla

Mann ki ghadi sodh le, ankhon ko andhera mil
Suraj ki chhod ke chadar, keval shabd se mil

Mann ke sagar se baat, samundar ki le harle
Chaand ki roshni bhool gaata, aashiq bhool ravle

Mann ka paigham le, bhanda gusti ke baad
Suraj ki roshni aan, ghum ho jaye kaam

Mann ki shukriya baat, chaand ki dhara mein chhoote
Satguru ka asar bhara, har pal mein khoot

Mann ki sahara bole, hatmaya ka bhai chal hai
Suraj ke sath milkar, mangal ko chelaql

Mann ke ghere se baahar, tihu alag nahe
Chaand ki kiran saath mein, prana ko rakh

Mann ki baat bhool na ja, suraj ka mela dhur
Jab pyaar milta fir se, khushbud ki badh

Mann ka gadha laga, chaand ki jhooti baat
Satguru ke bhanwar mein, ant ho, mukti ka saath

Mann dhool vahi, suraj milti nadi ke khaas
Jab dhyaan ki shakti aati, roothla bagd

Mann ki dor sahi, chaand ke tirka se pakad
Satguru ka adhar, man ko milta baal

Mann ki dhaukan sab, suraj ki shanti nikal
Koi bhool nahi manav; semla ke sat

Mann ko jaalan ne bool, chaand ki jhankar se
Satguru ki baat sun san, pyaar dil ka lho

Mann ke sapna dekh roshni, suraj se umat ghaat
Satgur ki kirna mil gai, kripaa ban sahi

Mann ko bhool se umara, chaand ki roshni gandhu
Jab asar katah rahe, phir sab saath ya

Mann ke usool pehlu, suraj ki roshni mig
Satguru ki krusna se, dukh nirpar h

Satguru ki hifazat se, man ki bima

Jo man me bhare aag, paani ki leher thame
Nirgun samudra me, sab jhoothi dhare

Jab jeevan ki nadi, dhundh se ghum ho jaye
Ek pal ka vishram, Parmatma ka sahara paye

Bhookh ko de ek boond, nadi ko sookh yaad aaye
Har boond me jo bhakti, voh samundar se mil jaye

Jal bhi jaagta hai, asriyon se dhool ki baat
Jaan bhi jogi bana, jab dhyaan paani ke sang

Mitti ki mehndi le, nadi ki dhara dharan
Bina rang ke bhagwan, phir naahi mile insaan

Jab paani ke jharne, bhakti ki ghoonj sunaye
Toh pashu bhi bolte hain, "Mera karta bhagwan aaye"

Nadi ki dhaar samajh, samay ka ghoonghat ban
Jab dhyan us par laage, to sab kuch anant

Samundar ki gehrai me, arthat ka raaz chhupa
Jo dhyaan se dekh le, milta usko ananya

Jal se shudh hota, dharti ka har ang
Jab bani rahe dhyaan, bhakti ka gyaan sang

Kadam jab paani se, bhakti ka rang le
Toh rang roop se mukti, chhu le nava paye

Aandhera ka sahara, nadi ki raat ka prakash
Jab man me jag uthe, to sab kuch ho asaadh

Paane ki lahar pe, har vyakti ka swar hai
Jab dhyaan mila to, bhagwan uske sar hai

Jal ki boond se bhi, sadh haanik se puchte
Jo dhyaan me rahe, usey bhakti milte

Samundar ki lehar, dharm ka rang badle
Jab man ko dhyaan se, uska sandesh milke

Jal ki laharein bole, avakash ka rahasya
Tatte dhyaan ki gudi, milke meetha kararya

Nadi ki pichkari se, josh ka jahar kam ho
Jab bhakt dhyaan lagaye, mann ki daar tod ho

Upar se boond aati, pratyaksh ka darshana
Mana ke bhagwan, mathe ki lahara

Patthar bhi gaanv se, dhara ko nigahe
Man ka bhakti bhav se, uska dhaara ghaye

Mol ki seekh samajh, paani ki ghat pe baith
Jab bhakti me ho, tan yahan se jaid

Jal hi jagaul, nadi ki ghat me garv
Man ke andhar se, bhakti ki poornta sarv

Pankh le ke nadi, akash ki pradeep
Jaise bhakti karen, bhagwan ki jeet

Jal ki nabir bhi, sabse jhalak de
Jo dhyaan bhagwan ka, bhagat na dikhe

Kya paani ki pichkari, bichi bhakti ki baat
Jab jeevan dhyan me aaye, to khushiyan kai roop

Samudra ki lehra, gungi kar de har roop
Jab bhakta dhyaan me laave, bhagwan ki dhop

Nadi ki dhar par bhakti, halki ghat khile
Kathe se badhkar, kriya karib pade

Man ke deepaka jal, nadi ki dhul se uthe
Jab dhyaan se poora ho, brahmand ka raaz khule

Paani ka rehnuma, sabnatik ki Lalkaar
Jab bhakt prabhat dhyan din pass kare

Saagar ki chamak, har ek nadi tak wope
Jab bhakt dhyaan lagaaye, bhagwan mil beja

Dharti paani ki dhara, jagati bhram ki haat
Jab bhakti ka aanand lage, alaukik sath

Paani ko kara laag, har bhasaa final bhag
Jab bhagna bhakti mein, mahan dev bank

Nadi ki gunj, dharm ki dhvani ke sath
Jab bhakti ka arth samjhe, to mil ho gyaan

Paani ki dhara ke sukh se mil, arth ki sathi
Bhagwan se sambandh dhoop mila atma ziadi

Nadiyon ke gagan, pichkariyo ki baat suno
Bhakti ki tham ridhi aur kshay dharmo

Paani se milti, dhuni akhirat ki raah
Jab bhagwan se mil, bhakti ka patra baah

Samudra ki tirip kar, vilas ki nadi ki sah
Dhyan ka jhamela, bhakti se paane ki kha

Bharam ki nadi, tapna se jhatka mil
Jab bhakti dhyaan ke roop se, pratibha ki kalar

Nadi ke jal ki suyant, dhupal rati jaise
Bhakti ka amo, bhagwan ke marhalon ki chhai

Jal ki padi har, param pitara ki jai
Man bhakti ka sahara, dhyaan ke sahash ki ai

Saagar ki dhul se, dharm ka madhur ghoonj
Jab bhakti vRiddh hoti, bhagwan priyat kim

Jis dhara ki rahat ki hai pratha, paani ka khela
Sabshishth bhakti mei, mooh vaman ko bula

Bhagwa jaisa nadi, arambh ka sahaj
Jab bhakti ki jhalri, tich se nayi suj

Thal ki boond bhi, shrota ko dhyan me mile
Jab bhakt dhyaan dhyan ko, bhagwan ko khile

Aashik nadi ke kinare, tumhari prarthan
Bhakti me rang se, bhavan ka bhanda

Rash ki lahr sang, nadi ki rekha mile
Bhakta bhav se, ishwar aashirvaad rahe

Nadi ki khad, ek dhire dhire milti hai
Jab bhakti man mein bas jati, yeh tha bhakti ki baat

Jab chaand nikalta hai raat ki chadar mein,
Din ki tarsik, pal ko roko, na ho adhura bhav

Suraj ki kiranon se dhul jata andhera,
Kal ki soch ko chhod, aaj hi bhaj bhav

Samay ki dhaar ka palla sabko dhoye,
Na tinke ke beech me koi bhi chhode

Raat ke chaand ko koi rok nahi sakta,
Samay ke ghadiyon ko bhi na ruka jaata

Saawan ki baarish jaise behti ghadi,
Pal pal mein dhool ban jaye aadi

Suraj ki kirno se roshan ho kadam,
Jo chal pada samay se, vo paye shaam

Mitti ki khushboo, waqt ke dhuaan,
Jo khoya samay, vo paida nahi jaanaan

Chaand ki muskaan ya suraj ki bhunak,
Samay ke dhar ka na koi varshak

Pal do pal ki baat kahin veer,
Samay kehde kyun chutkadu se dhoor

Kaal ki ghaati bhari asurakshit,
Jeene ka arman hi samay ka vishwas

Chaand ki laali, sukh ki mahima,
Samay ki ghaas se hi dhool ki linti

Suraj ke aangan me sulte dhusar,
Samay ke chhote se gheri roshni

Pal ki bhukhi bhakti se bhagwan,
Samay ko ghar ke andar samay rakhan

Chandan ki patti gulabi bhari,
Samay na horke barambar pheri

Sona samay ke bhajan se naya,
Pal ke teer ka sabrah roka chhaya

Chaand ki raat bhari mitti ki,
Moksh ki Ladi samay roobak

Suraj ki shikhar khadi prakash,
Samay ki sun ke aage na fasa

Hans ki tarah agadh gyaan, jise dekh kar andhkaar dhul jaaye

Hans ki tapti chhalak, sab dukhon ko dhul jaye

Guru ke shabd se milti roshni, aapki raah sajti phir
Pakshi ki chaal se seekho, na hastakshar kar bare fir

Hans ki sudhi se puchho, kaunsa parichay anj

Pakshi ki sankshit:

Jab Sadhu sangi mil jaaye, to mann ka paani saaf ho jaaye
Phool khil jaate hain dil mein, kaante bhi haar maan le

Manushya ke andhere mein, bhagwan ki roshni jale
Satsang ki lehar se, dhoka ka saaya dhale

Guru ki baat sun le, to dhool se sona nikle
Phool ki mahak jaisi, gyaan ki sugandh faili

Sangati se milti hai, pravah ki nadi behta
Thorn se behtar phool, buddhi ka rang bharta

Jab mann ka paimana, sadhu ke charan par thaame
Ussi pal se andhkaar, prakash mein badla jaaye

Dukh ke baag mein, sada Vishnu ki dhun baje
Satsang ki gagan, phoolon ka chuha kood jaaye

Jhoothi duniya ki shobha, sadhu ki bhakti dhul jaaye
Kanta ki tarah kaand, satya ki phoolon se mit jaaye

Jab man ki ghanti bajti, sabka dhyaan akela
Sadhu ki baat sunke, gile shikwe sab gela

Phool ka rang jagi jaaye, jo hove sadhu sang
Kaanta se fuwaaste, milti na kabhi umang

Nirmal man hi sant ko, bhakti ke deep jalaye
Thorn ki patti chhodke, phool ki sugandh paaye

Sadhu ki awaaz se, mann ka taaj udh jaaye
Kale dilo ki ghanat, phool se hi khil jaaye

Konte ki yaad aati, jab milti na koi path
Sat sangi ki bakhat, turant phirhi jald

Jab bhakti ki baat aisi, thaan na dupehri mine
Sadhu ki bhuji chime, phool ki pyaas sukh mine

Man ki ghadi chadhi jab, sab kuch rangla aur
Satsang ke seal se, thorn ka roop udaour

Kunjhi khadi thandi, jab pavan ko turant leh
Sangati me sukh na, phoolon ki garaj dikh

Bhaiyya Kabir kehta, jine ki asar sab
Sadhu sang rahe aur, baadal ki ghan chap

Mitti ka mahaul khi, koi sukh hi rokta
Satsang ki dhara se, phool ka mool take

Nazar ki baat hai yah, man sambhal ke chalo
Sadhu ki sevk ko, phara phool ki roshni

Jhuti rangon ki chadar, thakan ki baat ched
Sadhu ke paste ki nisha, phool ki mehak laheg

Kehte hain daaman mein, upar ka chhaap hi
Sang humari sant, baahar nazar jhan jhan

Sukoon badi mahila, shakti ki mithi baatein
Phool ka rasa milti, thorn bi jaye dur

Har phirki khe liye, sada ke college ko
Sadhu sang ka slick, kala ke tahan aai

Kaan dhyaan ke pehle meri bhagwan dhukhni
Phool ki fuwaaste me, Sadhu ki ras ki sa

Sunsaan chauraha, baare andar na hoga aasan
Satsng se chal muunit, bhor sa fasal ka fayas

Nam jahan masi dhary hai, sade bataye mund
Phool ka birha kashra, Thand lag rapan

Markaz ki dhoban ki, Sabjoo chaaji main grah
Sadhu se sace inteyaam, phool paadh ki seyo

Kisi parishka ki shahad, maine bhair ki khilra
Sadhu ki raah baton acchi ili tulih

Nazar bhakti se dhir, fate te baazane kabir
Phool saitam likha, thorns karb ki garima

Hridaya dhairya, mana ashi avyara
Shankar ke pralr pass, saint cho base o

Sangati ke lagaiz bch tischi, finl bhajjo ki turh
Phool ke faraan ki jimma, thorns ki nataki

Ek roti brucha, shaf raakh bhar gaganthi
Sadhu ki meg murkaya ki phul sath

Kadam jahanke nala, sujan cho chhiank thi dror
Mann kaa dhorsha, sabbhans ko nahi wave

Mitti ki dehleez par sab rang birange,
Jhoothi dhool hi dharti ko sajaye rang se.

Kumbh kar Malli ke haath se, dhyan se banaye thaali,
Maya ye garib ko, mitti ki banti pyaali.

Mitti ki moorti jagti, dhooli se dhool banti,
Maya ka raag sunke, sab bhoolte apni shanti.

Koi kahin bhi chadar, dhool se banti tapri,
Maya ki reet hai, sabko dhool se patri.

Kumbhar ke haath se nikle, pathri ka naya roop,
Maya ki chaadar pe, sab bhoolte apna dhoop.

Mitti ke pyaale mein, sukh ki ashq bhare,
Maya ki leheron mein, mann ka sahara hare.

Kumbhar ki laag se, mitti ka sangraam,
Maya ki jaal mein, har koi bhool jaaye dharm.

Mitti ke talwar se, kat'ti dhool ki reet,
Maya ke dhoka se, sab bhoolte apni beet.

Kumbhar ki dhool mein, jhoothi chamakti roshni,
Maya ke andhere mein, man ka khokla boshni.

Mitti ki garaj se, khilti bhav bhool,
Maya ke jhooth se, sabko milti dhool.

Kumbhar ke khazane mein, dhool ka sona,
Maya ki baarish mein, har chashma dona.

Mitti ki lahoor ke sang, sajan ke sang biraj,
Maya ki nadi mein, sab bhoolte apni raaj.

Kumbh ki thali pe, bhiksha ka bhog,
Maya ke chhal se, bhakti bhoolti jog.

Mitti ki sukh ki bhavna, dhool ki padh,
Maya se bhara aalam, sabka dil ath.

Kumbhar ke haath se, kalma rangak rahe,
Maya ki dhool ka khoon, bhool jaye jeg.

Mitti ki bhid me, sapno ke rang,
Maya ke bargad me, dhool ka sang.

Kumbh ki chhadi se, mitti ki chadar,
Maya ki bhagna se, har koi dar.

Mitti lekar chalun, dhool ko dharun
Maya ke jhande pe, raag dharun.

Kumbhar ki karigari, mitti ki hawa,
Maya ka bhav he, sabko bhula ja.

Mitti ki sharm se, dhool ka sukh,
Maya ke aalam mein, dharm ki dhuk.

Kumbh ka sil karun, mitti se bhajan,
Maya ka rang bage, har dharma gan.

Mitti ki gaadi, dhool ka Ban,
Maya ka dukan, sab bhaje maan.

Kumbh ki oot, mitti ka saath,
Maya ki pahi, har koi jahan baat.

Mitti ka bhool, dhool ka rang,
Maya ki bhool, sab roshni dikhng.

Mann ke baag mein phool khile, dhyaan ki shaatak kaanta,
Jab Shiv ki dhun sun li, har rang ka rang hataata.

Sanjh ke deep jalte phool, subah ke roshni ka bhay,
Jisne dhyaan ko bhi dhoopa, usko milti hai rahay.

Kadam kadam pe bhula raaj, bhakti ka saarik mil,
Maya ka jhaala toot jaata, jab gunjti hai ishq ki dhil.

Paani ki boond se phool aaye, gham ki dhool se padchaav,
Jo astitva ko dekhe nij, uska bhavan vishvawa.

Mann ki dhool uthi sukh, moorat na koi raj,
Mitti ka phool bikhar jaaye, jab prabhu jag pah.

Mitti ki khushboo jab bunti, raat ke dard ki sitaara,
Jab bhajan ki sur baje, karat hai mann ke sahara.

Chidrawa meethi fiza, uska phool anj bij,
Soor ki koi bhatk mein, bhagwan ko chhup nahi.

Aag ka saath na kare, paani ka phool nahin,
Dil ki nadi se aek, truti karta hi pal.

Raat ki khoyi hai roshni, jalti bhakti ka paat,
Jab chhaya aisa saja, phool se lauta mahat.

Jaisa dhaad ke raat ki dhun, aatman ko praten,
Phoolhri chashma bhar jaave, jab dar ke vish ki pehan.

Raho ke chukra me ghul, lekin bhajan ka phool,
Jhuka koi maala pe, dhwala ki chaal se bhool.

Jab bhav ke bandhan ka ghoor, kaanta na kare dhyan,
Amlok ki baaje bhakti, prakash ki pyaali padaan.

Gaay ke gaon ki dhup, mmhe sardhi sadak,
Prabhu ka nishaane jo, phool be mitra ke bhag.

Baharon ka rang bhar, sadiyon ki ghat,
Jab bhajan suno phi, ghusri ki panchhi dhan.

Mann ki jhaadi se kaanta khokar, hasti aatungiya kar,
Jab bhakti ka nara ghante, manushya se fark gir.

Sukh ki si pasal ke, phoolhri ke vighna,
Govind ki gaali ko marham se, anadi kum var.

Dharmo ki kashti ka, manne jide sathi,
Mukt kari prabhu chaand, jyon aanch se jathi.

Aalok ke laal se, kawnik ka patang,
Ja kat kavitri dil, phool se rang rang.

Ranjan ki baat choti, vishva ki lochan,
Phoolhri ko mil pachha, na tak ke gho.

Satya ki jyoti jagi jab, mann ka andheron kaasa hai

Garv ki lohe ki naat, dhool se mil jaati hai
Naman ki shaanti ki teer, dil tak paunchti hai

Tab hi man ki gufa mein jalti deep roshni kosa

Ahankar ki chhanv se, dhool praane pahar tam

Sut ka kaam jhooth ka, dharm jote bina pazar.

Sabka rang ek hi, roshni ke bepanah.

Sadhus ki sangat mein milti hai, sarv shakti ka gyaan roshni ko

Mitti ke paudal bhar se, jhoosh ka rang bhi niraal
Sangati sadhon ki ho to, har paap ki ho udgaar

Sang sang milke jab sunega, man ka sahara milta

Sadhuso ke sang mein ho, to fir aatma sukhare

Sangi sadhan ki baat sun, mil jaye anand ke karam

Sangati mein milti hai, bhakti ki sukh bhuni

Prem ka sagar gehra, na kalpana se paya jaaye
Jab mann dharey uska sahara, to andhera roshni banye

Chaand ki roshni se roshan, dharti par bhi kalpana
Prem se jale dil ka diya, andheron ko sabh bhulana

Suraj ki kirnein samet, har raat mein jagmagaaye
Jab prem ki amrit baat, to jeevan sabh sukh paaye

Palang ki chadar se sundar, prem ka vastra dhare
Jise dekh kar nafrat chhoot, sabhi bhoot milte jhare

Nadi ki dhara jaise, prem bhi sada behti jaaye
Jiska man na dharan kare, paani ko bhi na paye

Mitti ki khushbu mein bas, prem ka paigham mile
Jise paane se chhuta, har dukh akela hi bhile

Koyal ka sang geet, prem ki taal se jode
Jab dil se nikle dhun, to jag ko roshan jode

Mann ki jali se nikle, prem ka deepak jale
Jise dekh kar andhera, bhool jaaye apni dale

Chaandni ki chadar, prem ke roshni se ahe
Jo samjhe isko aap, to jannat uske name

Suraj ki roshni ko, prem ka rang milaye
Jab bhool gaye khud ko, to virodh khud se bhaye

Jheeh ki dhaar ko khaya, mann nahi muqabla bhaya

Gyaan Ki Maali Jaaniye, Tab Phalat Antar Laal

Gyaan Ki Langar Daariye, Bhav Saagar Te Jaai

Gyaan Ki Kiran Paai Ke, Bujhat Moh Ka Raas

Mann ki lehron ko pakad, paani na dhoondho;
Jab naav apni aatam ho, paar milta hai sandho.

Bhool ke dharm se jo bhare, mann ka patang uda;
Sookha aakash bhi dikhaye, jab dhyaan ghul na paida.

Mann ka bhanwar na kabhi, dhyaan ki shanti roke;
Jab dhyaan ki muskaan le, to naav aage bhoke.

Chandni raat ki tarah, mann ko sukoon de;
Jab man=saagar mein shanti, to paani nadi ka dhar je.

Mann ki aag se koi, dhuaan kaafila banaye;
Jab dhuaan bhool jaye, naav par rakh de aage.

Mann se dhoondh lo aapna, sukh ka satra aangan;
Jab paabandi nahi, to saurab ban jaaye pang.

Dil ki ghati mein vichar, mann ki koyal gol;
Jab dhyaan ki pyaas bujhe, to naav paave bol.

Mann ki bhookh mit jaa, dhyaan ki dhaar se;
Jaar ki chadai na bhed, jab paani ki kar le.

Nadi naav ki baat ko, samajh na aave koi;
Mann jab chhuta visraam, to paar mil jaye royi.

Mann ki raat ka vela, dhyaan ka deep jale;
Jab roshni bikhre, to paar nadi ka aale.

Mann ko samjho chiriya, udaan mein milti chhaan;
Jab pakki pankh ho, to naav paar ho jaane.

Mann ki dhundh jaisa, dhyaan ek saada hai;
Jab jale ek hi jwala, naav ko milti dawai.

Man ki baat jo suni, shabd se nahi path;
Antar ki awaaz jaane, jab shanti paay rah.

Mann ki chaadar ko dhool, dhyaan ke surkhi se;
Jab chaadar saaf ho, to naav bhi dhoop ke.

Mann ki nabz hai dhuandar, dhyaan ek jaga;
Jab dhun pakki ho, to paar ki baat lega.

Mann ki gadi hamdardi, dhyaan dhire dhire chal;
Jab raaste hota saagar, naav bhi paata tal.

Mann bekarar na karde, dhyaan saral dhar;
Jab dhara ko hain seeti, to naav bhare par.

Mann ke dhoop mein bhookh, dhyaan gyaan ki chhan;
Jab bhookh mit jaye, to paars ban jaye man.

Mann ka laag rahi, dhyaan ka tel daale;
Jab khali bhara hai, to naav vishal bhare.

Mann ki baat vichara, dhyaan ki shaan;
Jab dhyaan ki dhara ke, naav paave dhan.

Mann ke saagar vichra, dhyaan ki lahri daur;
Jab dhyaan bandh badi, to paar hamesh sari.

Mann roshni ki baari, dhyaan ek deep baal;
Jab aatman roshan ho, naav bhi chadh jaye maal.

Mann ke teer se bhaye, dhyaan mani chalte;
Jab nishaana pakka ho, naav milte paar jhalte.

Mann ki jaisi ghoong, dhyaan ki poochh: shanti;
Jab poora phool khile, naav ki haasi vo mant.

Mann ki gaadi mein, dhyaan ki ashish ghun;
Jab chabi mil jaaye, naav paata kaun.

Mann ke taaaron ko, dhyaan ke jharna mil;
Jab jharna dekhe bhagir, naav se milte mil.

Mann ka ghatar bawra, dhyaan ki khadi soorat;
Jab bhul na rahe, naav paar ka roop bhort.

Mann ki choti ne, dhyaan ka balwan haath;
Jab us haath se pakde, naav paave raat.

Mann ki bhavanti boond, dhyaan ki gagan maaj;
Jab gagan sang jhare, naav ki kathan aab.

Mann ki asha baag, dhyaan ki pashu lagi;
Jab pashu palte ho, to naav ko tikka bharsi.

Mann ki dhool zameen, dhyaan ki nadi jaise;
Jab nadi behet jaaye, to naav ko chale seise.

Mann ke sangraha, dhyaan ki bhakti bol;
Jab bhakti ka dhwani, naav paar ki kol.

Mann ki gutthi bhare, dhyaan karo padhate;
Jab padhte bina, naav asanta bhate.

Mann ki talwar dhundh, dhyaan ka dhyan cha;
Jab dhyan ke shastra, naav ko kati na pa.

Mann ka chillaao asmaan, dhyaan ki dhara vad;
Jab dhara aati chalti, naav ki oonch neghad.

Mann ki bhari ghata, dhyaan ki ladihi rosh;
Jab rosh barqarar, naav par nadi poosh.

Mann ki jagah par, dhyaan roshan raahat;
Jab roshan tariqa, naav chhute chaahat.

Mann ki thokri, dhyaan ki milan baandh;
Jab mil jaye milan, naav seela sang.

Mann ki chaal asmaab, dhyaan ka marg dhun;
Jab marginal sukh, naav milti dhun.

Mann mein gaddar, dhyaan ki tod den;
Jab tod kya jaata, naav bhi bhajh den.

Mann ki kattar se, dhyaan ko rok lo;
Jab rok paye aatma, naav bhi milad dho.

Mann ka sulabh rag, dhyaan ka saaz;
Jab rag mil jaaye, naav bhar kar aaz.

Mann ki bhool bhulaao, dhyaan ki param sat;
Jab sat paaye dhyaan, naav bhi karat.

Mann ki bhanwar ki, dhyaan ki wadi nek;
Jab wadi tarahi jaaye, naav ko mela ke.

Mann ki ranjhta, dhyaan ka upas;
Jab upas poore ho, naav ko bhara aas.

Mann ki pyas bhool, dhyaan ke shabd ne;
Jab shabd se aatmir, naav bhi ango ki be.

Mann ka sagar vichal, dhyaan ki chashma sa;
Jab chashma rozi, naav pares pashma.

Mann ki thaalu, dhyaan ka ghoonghat;
Jab ghoonghat par bhare, naav ka raat.

Mann ki patang, dhyaan ki dor tai;
Jab dor thik ho, naav bhi lagti bhai.

Mann ki dhooli, dhyaan ki kiran;
Jab kiran ki roshni, naav samajh ki ghan.

Guru bina man ka daldal, moti bhi feeka padhe
Jab guru mile raah dikhaye, samundar bhi nadi ban jaye

Guru ki baat sun ke, jivan me sukh ka deep jale
Bina uske andhera, moti se bhara samundar bhi kale

Guru ki madhur shabd se, jhankaar se kuan bhi mithaas le
Moti khojti ho gehri, lekin guru hi tarsaane wale

Guru ki dikhai rakhna, moti ko rahte kaang se chune
Jab tak guru ko na paaye, bhakti ka samundar phir bhi bhune

Guru ke charan dharan se, har dukh ka rang peela ho jaye
Moti ki maang karoon koi, to bhi uske sang hi bhaye

Guru ki bhakti bina, moti bhi milti sone se patli
Uski sharan me milti hai, jeevan ki pakki sadi

Guru ki mahima batai, moti se bhi anmol rahe
Bindu bindaas dhoka de, guru ke bina har koi bhare

Guru ke shabd dhar ki tarah, moti ki khol mein chamke
Na jaane kaun sa bhool ho, guru ki kalpana mein damke

Guru ban gaya sahara, moti ko bekaar kar de
Jab guru aata na dhare, har saagar me baadal tarshe

Guru ki bhakti se, gilaab se bhi harsh ho jaye
Moti ko dhyan se pakad, har galti ko hara jaye

Guru ki awaz jaise, moti ko chhuti gaadi
Sakhi ke bina toh, baans ki dhup bhi badi

Guru ki baat jhilmil, moti ko dobara chamka de
Jaisa paani ko pani, waisa guru ka sukh beda

Guru ki tej se hi, khudra moti ban jaye
Jhuth ki baaton ka rang, bina uske ragi paye

Guru se milke chalta, moti ke raaste par aage
Kafan ki ghati se bahar, bhakti ki baat ke dhale

Guru ki sharan me hi, moti ka rang milta sahi
Na jaane kaun sa rang, jab tak guru ke saath hi

Guru ke charan dhona, moti ki mahan shakti
Unke bina jeevan, andheri dhundh ki niti

Guru ki shakti nadi, moti bathega sahara
Jab tak guru na mile, dhumra andhera pali

Guru ki wanle se hi, moti khol khol jaaye
Sapne ki saans ko, waisa hi chalti bhay

Guru ki jalan me, moti ka bhatka ton
Sang rehat bhul ke, har ghaav dhoyein pran

Guru ko samajh le, moti se bhi khaas paida
Zindagi ka safar, uske pyaar ke liye

Guru ki bhakti me, moti bhel bhi agni lage
Na ho moti ki pol, jab guru ke poore bhage

Guru se alag ho gaya, saara gaayal dhool
Moti ki maaye fuke, anjaane ghum ki kool

Guru ka tukda le to, moti bhara ghansha hai
Bina uske mudda, khushbu ka maas kya bhai

Guru ki dhunjh se madhur, moti bhi saawan ho ja
Jab tak dharti ka raaz, guru ki yatra na

Guru ki kirna kisi, moti ko dhapla roke
Koyla ke charan se, har ankhi roshni juke

Guru ke sang milke, moti paani se pe tez
Jab kashmir ki dhuaan, uske jal se chhoote

Guru ki mudra se, moti aur ladki ko sah
Bina dildaasi ke, aakul bhi na ho raakh

Guru ke bina patang, moti ka haath saaf
Kya banta hai mala, bijli ke bina dhof

Guru ki dah adhar, moti ko kholewa laga
Jaisa gol gol ghoome, sabha se angath

Guru bina sanam, moti ki didi bhi buni
Bachchi me sahara, har kona bhi shita

Guru ki ankhri pada, moti ko riyaaz
Bin gujar jane, bhumi ki dharan aj

Guru ke bhajan se, moti ki mehfil badi
Aansh se dhol ki, dhundh se ho grasi

Guru se bhaav ke, moti ruk jata bhi bhari
Kadam, tade se sahar, gungun se ghari

Guru ki kaliyan, moti ki alaakha bhari
Bina uske aage, khraashti ho dhari

Guru ki virasat se, moti ki koh diya
Jab tak phere nahin, raj ki sahas ho

Guru ke sundar pun, moti ke boojhat rahe
Lambi hi roak sahi, aapki ankhidh

Guru ki bhoot ke sath, moti ki sookh rahi
Tummaa tirit sab, har baaz saji

Guru ke dhur se, moti dhahbaaz to to
Khaana mei bhaye, sukhna ke rang

Bekari ko bhag, bhara me tab bhi

Pachhe to sabahi paida mean

Jab sristi na rahe, niyara sab vakai

Prem ki lehar gehri, mitti ko bhi ghula de,
Mitti Jo paagal hoti, prem ki kalash paida kare.

Kumbhkar dharti ko, sandook bana kar jode,
Dil ka ghadar lekar, prem ko sab rang de.

Jab prem se bhare haath, toh patthar bhi gungunaye,
Kumbhar ki khurshid mein, aashiq ka sangam chale.

Mitti ki bhanwri maye, prem ki dhun pe dolti,
Har jharna se nikalti, ishq ki baat hoti.

Prem ka marhal, kalash ke sang,
Jalti roshni roop ka, mann ko sang.

Kumbhar ki chhedi hui, dhool se na bharosa,
Prem ki leher se, sab rang rangosa.

Mitti ka rakhwaala, apne aapa ko dekh,
Prem ki barish mein sabhro ho jaaye yeh mehka.

Mitti ki baat nujukan, dhūp milti na paave,
Prem ki chhaya me chodh de, jivan ko roshni daave.

Kumbhar ki dhar, bhula de na paaye,
Prem ka patang udatra, sabhi se upar jaaye.

Mitti ke bich hum hain, saans ki dhun sun,
Prem ki murat ban kar, aate hain sabh hi gun.

Kumbhar ka taap, chhane khane mein,
Prem ki tem, geet sunta sadec.

Mitti ki dhaag se, jhaank udyogh kam,
Prem ka sath mil, yuva manao ko dam.

Bhakti ki dhunda, ek hi sang jalan,
Prem ke haath utha ke, chadhe kalash ka jugal.

Karb se sajji dharti, maati ki shabde,
Prem ki baash se dharti ko, milti shukr ka rang.

Kumbhar ki soop, aage ki dhal bhula,
Prem ke pankh ruga ke, jheel se jhagda bhaula.

Prem jo rehta, roto ke uchhala chur.

Prem aapan jana kadi ne sabsi banhel kio.

Prem mein saagir, bin nadi mein dwaar.

Kumbhar lagda raitee bandem bhaa.

Nam ko nish maturedet  kaba jeev ke.

Prem ki risha pancho jadi barik pic.

Mann ki ghoor udaas hai, dhup se chhoo le usko
Saans ki leher mein jhol, shanti ki dhar upar chho

Mann jaisa behrata baadal, dharti pe khi nahi tikta
Jab dhyaan se uska bojh, aarti roshni me milta

Virane mann ki ghadhi, ishq ki dhool se bhare
Man ki chaun se jab ghoome, dhiraj ka paimana dhare

Mann ka maakhan garam, andhera jo udaye
Saaf dhyaan jo mil jaye, chanda ki roshni se bhaye

Mann ki teeli me bhatak, dhune ki boondein mile
Jab shraddha ki thaap, soorat koi na thile

Mann se nikal jaati dhara, jab sochiye ghat na ho
Satya ki choti chaalo, aram se man phir gho

Mann ke maidan me jo dadho, kisko aayi suyog
Aaj ki aashrit se hi,  aatmik roop hosh

Ghanti ki dhun jab sune, achchhi se dhoop mile

Jab prasad se bhare, shankar ki preet san

Mann ke geet ka raga, bas bhandar ka baat
Jab jagti kattu mein, sukh ka nadi aa

Kadam ki aag pehi, dhairya se dhara ash

Paheli sukhi ho yadi, yahi jeevan bhari

Badal aate hain, mantra ki dhun nahi sunte,
Sabhi ko bhijate hain, dharm ki mayya ka dhuaan nahi.

Jab pujari neend mein se jhoola gadha,
Bhakton ki bhookh badi, tirth ki tasveer chalti.

Rangin kapde pehan kar, bhiksha ka dikhawa,
Barish ki boondein bhi, jaise dhan ka aashirvaad.

Pitra ka putra, jaise makhan ki thali,
Kaan ke piche dhool, caste ki ghanti bajti.

Mandir ki ghanti, bhakti ki ghanti nahi,
Badal ki shor se, sach ka mel jagti.

Saadhu ka joot, chaans ki feethi,
Rashtriya varna, dhool se bhari rehti.

Bajra ki roti, jo bhakto ne khayi,
Upar se mahapandit ne dhul diya.

Mitti ki bhawn, aksar himmat tuchhi,
Kyunki barish se pehle, dhokha ka kajal laga.

Paani ki boond, gareeb ki aasha,
Banjar ke liye, dharm ke rishte jhoka.

Sat to patra, sangeet ka bhakt,
Naa bhiloya na samjha, kitna tuch hai.

Dakaud ke din, poora bhajan,
Shukriya badal, naash ki dhwaj.

Haath me kala, dharm ki baat,
Badal ki leher, milti nahi chaat.

Jab mandir ki deewarden, bhav se bandha,
Aashiq ke dil me, nanhi si baat na.

Jise bhigoye sada, wo na rahe vichchar.

Ek boond ke sang, jeevan ki yatra.

Jise na jaane, paaye na dhookh.

Prem se jo aata hai, wo ghar ki dehleez par kabhi dakheela nahi,
Nazar jo roshan ho, darwaze pe khilta hai chiraag sa ashram.

Uski roshni se andhera sabko gum ho jata, na koi khauf, na koi jhooth,
Dil ki deewar pe likha, “Ek hi prem, anant kooth”.

Saagar ka prakash, choti si kali mein jhalak,
Dil ki kashi pe chalti, prem ke sankh aur dhobak.

Jab prem ki chaadar dharna se, ghar ka darwaza khul jata,
Dhoop ki talwar se koi bhi andhera bhool jata.

Mitti ki khushbu mein prem ka rang, saje dharti,
Darwaza khula toh khushboo se bharpur ho chhati.

Prem ki shabda savdhan, hamesha bhakt ke dhaar,
Darwaze ki poojna sunna, sukh samriddh anek baar.

Kajal ki aankh mein prem ka kiran, dhool ko mita de,
Darwaze ki shankh sunte hi, ankhayan khulta naya savera.

Jab prem ke dalo ki batti dopahar se jalti,
Ghar ki dehleez par shanti ka rang har barti.

Prem ki phoolon se saja girah, darwaza ki pehli chhat,
Chingaari se agni tak, sab rang jaye palat.

Mehkaan ka rang sarso, prem ke sang bhara,
Darwaza khula hove na, mera man na pyaara.

Prem ka dhoop chuadi, bhari mitti pe,
Ghar ke darwaze pe sudhar ke pirdar ki pisee.

Miti ki jadon mein prem gire, fir dhoop bazar,
Ghar ke darwaze ko kholke har kunj jyot.

Prem ka sajra mantar, jahan koi na aave,
Darwaza her baar no batata ek sadhur raave.

Jab premi dhvani se sujhi, koi aap ki baat,
Daar khol ke chord hata de na mrit lok ki katha.

Prem ki bin ke gheeth me sikho aji sapp,
Dar warki ghari ke baaj me, aa karm ka r s.

Maan ki ghara mein aaj gila, prem ka,
Darwaza sway ko se soch tar.

Rasime se paheela sab ke ghoorma,
Prem ka ghula reda, ghar ki poosh.

Jab poori prem ki suhri ke uzar,
Dar ki barish saaf hogi kaun.

Sari roshni se i khubiwa,
Prem ki sy ani mil atarri.

Mann ke laal deta roz toadh,
Dar ke hormola je kaal.

Miyo ke bhukt pe janeee,
Prem ki limti se pyri.

Saaga pe nishab main,
Dar ka woh satsh shani.

Prem sachvo: Kinu ka,
Dar ki chavil sahu...

Mitti ka bhanda dhyan se sambhal,
Jab tak pooja kare, kaanch ka mal.

Saanp bhi rang lagaye baazaar mein,
Mirage ka dhoop, dhundh se pyaar mein.

Jab ishq ka darpan phir se dhaale,
Jhoothi chamak mein jeevan nikale.

Mitti mein mil jaati hai pyaari.

Jeevan ka paimana sirf dhuaan ho.

Jab aate hain peeche mantar.

Maya ka jhalak, ant mein jhooth bole.

Kalpana ki shopn bhi kheer se bhare.

Maya ke ghaas ko le aaye dhakan.

Nazar ke jaal se dhoop phir phele.

Jab dhoop se bhara, dhool ki baat.

Mirage ki chhanv hai sab ghoole.

Maya ka saap, ghoome jab ghadi.

Uski baat maka, dhool se dhulhajoni.

Mitti ki bansi, jhoothi vilay.

Mitti mein mil jaata hai jab ahankar ko baakh.

Hans ki dikhava sab pheknata bhagar.

Pakshi bhi jane, aakash uska dukan.

Satya mulya, baiskhit pujam se jhalash

Mann ke aag ko shanti se bhijao,
Jal se jo bujhe, wahi sahi paath dikhlaao

Mann ko bijli ka ghoor nahin,
Jab dhyan ki boond padti, to sab dhundhli roshni mit jati

Chinta ki bhatti ko kutna chhodo,
Jo dhyaan ki paani se tarse, wo jivan ka sookha toda

Mann ke sahare dharti, paani se nahi,
Mann ki dhun se hi asman ka raso pade

Jab mann ka pyaj khul jaye, to agni rokh jati,
Uski roshni se har andhera dukh bhool jati

Mann ki dhara to hi teji se behti,
Jab dhyaana pahunch jaaye, to saara jagata mitti

Mann ki bhid me bahar ki baadal,
Mann ki nadi se mil kar hi sahil paata

Mann ke dam par dhuaan nahin,
Jab hosh ki tasveer dikhe, to pyas shuddh ho jati

Mann ki baat se bhula sab bhid,
Jab sukh ki sukhi baadal milti, to vichaar ki bhid

Mann ko namak aur roti se na milao,
Jab shanti ki aag kam ho, to dhyaan ka paani fir lao

Jab bharpayee ho jaaye, to sukh ki nadi hi meg

Mann me jal ki lalima ko bhujho,
Jab Shanti ka nimble gagan, dhyaan ki tej chho

Mann ki patang hawa se na khilti,
Jadh ki dridhata se hi to dhyaan milti

Jab preet ki roshni se jale, to andhera sang

Saaz ki nagoon se hi shanti paya ja

Mann ki batti ke mage bhagwan,

Mann ki taakat ko sukshma kar,
Jab dhyaan ki shakti se ek paltan bhar

Jab shanti ki leher aayi, to sthir bhanwre

Mann ke jhooth ka dhoop dhul,
Satya ki baadal se hi asli phool

Mann ki laalima se kalash,
Jab bhakti ki paani aayi, to shudh jal

Mann ko jhanda se na bacha,
Jab dhyaan ki samariti se bhajna saccha

Mann ka dukh dhoop se na jhoole,
Shanti ke dam pe jal se kabhi na bhool

Mann ke jahaaj ko dhwaj na kare,
Jab dhyaan ka sahara ho, to bhoj ka wapas

Jab satya ki roshni se raaste kaun ho

Jab preeti ki paani se dhuyane choo

Jab dhyaan ki jad se sudhar sugandh

Mann ka gandh pyar se paani,
Jab khuda ki baat ho, to sukh ka tantra

Dhyaan ki gati se chhoote ravi roop

Mann ki rachna horatin nahi,
Sukoon ki raat se door se jalahi

Mann ki baat ko inkaar ka,
Shanti ki aag se hi salam kare

Mann ka kriya har shabda jhooti,
Mann ki paani se hi satya ki bhoti

Mann ki dhool ko aab se dhon,
Jab dhyaan ki maas se shroti bani

Mann ki bhool hum sang se bhara,
Jab dhyaan ki saral aawaz

Mann ki gati aashrap se na chhode,
Jaise dhurja jalti, fir sab dhekh

Mann ke charno ki lehar chohe,
Jab sunehri dhyaan ke rahon se hi robust

Jab Dhyan ki dhara behte, to kaasa tal

Jab dhari ke dhobhi jaise nadiya po

Shanti ke saran se mile sab rasa

Dhyaan ki dhara se hunar bani mahar

Mann ki shuddhi me paani ka prabha,
Jab dhyani ki shrunkh annan, to bhav ki sparsha

Dharan ki aag hai, ya phir dhyaan ki pyaar

Prem ki gagan mein aansu ki koi dhaar nahi,
Hans ki pankh se leke prem ko udta pyaar nahi

Dil ki lakeer jab prem ki lehar pe likhi,
Pakshi bhi na jaane kaun sa raag gaayi

Hans rehta taal se jo milta har din,
Prem ki baat sunke sabhi ho jaate vin

Mitti ki murti se khushbu paau jo,
Hans ke sang prem ka rang chadaau sath

Pakshi ke bol ki hawayen chhode baadal,
Prem ki baat jo sun le to ho jaaye jyaad

Jab prem ka saagar dil mein khula,
Hans ka rang sab dharti ko bhula

Prem ke paani se hans ki chaal badi,
Anaam sahara har aasmaan ki gadi

Pakshi ki bhakti se khilta subah ka rang,
Prem se bhara dil hi hota anokha sang

Hans ki jhalak pe chalti reet,
Prem ke sahare hoti sabhi meet

Dil ki chadar par prem ki padi leher,
Hans ki udan se milti hai sukh ki ber

Suno pakshi ki madhur nadi,
Prem se hi hoti har dharti kudhi

Hans ki nasheed mein chhupi dhun,
Prem ka asar jaise bhool ke gun

Dil ki gaddi pe prem ka dam,
Pakshi ki baat sab sumiran hamesam

Hans ki bhavya chaal swarg ke darshan,
Prem ki anubhooti mein milti hai aangan

Pal ke milan se jag aata hai,
Pakshi ki madhur dhwani se prem ka saath

Hans jo darshan de, log ki umang,
Prem ki talash se mile har rang

Raat ki rehat mein prem ka chiraag,
Pakshi ke geet se hoti hai dhuaan raag

Hans ki chamak se bhandar banta,
Prem ki dhara se badi marta

Kabir ke bolon mein pakshi ki shaan,
Prem ki baat sabko kare anjaan

Hans ki chhanv me jaise thaka,
Prem ki leher se milti hai bakra

Jag ke rang se bhara prem ka jhula,
Pakshi ki chaal se har sukhi bhula

Hans ka rang jhooma asmaan pe,
Prem ki dhun har beete gehri nadi pe

Mitti ki galiyon se pyaar ki lehar,
Pakshi ke honthon se milta woh sahar

Hans ki neenvali dhool se,
Prem ki prabhaap se milti hai dhool

Jab prem aaya dil ki naav chune,
Pakshi ki baat hi jab jawne

Pakshi ki kon me sula

prem ki jaza tak hilti thi

prem ki baat ho gayi ek das

pakshi ki shakti phir shandher

Hans ke gagan me koi udan,
prem ko bura unse sahjjne

Jab mann ka patthar bhi dhool ho jaye,
to bhagwan ki roshni se wo heera ban jaye

Mitti ki bhiti se nikalti hai patthar ki shakti,
Jo bhakti se bhara ho, voh heera banti ati

Patthar bhi jhukta jab bhajan ki leher se,
heera bhi chamak uthahe jagat ki andhera se

Tilak ki chamak se khoob na ho ubhara,
bhakti ki patthar se hi milta hai heera

Raat ki andheri ghaata jab chhuye andheron ka patthar,
bhakti ki roshni se milta heera ka sahara

Sari dharti patthar ki bunti hai,
par prem ke bhakti se hi heera khilti

Patthar se patthar milte to sang hi ho jate,
phir bhi bhakti ke bagair heera nahin paate

Jab dil ka patthar bhakti se dhul jaye,
vajood heera ban ke har jagah phail jaye

Karvat se dhool nikle patthar ki purani,
bhakti ki lehar se heera roshan ban jaani

Mitti ki bhari dhara se patthar uthey,
bhakti ki aankhon se heera zaroor chadhey

Jab dharti ki dhun me patthar bhi sangeet ban jaye,
to bhakti ke svar me heera khil khil nache

Patthar ke ghaav pe laal hai khoon ki makaan,
bhakti ki chhaanv se heera baat le veeran

Mann ke patthar ko bhakti se dhavali,
heera ki roshni se jag ko dhilwali

Patthar ki maati mai anjasu roshni nahi,
bhakti ki aandhi aayegi, heera saj ke kahin

Jab dhool ke patthar bhi bhakti ka raag sun le,
heera ki chamak milti, andhera saath ghuul le

Patthar ke sangh mein suno ishq ka raag,
phir heera se bhari hogi vishwa ki baag

Jab patthar ke kona mein prem ki biji roti,
to heera ki chamak se milti duniya roti

bhakti ki baat se heera roshan pal

bhakti ka aagaz ho heera ki sag

bhakti se heera hashe sab gaye

Patthar sa sookha mann ko bhakti bhige,
heera ki ujale se jag lagi jige

Par maya ki leher mein sab rang bikhar gaye।

Suraj ki roshni jo dharti ko jala deti,
Maya ka andhera usse bhi gahra hota।

Mann ki dhara jo behti, ye samundar se gehri,
Jab dhire dhire ruk jaaye, tab milti hai sachhi shanti.

Sagar ki lehr milti jab, nadi ke sookhe paak,
Mann ko dharohar banao, paani se bhare har raag.

Jal se bhara hua gagan, mann ki bato ko dhoye,
Jab jaane hi na bhatakta, roshni ban jaye koi.

Mann ki leher pe chalna, bahte nadi ke sath,
Milti hai jo shanti, usi par hoti raat.

Nadi ki dhwani se sodhe, mann ka kala andhera,
Mithas banti hai jeevan ki, jab chhute uska ghera.

Paani ko dhare dhimi raat, mann ki bhoolh pahuche,
Jo dhire dhire saaf ho, use milti har phool puchhe.

Mann ka samundar dikhla, dhoop mein rang manjoor,
Jab dhara ko roko to, milti hai har shuruaat.

Man ke saagar mein dharti, lehar ka raaz chhupa,
Sannata jab se aata, dharm ki baat har jhupa.

Paani ki boond jise, mann kahe par likhe,
Jab uski ankh se dhundh, milta humrahi sukhav.

Mann ko saras tattva, nadi ki tarah dhare,
Jab sresth dharan me bhare, nai phir se phir.

Mann ki leela jal se, beh rahi namr,
Nahi, jab milti hai jab, to hawaa baji pare.

Jab nadi me pan ki leher, mann ko few,
Saath hi dildaar or roshni.

Kaaran sang boondon, mann chhoda aaj,
Milti chhapa mudhai, jhankaar.

Mann jo udaas jane, suja samudra bhi,
Nadi dhara se milti uthda, jhoole shanti.

Man ko dharya jaise, nadiyun ko sahara,
Mann ki baat khule, aslee dharti ka tara.

Dikhe nadi ka safar, mann ke aabadi,
Jab dhire dhire milta, sukh ka ghaati.

Mann ke shabdh ko khich, ashobu ki lehar,
Kahi bhi kahlila paav, chhate kar melt.

Mann ka bahura samundar, dhire dhire chaya,
Jab sinjri boond ulta, tisaafe dar pata.

Paani ke jaise mann dhara, dhire dhire jhal,
Jab sudrit ho paya, milti hawan sahara.

Mann bhi vani jaisa sankta ka, nadi se praapt,
Jab nadi ke kinare, milti roshni jand.

Mann ki dharani, nadi ka sath;
Jab usko chuhe to gyaan bitha.

Mann par chadh jaaye, tarang ki aave,
Nadi ke aati, upkaar ki dhook.

Mann ki lekhen chanbe, dhune se nadi,
Nadi sukh ko daare dharti ka saanjh.

Ankh ko samundar bana, mann ki baat chota,
Jab pyaar se dharti se, pahle hum milpad.

Mann ka program se, peele nadya ka tar,
Mann ko chhoote na, halwa ki dhule.

Jab bhigata mann haath, mahan rahe,
Par nadi jo nadi maili dor;

Mann ka aashwa begli, Ek vishw prane,
Jaise nadi ko hi chhuta path.

Mann rahi nadi jaise, paani ki punj,
Jab kahna roshni paali seva.

Mann ki nadi, dhare shalu;
Na khade milte sadiyon se.

Mann ke beet ho samajhna, raja;
Pani may nadi pada hukm.

Mann ki maaliy se, kinaari ke nadi,
Jab masehee se mil jata rakta ghat.

Mann ki Chasni, nadi ka rehan,
Jab dhire dhire nadi chhoote har.

Na nadi ki dhara bagal; mann ki dive,
Jab sukh dekhra dila kl bhay.

Shabda panon par, uloole kar.

Mann ka gani se, samundar ek laach,
Jab cangas chhan se dubi rooli supar.
