Tab talaash hain gult.

Jab mann ka talab saaf, Hans bhi daudta dhar ki ore
Jeevan ki bhool bhool ko, dhundho apne antarmoh ki roshni se

Kali ghata ke baadal, mitti se lete nahi aavashyak
Hans ki pankh pe bina padhi, gyaan ki rekhayen rang laate hain

Sukoon ka tihra raasta, bhool bhool ke bazar mein milta nahi
Hans ko dekh ke samajh ja, atma ki pyaas kabhi bharti nahi

Jab dil ki dhool saaf ho, to bhakti ka rang naya hota
Hans ki shakti se bhanjti, andhera ko chamkaataa roshan

Mann ki nadi mein basti, soch ki lehron ka samundar
Hans ke udaan se milti, manav ki atma ki chadar

Pitri ke paath ko chhodo, pran ki dhun mein dhun bhajna
Hans ko dekh kar samjho, sach ka rang bas prakash

Beej sadiyon ka, ankhon se na pakad sake koi
Hans ki talash mein milti, sookshma roshni ki roop bhayi

Mai re maya ki baandh, gyaanik atma ko bandarhi
Hans ki adhoot srishti, veer jaisa ubhar khadi

Mitti ki chatri ke neeche, baadal ki kamal nahi
Hans ka milna atma ke andar, judaahi ka kshama dahi

Gyaan ke ranjhe se jo bata, rachna ki nadi ka chalan
Hans ki watan pee dharti se, vishwa ke mulya de dhyan

Suna chhupa dharti, jab mann ka haar rahe turant
Hans ke pankh se aadar, kiye man ki hai sandhi

Anjana ghoomti ghan, man ki barish ko roke na paave
Hans ko dhundho samvedan, kabir ka roshni sadhave

Chhupa roop roop ki vasant, dhormi ke palm se teenahi
Hans ki bindiro se samjho, antaran ke dhiran se pehli

Mitti ki chadar par mast, raat ki chudiyaan chhode
Hans ki clue se aado, vishwa ke pariksha rogde

Phillki khilti rahi, janam ke beete saathi
Hans ko dekho to pucho, keval bhraaman shanti

Jhilmil roshni ka andhera, sabhi dhulaa koshik ke asar
Hans ki gaanvan baazi se, gyaan ko koi dhara mar

Bandhan ki belli ke bade, sare jhakki ki satiyan
Hans ki poojan ke liye, har dhara mein milti jivan

Bhram ke mitti se dhoop, jivan ki dhadkan dunia
Hans ki reina se dekho, shanti ka rango bande

Mann ka taar kyanin, choti se sitara hai
Hans ki simti aawaz, aadhyatma ke sewa

Raat ke aangan mein, har hor ka chin baras
Hans ke baadal se jhoome, datum ki sugandh ki kshat

Sannata baadal ki bhari, sudha ka prabhaat bhi na hai
Hans ko bhagyasha ki kumti, andar ki chadhayi

Mann ki saysi jehan hai, patrasth dhoop ki mree
Hans ki daani na ki, bhagwan ki baat ko

Rah ki talwara, man ki chal ki dhne se
Hans ko aapne hum, sukhi samaj ki nigah

Pran ko bharatiyan, garam jogi rahti
Hans ki wasili hamari utri gyaan ka

Ganga majh ki dhara, thand ke badi jhol
Hans ke sapno se balin boli, bhakti ki padi

Aankh ke saaf, bhul chahati ki doori
Hans ke roop se dekhna, har dogho ka ladna

Nadi ka thahra height, jayantra ki jhiun khok
Hans ki chadar se vihi ki uthuth

Mannaa ka komal premun, soorya ki bhor ki raate
Hans ke chakkar mei sukh se jitne liye

Shukal ki chhan, dharm ki dhoop chhal
Hans ki pir ki nirdhan aur shashwan

Ektout ka avar, sara mukti poom
Hans ki pehal men dhokarat ke dha

Nadi ke chandmo bhoot te, ijda ke nindak ki manai
Hans ki achaap mantar milat nadi manche izhar

Jeevanasun se deep loyi, kal ka asparsh ke sadaa
Hans ki dharm se poja chalta kyun raaz

Miti ko aaj la, saada baar ke mahatih raj
Hans ke guru na ke milan, jahaan roshni ki balam

Tiranga jelaate, sang aangan se nara
Hans ke jaal ki bari ka nava haa

Kabir ki bhakti aayi, mana se naav chhodi
Dil ke dariya mein, prem hi paar dhodi

Jab mann ka ghumtaa hai, mooshak se chalak re
Jo vilamti chalata, uska raah sukh bhare

Mitti ke putla karj, dhukha na dhyaan ka
Brahman ka paani pi, man ko dhool se dho

Taal mein bhajan ki lehar, hosh ke baadal chale
Naav ko samajh gaye, jo dhoop aakaar le

Jheel ki rassi koi, satya ki shakti bhari
Jab man bilkul cheen le, naav ka na samjhaari

Saagar ki lehar aayi, naav ka haath padhaye
Jo dharti se uttha, bhakti se aadhyaaye

Mann ka girah bandha, tooti parchkaan ki talaash
Mitti pe likhi baat, kaun bhar de uska aash

Jalwa ke daur se, naav ki chaal dharti pe
Bhakti ki mashal se, har andhera dhruj me

Pashu pashu bolta, naav ke raste joda
Magar jo nahi maane, uska phool na todha

Mann ka ghoomra ghee, tuta na harkahi
Jab dhyan dhool se bhara, naav mile satya ki sahi

Dukh se bachke rah, naav ka bahana na kar
Jo bhakti ki sahar, paatha vishvaas ki bhinn

Nadi ki dharti mein, aatma ka safar
Kahin batriya wae, koi aakaash ke khadar

Patra ko padhkar a, raasta dhundh tars
Jo doob gaya, usi ko naav ki sang

Jhilmil pyaala nadi ke, aadi vishwa ka aadhar
Bhakti ki laharen, parvat ki choti se jodh

Aati re dhara, naav ko dhokar aave
Nam ke sang se milti, isma sabhi rakhave

Ghadi ghadi bhav, aavaj ke sang laye
Jo bhakti man ko, uski chiti dhokar sathaaye

Kahan se aaya karm, kahan se jaave yeh
Je bhakti ko piche bhul, naav uska dekhe

Nar koi naavat bhakt, krip jag ho thai
Paratri samundar rama, dhire dhire bolyai

Mitti ki shangri, nadi ki baheta roshni
Bhakti ke darwaze, naav ko dhak mitra paani

Kaidi ka jala, dhar ka bhi lahan sandar
Naav sang dhul janaa, jannat ki disha samandar

Jug jug gadh shauk, man ki bhakti sandh
Naav ki aag nikale, shri aashirvat anand

Jheel ki dhapri; bhakti nayi sochi
Jab bhagwan ki amar, har veo samjhai

Agar man ka paim, roop roshan roshni
Rang vina naav hal, raat ka mahanani

Saree suyag, phool kosha naav, gagan ka
Kadam ki rasta, bhakti se khushi fatah

Samay ki lehr bhari, naav ko chhuna padta,
Jab paar na pehchane, to naav kahin bhi na taba.

Kadme ki dhool se bhara, samay ka tirath pota,
Jab halke haath lag jaaye, to samajh aata bhota.

Naav ko sooraj samaye, chhaap to chubhti dhara,
Jab samay ki dhun na suno, to gajab ka naara.

Kirnein milti hain nadi, samay ko kya paida,
Jo naave dhare dekhte, to kahan se aayi harida.

Chalti hui ghadi, naav ki dhaar jaisa,
Jab baarish bhari ho, to kabhi na miley dhoosha.

Paani se bhara pot, samay ki reet bunti,
Jab naav udegii, to gire na bhanti.

Aankh se dekho samay, naav ki maang potem,
Jo kabhi na uthe, voh moh ka sathi dhom.

Jal ki lehr samay, naav ki naav doon,
Bandhan jo tutta, to milte hain pune.

Pushp raat ki, samay ka ghum, naav milti nazli,
Jab khumaar chhad de, to milna nahi koi khali.

Samay ki dhula, naav ki matirang,
Jab man se milae, to aati nahi tanga.

Van ki godi, samay ki kahaani, naav dooda dhoor,
Jab dhaara samne aayi, dukh nahee sake koor.

Raat ki nadi, samay ka mod, naav ko doobna,
Jab sandhya hue, kankar bhi gire jodna.

Mann ki uljhan, samay ka sagar, naav ki patang,
Jab dhyan se dekh le, to milti na bhoot rang.

Samay ke raaton me, naav se nahin dhoor,
Jab dharti girti, to milti na ghur.

Mitti ki batti, samay ki gati, naav ka dhoop,
Jab aalok kare se, to milti nahi chhoop.

Aasman ki leher, samay ka pran, naav ki baadh,
Jab pahunche sukh se, to dhyan bhul raha sadh.

Pal dobaara, samay ki mahaka, naav ka jharna,
Jab uthi dhool, to jaaye na pehran.

Bhoole jo samay, naav ki sies,
Jab uske bina, milti nahi visesh.

Jal ki kadhi, samay ki rekh, naav ki pichli,
Jab bikhar jaati, to milti na bhikri.

Kashmir ki nadi, samay ki sahara, naav ki raftaar,
Jab farsh chhuta, to aashra kam aabaar.

Man ki dhara, samay ki laakh, naav ki lag,
Jab chadh jaati, to nirmal na ho bhag.

Ganga ki goonj, samay ki gujar, naav ki kayi,
Jab raasta nikle, to milti koi suyayi.

Raat ke pahad, samay ki awaz, naav ki rassi,
Jab dhund lagaai, to milna bhool kassi.

Mitti ki baat, samay ka mel, naav ki reh,
Jab chand ka roop, to sangh kam aashil.

Dharti ka pavan, samay ki richi, naav ki chhaap,
Jab dhoop ki kunj, to milti hi sudhap.

Jal ka jharna, samay ki sund, naav ki karta,
Jab bhool ho dharti, to korban achha.

Ghum ki ghadi, samay ki maati, naav ka khura,
Jab bhari ho baaj, to milti bhula.

Mohan ki chhanv, samay ka jad, naav ki khand,
Jab jali rahe, to na rahe andhar.

Pankh ki roti, samay ki dhul, naav kai pul,
Jab soya saaya, to milti na bhol.

Ragh ke raaste, samay ki lap, naav ka rang,
Jab prithvi nachti, to milti pyar sang.

Aas ki dhool, samay ke sanket, naav ki sahar,
Jab dard dhunka, to naye din ki pasar.

Saagar ka suraj, samay ki lehr, naav ka baksh,
Jab dheere chalti, to na chara akash.

Kal ki khumaar, samay ke raaz, naav ki dharm,
Jab dharm se na jaye, to jehan aati zam.

Mangal ka din, samay ki badi, naav ki hansi,
Jab bhul jaye rishte, to milti bhoolesht.

Oorja vahan, samay ki lehar, naav ka bandhan,
Jab jhilmil hoti, to na keval dhala.

Kadmeer ki kiran, samay ki poori, naav ki pankh,
Jab aashirvaad milte, to jeevan se sath khank.

Pushing gali, samay ki nadi, naav ki rahi,
Jab dharati ko chur, to milti koi rahi.

Ankhon ka paudh, samay ki dhun, naav ki dhoop,
Jab tathaara ho, to baadal na dhup.

Kagaz ki ship, samay ki nashaa, naav vaan,
Jab raahein gehri, to laila ke sang.

Madhur swar, samay ki chad, naav ka lini,
Jab dhoop path, to sukh aash ramni.

Lakshya ki palki, samay ki lagata, naav ki duhai,
Jab sang hati ki, to milti na alai.

Aatish ki bayaan, samay ki nik, naav ki chir,
Jab gulab ko aati, to milta na chhir.

Pankh ki bhari, samay ki bauddh, naav sechan,
Jab jazba kharcha, to milti asas mein.

Jal ki dhara, samay ki khani, naav ki bhang,
Jab pahar taapte, to milti na rang.

Aag ki jhalar, samay ke bhan, naav ki sah,
Jab shakti se, to milti anukhan.

Raat ki tarah, samay ki ma, naav ka juk,
Jab aaj ki dharti, to milna bhavuk.

Sookhi vaniya, samay ki bhari, naav ki hava,
Jab brahma tegi, to sukh da nava.

Prem ki kath, samay ki noor, naav se aadi,
Jab bhram intezar, to galat peadi.

Mitti ki bhag, samay ki aaj, naav ki dire,
Jab istemaam badi, to milti dhoor.

Awaaz ki raat, samay ki charkha, naav ka pattan,
Jab dur ho jaaye, to milta abhi nattan.

Jagmag paath, samay ki dhoop, naav ki mith,
Jab bhaktil ko, to chut jaata kit.

Satguru ki chhaon mein jai, milti hai barsaat dhan,
Jab dhyan se dhara chhute, to bhul jaye sab vichaar.

Badal jaisa mann dhoye, jo dhup se bhara ho,
Sohra bhajan ki boonden, bhool jaaye andhera.

Jab sangati sadh-ras hai, to bhoola mausam ka dukh,
Mitti ke bhanwar mein sukh, jaise paani ke sookh.

Sant ki baat sun lo, barish ke jaise anup,
Jal jahan se dhare, waha se milti hai chaup.

Chandni ki dhup mein bhi, sant milte nahin,
To boondein badal ki, bhari jeevan ki dhun.

Mann ki ghata ko dhoye, jab bhakti ka jhoom,
Khud ko paise ki barish, bhool kar gaye ghoom.

Sadh-sangati ki boondein, chahe ghanere baadal,
Taal ko bhula de raati, gagan ki chadar dal.

Jhuk kar jo sang kalika, bhare bharosa ka bhandar,
Barish bhare talwar mein, milti hai shanti ka aakar.

Sant ki dhwani se dhul, rang jode sukh bhara,
Jab nikle gaadi dhara, har tarah ka sukhra.

Bharat ki dharti barish, sangati ki boondein kare,
Jab dhyaan se chhalke, har roshni ka nariyan.

Rimjhim ki boondein satguru ke, samjhe karuna ka rang,
Jaise rusmai aayi hai, man ki madhur dharanga.

Munh ki baat to lagti, baras ki baadal bhari,
Sang kamal ki ankhon se, milti hai gyan ki dhari.

Sankat ki barish aaye, sangati aap samjha,
Har pal ka phool khile, jab milti hai ek doha.

Badal hote dhumein phir, bhool kamzor dilon se,
Sant ki dhun se padhare, jagte hain gagan ke sile.

Mitti ki boondein sab jhilmil, jab sangati siddha ho,
Reth ki ghati ka ghum bhool, sukhi ho jaye pair.

Satguru ki chhanv se, barish ka rang badh jaye,
Sabhi ka mann rahe, jaise bhanwar ki baaz.

Bheege hum sangati ke, jaisa gagan ki boonde,
Aashirwad ki bhadi se, mann ka sanam ghoonde.

Kabir ki sangati me, badal ka rang anup,
Har vishwan me baje dhadkan, karan ki dhup.

Mann ki baat aisi, sadh ki boonde baras,
Jab ghee se bhi mil jaye, kertas ke rang ke vas.

Jab simrat bhajan ki barish, chahe badal udaya,
Sumir dhyaan ka rang, ghar ka dhool mita paya.

Sadh-sangati ki kamli, baadal ki nirmal taan,
Aao bhaj sabko bhanj, riti ke karam dhyaan.

Mitti se monti jo, barish me nikle paya,
Sant ki bhakti ko, lokon ki patang bhara.

Sangati ka paheli, barish ki moshik chhaye,
Satguru ki sanskri, har dhool ko roshan bhaye.

Chal sahaaye sang, barish bhari dhunon ki,
Magar jaise vishal jhool, padi paan ki rani.

Sadhana ka raasta, barish ki baadal ki roshni,
Sankalan se mita hua, sabhi chhupte rothi.

Jab mil singhal badal, sant ki preet ke dhaar,
Har jhoothe roshan ho, badlon ke roop mein haar.

Nadi ko paani jaise, sant ki bina aashir,
Badal se bhara nadi ka, mil jata neeti ki dhar.

Kabir ki boondein, sangati ki raat ke char,
Durdarsh haanta main, aise hota sahhaar.

Bhraman ka raat jaisa, sant ki boondein hote,
Jab bhi ankh se behle, barish ka dharti mein float.

Matha baandh dhoop se, sant ki baadal ka sang,
Manjil ki agnike jaisa, baadal me gandh ka rang.

Sant bina chhoot jise, hunar rahe bandhan,
Nadi aur havale aise, barish ke roop me panah.

Sanskriti ki kavi, badal ka pardey daal,
Sant ko dekh yaad ki, shabda ka bhasma.

Jab bhakti ka varsh, barish ka rava gaye,
Kuba karun mantri bhi, sadh ki aazadi bhaye.

Aadhyatma ka jahaaz, bhir dh udra meh,
Sadh-sangati badal ki, ye anant vikas ke.

Dhire dhire baadal ke sang, sant ki aabir dhoop,
Mann ka nadi, saawan, jeevan ko dhool se roop.

Dikri se ghoorna, dhoop ko baadal na hoy,
Saach sangati ki roop, milti diggaj ka jooy.

Jab sadhna ke maalik, barish ka uslub sag,
Mann bhi phool ki odh, kahin, dharm ke sang.

Sant ki galaj, dhumri ki dhun, sahare baadal,
Jab jag me asal mahar, jab chhoka dhundha sthir.

Barish ki boondein prahar, sahaj ki jati sahar,
Sangati paate hain desh, jab vakt me khola dhar.

Satguru ke jaise, baadal ki roop bhari,
Har pranayi ko milti, bhakti ki gudi soori.

Bhoomi bardi ki dhool, line barish ke sang,
Sant ki aark man, bhakti ka dhwane rang.

Bári barish mati chura, har dhurandhar he,
Mann ko sina, dassh sahar mein hi bharat re.

Satchip ki baadal ki, bhakti men prajal taab,
Sant ki sundar aadar ata ke sang oh.

Tandav ka jaalam, barish ki dhool se ma,
Maal nidhan sabke, sant ki seva ke kaam

Bangal ki jhilmili, barish bhandal ke te,
Mere bhakti me radhi, aave sant ki akel.

Saagar ka katar, barish ki masti se zh,
Sant ki dana me poojan bulta sab jh

Sangati ki dhuk, barish bhari sara ke,
Bhoshi baat bichar ke, jag ke bhanje ne.

Guru ki baat ko sun, mann ka darpan sapna ho,
Jab uski roshni padi, andhera bhi chamak jaata hai.

Kaanch ke jaisa naazuk, guru ka shabd le chal,
Jhankaar se bhare mann ki bhav, dhundh se pakad le pal.

Guru ki bani se hi, jeevan ki kahani khul jaaye,
Darpan mein apna roop dikhaye, jise hum bhool na paaye.

Jo guru se door bhage, uska hi chara dhool ho,
Palang ki piroti mein bhi, uski yaad ka bhool ho.

Guru ka ayina hum, apna hi andhera dikhaye,
Uski jhalak se hi, roop sadhna ka safar ban jaaye.

Darpan ka chhavi wo, jo sachcha dhyaan sikhaye,
Guru bina man ka rang, andhera hi rahe dhusriye.

Guru ki maang par saja, hum sabke sapne ke jale,
Kaanch ki prashasti se hi, dil ki paayas mil jaale.

Guru ka aashirvaad se, jeevan ka saagar sukh bhara,
Darpan ki baadal se bhi, disha na bhoolna pyara.

Guru se milne waala, apni rooh ka darpan banaye,
Jab bhool jaye sach, to kaanch ki bhang se samjhe.

Guru ka paath padh ke, sab dhul kharchi nikalti,
Kaanch ke bano ki baad mein, bhakti ka rang phailti.

Guru ki baat ko jaan, man ka parda uchal jaata,
Jaise darpan ka aabro, roshni se sabkhilta.

Guru dhare jaave aag ka, jo mann ko pighale mil,
Kaanch ki choti duniya, tab hi roop bhav se bhil.

Guru ki nadi ka main kahin, man ke piche bhare,
Darpan ka har shabd, ujala doosri dhare.

Guru ki kirna se hi, kaanch ke jhilmil raaste,
Mann ki dhool mita de, jinhen andhera dhoste.

Jab guru ki tasveer dakke, to darpan ghoome shafaf,
Uski chhaap se baahar, na rahe koi faltuf.

Guru bin dharti vadi, kacchi shaktiyon ka khal,
Darpan chhupa jo, usko dhund se hi pakad le.

Guru ho jagat ka sahara, darpan se sach ko dhoondhe,
Kaanch ki chubi mein bhi, sukh ka prakash chhodhe.

Guru ki baat kahin, man ki dhool dhakar jaye,
Darpan ki shaili ban ke, sach ka rang dikhaye.

Guru ki boondri se, milti hai sabki roshni,
Kaanch ki zoor se hi, jeevan ki dukan kholi.

Guru ki dhrrr se baazi, man mein suyog ka vastav,
Darpan ki bhavna se, sabko mita de bhav.

Guru milte hi dil ko, vishwas ka pola milta,
Kaanch ki tasveer, anek chehre dikhaati milta.

Guru ki pehchan se, andhera bhi chamakse,
Darpan ki dhaar ki tarah, sab ki ashram se bhare.

Guru ki choti ladayi, mann ke darpar ki jhal,
Kaanch ki tinke se bhi, man ka paang garshal.

Guru ke bhakti se man, manzil ki roshni paata,
Darpan ki saajh se hi, uchcha dhume se mitaataa.

Guru ki leela mein, man ka bhi mazboot darpan,
Kaanch ki bodhi se, maan sikhaye nirmaan.

Guru pure kar sab, shabdon ke saajh darpan,
Kaanch ki chaap se hi, sabko gahranto na samjhe.

Guru ke charan shabd, jaisa prateek darpar ki,
Man khaadi mein bhi sajaaye, raahez ka ek bharpur.

Guru ki kasam, man ka patra, kaanch ka papad,
Darpan ke sang kabhi bhi kisee ko shamil nad.

Guru ki bhav se jag, sab ras ki minar choda,
Kaanch ki mehfil mein hi, roshni se bhara.

Guru ke aaj ki anubhav, bhav is saamne darpar,
Kaanch ka bhoot jab jaaye, man ka rang aag jal.

Guru ke gita, benjri ke darpan, dhoop se khule,
Man ki chamat karna bhi, baat ka prakash hu jale.

Guru ki madhur dhun, har dhuli mirch koyi,
Kaanch ki limp se bhi, jaise roti ka paigam hoyi.

Guru ki baaton se dharm, sarv-ras mei batata,
Darpan ka noor se, mukt hi dharm niraata.

Guru ki vitri, man ki jhalak, jhoothi bahu,
Kaanch ki aabadi sai, bhakti ki shakti jagaye.

Guru ki pairi haath me, man ke kailash darpar,
Kaanch ki aab shreemadhi se, bhakti ka dwaar bhare.

Guru ke charas se, jhulay ham man ki dhool,
Darpan ki bhakti mein hi, jivan ka sukh ghoole.

Guru ka aadarsh, sab khola darash, man ka isnad,
Kaanch ki darshi bhi, rahim mein mil jaata prasad.

Guru ki chitthi mil ke, darpan ki tarah se baat,
Sab shabdon ka rang, kitaabi path se aata baat.

Guru ke shabd ki kund, man ka dhulusun darpar,
Kaanch ki dhara se samein, aise roshni ka kar.

Guru ki sabha bandh, nahin koi prashn ko chhod,
Darpan ki dhara me he, yah sarvashakti svid.

Guru bina aankh kiandi, dhool jeevan ki patni,
Kaanch ki vaat mein, mana dhoya chara nahi.

Guru ki gatha suri, man darpar ki tychh,
Darpan ki raat se hi, rahen dil ki roop kyoch.

Guru ko dhooli badi, dukh ki jay ki hoiet,
Kaanch ki paarshil se, hoit janbad ki bhuur.

Guru ki har paasp, man ko ashish bhari,
Darpan ki barah se, roshni ki aashir bharii.

Guru ki gat, man ka shalim, yo rah ki intizaar,
Kaanch ki dharani se, paay sakte chu bhi pyaar.

Ahankaar ka jhaad bhara, naav na dhaare koi,
Sahasri samundar paar khaale, jogi bhare aayo gaye.

Man ke dhoop se jalta, naav ka paani bhi kare,
Jab ahankaar tod do, to sab ko milti raftar.

Naav chalta dharti ki dhun pe, ahankar ka ghana,
Jab harbar rahi dharti se, to milti shanti bhara.

Aakash ki tarah baadal, naav ki shakti gaay,
Ahankaar jab ghul jaaye, to paani mil jaaye.

Naav ki lahar se gaye, ahankaar ki bhari,
Jab dhyaan uth jaave bina, to paani sukh bhare.

Jal ki lehron mein bhari, ahankar ki dhoop,
Naav ke aage kood ke, bhool jaao roop.

Paani ka jaal hai anmol, ahankaar ke dikhave,
Naav se joh ho sahi, mil jaataan har savere.

Machhli ke sang jhooti, ahankaar ki paal,
Naav ke beech chhidke, milti hai mahan baal.

Samudra ki shaanti me, ahankar ka dhool,
Naav ko chalne do milke, mil jayein sookh school.

Jab ghadi ka tha kaam, ahankaar ki bhavra,
Naav par dhire dhire, poorna mile sada.

Dhwaj ki hawa chalti, naav ki aas-wali,
Ahankaar se baazgi, Chhode jaye masti anjali.

Nadi ki baat se kahe, ahankaar bhul ja,
Naav ko khune se bhara, nadhi ke korche pa.

Tara ki roshni me, naav ki tattva paid,
Ahankaar ko na pade, jaise nadi ka aatma ga.

Naav ke ghul gaye, ahankaar ki bhav,
Jab chhodein udasi, jhaankar ho ja santav.

Palki ki feed me, ahankaar ki bhumi,
Naav ke sang na rahe, milte hain sahi dhuni.

Mitti ki paani se jhuta, ahankaar ka sankat,
Naav ki chaden dharye, sabhi chil karte sat.

Dharm ki banti se baje, ahankaar bachhau,
Naav ke marg par jaane, milkewale farsh bhav.

Nadi ki baadal me milti, ahankaar ko mrityu,
Naav par baansi saav se, pahuch hae nava.

Raat ke aashiq hue, ahankaar ke santu,
Naav ke srishti ke liye, bhare moksh ka dantu.

Ganga ki dhool ko likh, ahankaar tatha sar,
Naav tarob hata gava, khud basta side dar.

Charnas ki pahin bhaag, ahankaar uttarh,
Naav ka ghoshi hai, khooj ke satta ko ratr.

Kankad ki ansu, ahankaar ke sahi,
Naav ke gath te phir, baandho khaas chaadi.

Madhyam ki drishti maadi, ahankaar jab jhaalee,
Naav mashon dhara, san chuk jati viyeli.

Sahlaap ki baat se, ahankaar ki dhara,
Naav ke nadiyon pe, bhagpur kara saptara.

Nadi ko darna ada, ahankaar ko dhundho
Naav ki hathmey parchhe, swayam bandhu bhoundho.

Mehli ki aab adhi, ahankaar ko bhool,
Naav khula nahi ghoore, jair ham udhar koot.

Saadi ki satya ki baik, ahankaar  pe neu,
He Raja linterath, naav dil me sute.

Pag dhoop kal, ahankaar dhire re,
Naav ke sivogaar sahi, daroga fee ke feste.

Bharat ke padi dhola, ahankaar ko nihal,
Naav ke kura saye, chood best meer kaviyal.

Dhumra gaayak ki, ahankaar aahi tak,
Naav khisak yahi sang kisi re me bata.

Moksha ko gajvi, ahankaar chhinak se,
Naav me namdah, jis se sagin ho jab.

Ujaal ki kiran, ahankaar you le,
Naav ka abse, mol dam se ratte.

Ladki ki umar, ahankaar hilna,
Naav se chqnous, limb jeya tar.

Nihitiar aur bhakti, ahankaar zivmeh,
Naav per bantu, bhagyo rati shoji

Sadhak ki dyana, ahankaar tor ka,
Naav har noogh, lahaz ka jagrat.

Chadaav ka choirh, ahankaar abagaan,
Naav kep hari sami, dun jeevel saran.

Kalla ki saan, ahankaar ka gha,
Naav beini naih, jig arjari kar datha.

Jab dhokho se nikal, ahankaar kshurd,
Naav kara tangri koi, hit po soono.

Suryam se desh, ahankaar hai kabhu,
Naav di botishan, sui rakh dham.

Geli anchal, ahankaar humka,
Naav ke asar chewing, yogur lea rubara.

Moj noor, ahankaar nele,
Naav ke chanpati GRW.

Zamana rahat, ahankaar murru,
Naav po thhe, koosh nahk.

Shram ki sat, ahankaar chij gas',
Naav sap asmid ke wire.

Ek hi samaj, ahankaar acest,
Naarj navi ghula der.

Pani kaha, ahankaar betha,
Naav vein gend li pomey

Asha ki dhok, ahankaar car,
Naav phyayalini slot.

Buddhi ki likhne, ahankaar mop,
Naav par shikri uska hoston.

Jo roshni peeth ke, man ka andhera dhulta

Jab bhakti ka jal chadhe, hasti dhool bhi milti hai

Jab haath se bhare kavachu, maya ke rang jale,

Jhoota sukh dikhata hai, dharti ke sannate,

Maya ki chaadar odhi, gaon ki raat andhi,
Jo dhola se baitha, sukh ki bhainsi jhanke.

Mitti ka ghulna, saans le jaaye,
Maya ka rang girta, atma ko chhode bhaye.

Saagar ki lehron mein, dharti ka paani,
Maya ka jal bhare, chalta hai kahani.

Kumhar ki mithi chul, sadiyon ka chehra,
Maya ki roti par, dhool ka bhancha.

Jeevan ki patang, hawa se baandh,
Maya ki dhool se, rassi kabhi na band.

Jala hua diya, maya ka rang,
Lora hansne ki baat, buta usi sang.

Raat ki kali ghadi, khumari ka asar,
Maya chhadi aag, kal bhi roshni ka ghar.

Bhookh se bhare rakh, dharti ki paath,
Maya khinchti aabhi, anant ki baat.

Saans ka ghonta, maya ki lat,
Kumha ke haath se, patthar ko choon mat.

Mitti ka jhonka, bhari kankar ki,
Maya ki karwat, dhokha dikhaye dang.

Jag dhokha ka gaban, khokla si dhoop,
Maya ke sapan mein, sabhi rang roop.

Mitti bhari chhadi, dharti se taap,
Maya ki lehriyal se, aashiq ko aap.

Kali chadar mein, sulagt hai chhaina,
Maya ki bhatki dhara, poonch ko pilana.

Churi ka rang, maa ki kahani,
Maya ki bhunti mein, aankh se bhilani.

Rasmal kshetra mein, sookh ki jhadi,
Maya ka paath, dheere dhire nadi.

Mitti ka rang, bhanwar se dhik,
Maya ki chhaya ban, dhool bhul ki pich.

Jag koi diya, naash ki roshni,
Maya ki jholi mein, bhoolte hain khushi.

Talab ki baat, chaka ka roop,
Maya ke bhanwar mein, saap ko sabh khoop.

Mitti ke phool, karo dhun aalam,
Maya ki param, vishwa se ukhlaam.

Saawan ki phurti, jal se bhara,
Maya ki ghanti ghadi, ankho mein se jarra.

Kumbhar ki bhatti, andhiyara chhoda,
Maya ke daal se, dhool bhi ho soda.

Mitti ki khulha baje, rehte sab,
Maya ki murkhata se, dhurandhar rok.

Aashyu ki patang, raat ki dhun,
Maya ki sanje gayi, sekon sabhi gun.

Dhaaran ki chaudi, mitti ka coy,
Maya ki dhoop se, andheron ki choy.

Har pashu ki baat, dhyan ka base,
Maya ki katri roti, mann se upase.

Ujli hawayen, dharti ki chhiri,
Maya ki murcha, prakash ke sithi.

Kumbhar ke haath, bajaate rahe,
Maya ke jhooth se, dukh bhare rahe.

Bhole ke virohit, bhakti ke raag,
Maya ki talab main, zamir mein shag.

Mitti ka varna, dhool ka ashban,
Maya ki leela mein, angko rekan.

Brahma ki chadar, bhanwar ki,
Maya ka pul, murga ke sahar.

Talab ki sutli, parachhatri ki,
Maya ke patton se, bisri kintu sikh.

Jal ka jhoola, dharti ki pyas,
Maya ke heth hain, bhookh aur as.

Kumha ki kaas, chhai ki chhalang,
Maya ki sukh bhang, dhairy ko baang.

Mitti ki pooja, suvachik bhakti,
Maya ke dhoonde ko, bhaz, bhitar qhti.

Sankal karey, dhadha ke boond,
Maya ki lasa, antih sookh mund.

Bobbar ki bhatti, aaten ke pat,
Maya ke aangan mein, torsi num.

Bhaav ki madhur dhool, dharti ka ban,
Maya ki tej se, jeev lok bhaan.

Mitti ki yantr, dhare bhanwar ki,
Maya ke veda me, rang raoche niki.

Saag ke patte, raat ke dham,
Maya ki ling ko, paap ko dam.

Saadh ka andhera, jhoota maan,
Maya ki aag se, sukh bhoot gaan.

Raat ki nadi, peeri ke pool,
Maya ki pratigya se, agle aul.

Karvan ki vare, dhool ka baat,
Maya ki reet se, bhoolti hai raat.

Mitti ki jheel, dhokla ka khel,
Maya ke shikaar, ankhon ke nel.

Chilman ki bus, tulsi ki roshni,
Maya ko chheda, paap ka roshni.

Mitti ki dhoom, dhuwan ka paath,
Maya ki teekhi, man ko dhath.

Jharna ki khumari, jhooma veg,
Maya ki baajti, bekaar jag.

Diya ki raat, dhool ka ndīn,
Maya ke rang.. (continues)

Mann ki udan se jhoolta, pakshi ka pankh chhuta,
Satya ki paani mein dhoye, mann dhire dhire sukhuta.

Hans ki shaan se jo bata, apna mann bhi udaas,
Jab shoonya se mil jaaye, to aatam ka vishwaas.

Mann ka jhonka ghanera, pakshi ki udan chhoti,
Shanti ke pankh chune jab, to bhool jaati dhoti.

Hans ki nazar se jo dekh, mann ka badla dhale,
Aaradhna ki rekh mein hi, milti hai kaash chhode.

Mann ki murchna bhari, pakshi ki peedh niraal,
Antar ki shakti se hi, milta hai uska haal.

Hans ke pankh ki tarah, mann ki chanchal lahr,
Jab prabhu ki dhun suno, to baje uska sahar.

Mann ke baadal baandh ke, pakshi udaas ho jaaye,
Satya ka sur jab bhaje, to mann mein prakash aaye.

Hans ki sundarta ko, mann ke vilay se puch,
Yeh jeevan ke safar mein, milta hai anand vich.

Mann ka daldal re, pakshi ka sang laal,
Shabd dhyaan se nikal jaaye, to milti hai chaal.

Hans ka swar anokha, mann ke ghum ko mitaaye,
Jab dhyaan ki lehron mein, dharti se mil jaaye.

Mann ki gati roke jab, pakshi udan ki preet,
Yahi atma ki baat, jo sukh ko meet.

Hans ki poonch ko chhoote, mann ki har koi baat,
Satya ki reet me hi, milti hai vishraam ki raat.

Mann ki ashakti dhool, pakshi ke panktit se,
Jab bhakti ki dhun bajti, mann dhire dhire re.

Hans ki baat suno, mann ka krodh nahin,
Prem ki madhur dhara, apna le yeh man.

Mann ki baans ki jhin, pakshi ki taal se,
Jab bhakti ki dharan ho, to svarg ki baadal uthe.

Hans ki khoj mein jagah, mann ko dekh kar,
Satya ki alok me hi, shanti ka asar.

Mann ka gufa chhupa, pakshi ki awaaz pun,
Jab dhyan ka deep jale, to milti hai roshni.

Hans ki chaal dhire, mann ki bhool mita,
Bhakt pran se hi aati, anant sukh ki chhama.

Mann ki raat andhera, pakshi ka udaan rosh,
Jab prem ki dhun suno, to milti har subh.

Hans ki jeet samajh, mann ke bal le,
Satya ki chadar me hi, milti dharti pe.

Mann ki teeli uttar, pakshi ki leher,
Jab bhakti ka sagar bhare, to milti khair poor.

Hans ki man ki sanket, mann se dur na ho,
Jab dhyan ka deep jale, toh milti rah ki ro.

Mann ki dhara ke sahare, pakshi ki panka,
Dhyan ki vayu se hi, milti hai shanti ka sank.

Hans ki dhun ankho me, mann ka sukh bhi,
Jab bhakti ki lahr chale, to ho sabhi.

Mann ka sahara dena, pakshi roshan raah,
Satya ke charan mein hi, milti sabse chah.

Hans ki masti se mile, mann ka sath,
Jab prem ki baat ho, to bhool apni path.

Mann ki bhool gan on, pakshi chingari jo,
Shanti ki baat jab tujhe, milti nayi dhooni.

Hans ki talash ko, mann ki leher,
Jab satvic dhyan ho, to milti rosh.

Mann ki dhund dhoop, pakshi sang mil,
Satya ke jankaar se, milti vishwaas ki v?

Hans ki pehchaan, mann ki chahat,
Jab bhakti ki roshni, se mett nan?

Mann ki aagnik rosh, pakshi ki aan,
Jab prem ki baat ho, to sab milhan.

Hans ki dhenu se man, dhuau ji sapan,
Satya ka rang bhara, milti sukh ki dhyan.

Mann ki jaldi, pakshi ki udan,
Sham dhoop mein dharti, milti charan.

Hans ke dharohar se man, jhuka,
Jab bhakti ki roos, to poon.

Mann ki flags, pakshi ud,
Satguru ki bari, mil man ka suk.

Hans ki tehal se, mann ki sani,
Jab dhyan ki shuruaat, to mil shagun.

Mann ke sahare, pakshi ki awaaz,
Satya ki roshn, milti aadi.

Hans ki kahani, mann ki poori,
Jab bhakti ki beti, milti sukh se boori.

Mann par bhari, pakshi laga spin,
Satya ka saja, milti raah ka din.

Hans ki mala, mann ki dhun,
Jab bhakti ki geet, mil ke mana.

Mann aur pakshi, na chhodo to,
Satya ke baad so, mil prabhat ko.

Hans ki aarzoo, mann ki piet,
Jab bhaktan ki baat, milti shanti.

Mann ki shraap, pakshi ki ghos,
Guru ki baat sun, milti aash.

Hans ki baat dhyan, mann ki dhara,
Jab bharat ki raah, milti hita.

Mann ka dhara, pakshi ki nadi,
Satya ki raahe, milti swasth.

Hans ki lehare, mann ke gaon,
Jab bhakti ki jhoom, milti shyam.

Mann ki jal, pakshi ki sitare,
Satya ki baat san, milti pral.

Hans ki chadar, mann ki sunehri,
Jab bhakti ki talash, milti nij.

Mann dharti se, pakshi ko chur,
Satya ke buland, milti sukh.

Hans ki leher, mann ki dhun,
Jab prabhu ki nadi, mile the.

Mann ka gau, pakshi ki jhal,
Satya ki nagri, milti kal.

Hans ki lekh, mann ki kirn,
Jab bhakti ki aasha, milti din.

Mann ki nadi, pakshi uda,
Satya ke rishte, milti gl.

Guru bina manushya boond jaisa,
Jinke sharan mein milti roshni chhoot nahi.

Moti bhanr koni milata samundar,
Guru bila milti sirf ashobh raatar.

Guru ka charan dharan se, andhera chhoota,
Jag ke andhar bhi milti roshni ka jhoota.

Koi sharmata nahi milti mooti,
Jab guru ki seekh ho pichle pooti.

Guru ki bakshish se banta hai gyaan,
Ankhon ki aashna se milti anoot ryaan.

Moti ke bhanr jaisa wo guru,
Samasya ke samundar mein mile sapna gulu.

Guru bin dhool se bhi pyaara,
Jab mil jaye to bonta hai pyara.

Kaisi bhi thi vyatha ki raah,
Guru aata hai, bunder phir koi khoj na haah.

Guru ke darshan se hoti sankat,
Moti pe khade ho, dharan ka jhad.

Guru ke shabd se toot jati dharm,
Moti ki talash mein nathi ghoint karam.

Guru aani samayik roop se,
Moti ki ankho main rang sab roop se.

Guru ki soorat milti prabha,
Moti ke jaise jaise arman dhoba.

Guru se samarit jiv har sah,
Moti ka sahara, punj ka kadm.

Guru ka ashirwad milne se,
Seep ki tarah bhitra jodash ke chhe.

Guru charan rake, bhatka na koi,
Moti saar ko dekh sot ko bhi.

Guru ke samarpan se hoti bal,
Moti ke dhara baghti kal.

Guru ki stuti ka gungun,
Moti ki soja bilau.

Guru ka anugrahan bhasha,
Moti ke sanket ki shabda.

Guru aata bana ae deep,
Moti ki ghata ban jaati reep.

Guru bina sun nahi milataa,
Moti ke tutne se doosa niraataa.

Guru ka vatsa ka jivan,
Moti kood bhala aakri asan.

Guru se dhyaayen ant main jale,
Moti ki tarah khilahat poore bhale.

Guru ki baat mile jharna,
Moti se duniya sab bhur vara.

Guru ko choona hove bhalwa,
Moti ane, aapni kavaal ka dhala.

Guru ka sharaab piye devo,
Moti phool udat ma akhav dav.

Guru ki chaap mein teen udaan,
Moti ka jhoole se asmaan.

Guru dhundla asphaal,
Moti ka shirkhoon savaa vaa

Guru ki preet jhula,
Moti ke paani se nayi dutka.

Guru ke bin dankaaj kho,
Moti kadah pathar kevay.

Guru yaad raho man se,
Moti ki nadya bhi aav se.

Guru ko prabhat, amrit, laalan,
Moti ki dwani daakinga chelan.

Guru ki milti mamata,
Moti baaba bhogi bhara.

Guru ke jaisa koi ka tei,
Moti ke sach yaa shri.

Raat ki chadar pe jo apna garv suuta,
Subah ki kiran hi usse dhool mitata.

Andhera andhar ko angdaai le aata,
Jab ahankar ki mote baal dhool mein baith jaata.

Choti si chatri samjhi vo chaand ko apna,
Dhawal sooraj aaya to chhatri ka rang uda.

Din ki dhool se nikli raat ki baat,
Jo na samjhe, pakd le apni anjaani khat.

Savere ki poonchh pe jo bhav ki dhool,
Usey ehsaas hi nahin ki uska saanjh ka fool.

Raat ka sarkash roshni ko de mar,
Jab apna aap ko bade samjhe yaar.

Chand ki roshni ghul jaati har hithaab,
Jab ahankar ki dhool se kare woh zaab.

Uttari hawaa ko bhi ghoor ke ghoor,
Aapna kaam karo, bhool na kar koi choor.

Ujala ki kheti mein hi beech khoj,
Mitti mein bhool ja egam ke saaj.

Mitti ki mitti poochti apna rang,
Jab dil ko naidaan se milti bhang.

Savera ka talwar kaisa bhare bahar,
Jab ahankaar se sab raat ki anaar.

Raat ka paimana bhar le hoshiyar,
Aapna pet se sidha dhokha chhvaakar.

Chhati ke kinare dhoolon se rehna,
Jab jagat ki raah mein hum jan'na.

Dhoop ki laali ko na samjho chhost,
Andha dhundhla bol, ahankar ka khandar host.

Mere ghoosa ka paani to aankhon se dhoka,
Jab atma ko darr se dhare jodo jho.

Mitti ki baat aise chadh kar jaati,
Jab khud ko sabse bada samjhe raat badi gaati.

Raat ki ghadi pighalti uthonka,
Taj mahal ke pinhe se anjaane rooth.

Jab dimag se bajti deriyaji,
Bhooti dugdi roop se bhasht.

Nadi ke gahare mein dhool ka rang,
Jab aatman ki kaayam na ban jaye sang.

Paani ki baat paani se badi,
Jab anahuti se bhara ghamand ki.

Asta ki rehmati baaje dhoop me,
Kis darod ko newae chauraha ki.

Dhooli roshni aaj ka antadii,
Jab beejna khil nhi aapka.

Raat ki magaj dharati se lagti,
Jab ahankaar ko itna hi samga mein.

Sugandh ki hawa ko utha,
Jab nirankar apsah ka virudh.

Jhilmil bade raat ke paadu,
Apna anupasa hee chhadi.

Shanti ki dhup mein hum karte rui:
Jab ahankaar denge daras ki kati.

Samay ke baadal gire, chaand bhi raat ko bhaye
Jo na samjhe pal ki baat, voh hona hi gaye

Suraj ki roshni jaisi, aaj se kal ho andhera
Jin ne samaya sambhala, unka hi dharohar tera

Kheti ke khet mein, fasal bhugatati samay ki reet
Dheere-dheere kat jaati, jo na hoye ankit peet

Samay ke haathon mein, sabhi rang ho rup

Kagaar ki mulakat, waqt ke sawal ka jawaab
Jo pal ko na samjhe, sadiyon se kare aab

Chaand ki kirna dhundhli, andhera bhi gaaye
Samay jab chhuta haath, na koi aasan bhaye

Suraj ke dhup se, jalti hai dhool ki jhal

Jab haath mein chhote, kaun badhe savat

Jo na rok sake dhara, woh hi asla jale

Mitti ki hifazat ki, din raat ka khandar
Samay jab banta dar, dharam ka bartar

Jo samjha samay ka paya, wo hi gyaan paye

Patang ki dor, samay ki patang seeh
Jagi na chhutti, yar baadhti reh

Chiriya ki sukh batti, samay ka kotha bana
Kanwal ki raat, sukh ka laga panna

Khul gaye nagar ki kimat, jo samay ki ghati

Saaf jo ho jaaye, tabhi prakash kohra chhodey.

Saans le man ki shakti ko, jaise paani se darpan,
Jab gili ho jaye to chhupa gyan ka sapna.

Bichhoṛe jo andhera, roshan ho jaata pyara.

Mann ki safai se mil jaye, param satya savera.

Jab usmein sach ka ujala, to na ho koi bhaye.

Jitni jaane na ho, utni saathi bhakti.

Mann ko daande se mil, na ho sapna bhaal.

Phir bhi dharti se jude rahoon, haahar raah.

Mann ko hai saath hi satya, jo ho kus tar.

Badar Ghir Aawe Gagan Par, Jhar Jhar Paani Barsaaye
Mann Barasat Te Bacha Raha, Naam Ki Oat Lagaaye

Mann Mor Na Naache Re, Maayavi Pankh Failaaye
Naache Jo Hari Ke Dwaare, Taahi Shobha Paaye

Sejiya Pe Mann Na Sove, Chaar Sau Jaag Jaaye
Jabase Paaya Saadhu Sang, Tabase Chain Aaye

Panchhi Jyu Mann Ud Jaawe, Khojat Phirat Bipaaye
Prem Ki Dori Tut Gayi, Taahi Kaal Ghere Aaye

Bheetar Jo Barsat Hoi Hai, Taahi Agan Bujhaawe
Baahar Megh Garjat Hai, Mann Paani Naa Paawe

Mann Ka Kuaan Gaadhat Hai, Paani Laagat Door
Saadhu Rassi Lagaai Ke, Nikale Madhur Neer

Bijuri Badal Mein Chamki, Mann Aasha Jagaaye
Ek Pal Ki Jyoti Dekhat, Maaya Jaal Samaaye

Kabira Mann Ek Raavan Hai, Das Sir Uthai
Naam Ke Bhaan Se Mare Te, Nahin Aur Upaai

Mann Nadiya Ke Jhaag Jyu, Umath Umath Samaaye
Haathon Lo Na Paakariye, Chhune Te Yeh Tute Jaaye

Maati Ka Kaancha Mann Hai, Saans Laagat Sajaaye
Aag Bina Pakka Na Hoi, Dhool Mein Mil Jaaye

Baadal Garjat Paani Barsat, Mann Garjat Kachhu Naa Paawe
Jihi Mann Ki Barsat Bhayi, Tin Sada Sukh Paawe

Mann Haansani Bina Pankh Ki, Talab Mein Bhramat Jaaye
Guru Ke Shabd Ke Pankh Mile, To Aakaash Udaaye

Sab Ghadi Mann Badalat Hai, Ek Pal Ek Suraat
Prem Ki Doraa Jo Bandhiya, Bhayo Sada Ik Jaat

Mahal Banaaya Mann Ne, Tinke Tinke Thaaye
Pavan Ke Jhonke Aawat Hi, Sab Dhool Mein Milaaye

Kahat Kabir Suno Bhayi Sa, Mann Ko Na Bisaraaye
Mann Ke Dush Mann Hi Kahaun, Aur Nahin Upaaye

Andhiyaare Badal Chhaye Hain, Diya Jala Lo Bhaai
Surat Jyu Baati Rakhi Te, Paap Na Andar Aave

Mann Makadi Ke Jaal Jyu, Laage Apne Haaye
Apan Hi Jaal Mein Phansa Ke, Paachhe Pachhitaaye

Chaar Sau Badal Chha Gaye, Mann Ghulaam Hua Jaaye
Naam Ke Tej Ugg Aaye, To Megh Door Bhaagaaye

Seep Mein Moti Soya Hai, Seep Samajh Na Paayi

Sapne Mein Sukh Dukh Dekha, Aankh Khule Mithya Paayi

Maya Mein Uljha Jeev To, Ho Gaya Kangaal

Makri Jaal Buna Rahe, Pankhi Usme Aave
Maya Ke Jaal Vishaal Mein, Jeev Sahaj Na Paave

Badal poochhe na kahu ki jaat, barsat lagi sab khet
Pandit poochhe kul aur got, man ki mail na met

Garaje badal barsat nahi, jhoothi ghamand ki maala
Pandit paddhat padhe rahe, manuva jaise kaala

Khetan mein badal barase, chaah aur taal bharoy
Man mein jo prem na barase, so jaat ka bharam na khoy

Sabai khetan barsat ek, upjai sabai anaaj
Pandit apanai jaat mein, jhootho kare gaaj

Barsaat mein sab bheej gaye, Brahman bheejaa chamaar
Tilak lep sab dhul gaye, bheejhe sab sansaar

Baadal barase taal sarovar, paapi punit bharoy
Pandit bhandara bandhe rahe, pyaasa jo piya na hoy

Kuen mein baadal barasai, koyal peekat paani
Pandit jaat bataai ke, bich bichhare praani

Megh barase sab khetan mein, kahu na rookhe maahi
Pandit kahu na maanai jo, neech kahai sab jaahi

Megh barase angiyara par, bujhat lagi taahi
Pandit pakhand jare na jo, antar aag jaahi

Bheejhat baadal upjai phasal, sab khetan ek samaan
Pandit apnai jaat mein, kare ati abhimaan

Baadal megh barase bhari, sab khetan mein sukh
Pandit jaat mein bharose, man mein khara dukh

Ghar ghar mein badal barasai, sabahi kahu na chhed
Pandit jaat na chhorai jo, so janm janm ka bhed

Aakaash mein megh udaya, barasai sabai paasa
Pandit ek paasa maanai, so jaat ka phaansa

Nirmal badal gagana ke, jal nirmal sab dhaar
Pandit tilak taja na man, manuva maila bhar

Baadal ghuma chaaron ore, sab kuen talai bharoy
Pandit ore ek pakarai, aurahi ko ujaroy

Badal garaje barsat hai, khetan bharai anaaj
Pandit garaje paddhat mein, bhari bhari laaya saaz

Gagara mein baadal barase, jaame purai paani
Pandit gagariya mein bhari, jhoothi jaat kahaani

Barase badal sab hariyala, oonch neech samaan
Pandit jahaan na barase so, sookha so jaat gyaan

Baadal barase sabahi te, maila kahu na koye
Pandit aapan te paavak, doojan ka maila hoye

Megh dharai sabahi kahu, dhoi leye bigaari
Pandit aapan jaat dhari, bich bichhaare saari

Mandir mein diya baahar hai, andhiyara ghar maahi
Pandit dekhat deepak ko, aap andhiyara paahi

Ganga jal sip karat hai, man mein bhara krodh
Kahai Kabir aisa ko, paap keenho na chhod

Jo pandit pade pustaka, soi pandit naahi
Jin prem ka gyaan nahi, pandit kahai kaahi

Astar dhoye tilak karai, pooja kare dina raat
Antar maila na chhude jo, saafai kahan ki baat

Kaaya kaagad mann leep, chit chhabi likh naam
Kahai Kabir chit maila, likha jhootha kaam

Chakki ne dekh daal ki, oonch na neech banaai
Sabahi ko ek dharai, phir nichor lai jaai

Jaise til til ka tel nikare, sab mein wahi samaai
Vaise sab mein Ram nikare, jaat na kahu bataai

Pandit shastra parhai rahe, maanai gyaan nihaal
Kahai Kabir prem bina, mukut sir par kaal

Pandit pooja kare mandir, chhati pe tilak dhaari
Kahai Kabir paakhanda, jeev chaureasi jaari

Diye ki lau uupar hai, nicha tel bataai
Kahai Kabir aisa pandit, sansaar mein bahut paai

Pandit paddhat mein atake, svarna mukut sir dhaar
Kahai Kabir jahattai, antar narak sansaar

Naam liye mukh se jo, man mein maila paat
Kahai Kabir naam bina, so jaata narak ghaat

Pandit sab kahu sikhaave, aap na paar utare
Kahai Kabir aisa ko, jhoothi paddhat saare

Shivaling puja kare, tirath barat nitaai
Kahai Kabir man maila, kaahne lep lagaai

Saaton dweep navai kari, saagar tel lagaai
Kahai Kabir man maila, paap naahi chhudaai

Ganga tan ka paani hai, man maila ganga teer
Kahai Kabir man maila, na paai nija neer

Naiyya paar karu jo chaahu, prem binu kya hoy
Kahai Kabir paakhand te, utare naahi koye

Paakhand ki potariya, sir par lai sawaar
Kahai Kabir aisa ko, laagai narak dwaar

Stree purush ek saar hai, jyun chingaari ang
Kahai Kabir jo bhed kare, so laagai paakhand rang

Chamar chakari karai jo, Brahman thaan tajaaye
Kahai Kabir oonch neech, dono ek samaaye

Jaat ka bhaaram sir par, dehure par dolaye
Kahai Kabir maila man, dhoi na sake ko aaye

Ooncha maanai oonchi gati, neecha maanai naahi
Kahai Kabir jo maanai so, chourasi gati jaahi

Guru ko kehat deohra, chela kahu na cheet
Kahai Kabir aisa ko, dhoondhat baahar preet

Janau lai pandit phire, gyaan kahu na paaye
Kahai Kabir aisa ko, janau aag lagaaye

Pandit apnai kul banaai, auran ko nivaare
Kahai Kabir aisa te, sansaar se haare

Maanai aapan ooncha ko, dekh auran ko neech
Kahai Kabir manuva mein, basai paakhand beech

Ache dharm ke naam pe, lakhon ko mar daal
Kahai Kabir dharm hai kya, jihva par jhoothi chaal

Mandir masjid bhed ko, jo mann mein thikaana
Kahai Kabir aisa man, phire narak ka jaana

Dhan dekhi aapan ooncha, daridra neech janaa
Kahai Kabir dono mein, Ram ek samaana

Jaat na poochho saadhu ki, poochho lijai gyaan
Mol karo talvaar ka, padi kyonkar maan

Man se jise dhoonde, so satgur ke sang chalta
Phool vi ho karaan, kaanta vi uska saath laalta

Jab mann dhool mein mil jaaye, to rachna ka raag sun
Sadhu ki baat sun, dharti pe chutki phir san

Sang me baith kar jab kabir bole, andar ki garmi dhula
Phool ki sugandh se, kaanta ko bhi mil jaaye jula

Har charan dharo jo dhool ko, makkhan mein milata mil
Sadhu ki baat me hi, man ka daanval chhil

Karat bhakti ki roop dharti, jab phool se phir vishwa su
Sangat ka panjrah, kaanta ko bhi banata du

Kavita ki dhara, satgur ki baat se rehti
Phool ki jad, kaanta ki haad, sahi camel me seethi

Hari ki baat ko sunte hi, man ki dhool tali
Sangat ke bina na koi, phool ko milti jhuli

Jab sukh ki bukhar jagti, to sangh ki muskan mil
Phool sang kaanta, hanikaar sandhye riyal

Jivan ka phool khila hai, jala re khadi ho dharti
Sadhu ki shiksha mein hi, kaanta bepadti bharti

Har saans ka svapna, sang satguru ke pyara
Phool ke bagiche me, kaanta bhi pyaara

Sangh ko dekh kar dekho, man ki dhool nayaab
Kabir ki bhajan, phool ke hue samad

Mitti ke paad bhi, jug se fank chhedu jaye
Sadhu ki sangati, phool jaye baandh thaye

Badi josh se jab dhun ho, to man ke ras milta
Sangat ka paimana, phool se ghunghra sita

Sukoon ki chal, jab satguru ki baat mil
Phool bhi gunde, kaanta bhi bhair jaise mil

Satguru ki asar se, man ki bhav bhari jaye
Phangar ki dhara, phool aur kaanta sath jaye

Sangati ke charan, har lamha ke pyar
Phool ka rang bhi, kaanta ki anwaar

Satgur ki upaasna, man hi mann ki dhool
Phool ki lachhan, kaanta ka roop plant cool

Kharaab man ki baat, sangh se bekaral jaye
Phool pachaar se, kaanta ka tur sang jaye

Jab satguru ki chikha, man ke churak beghar
Phool khushbu ho jaye, kaanta bhi sahaj bhar

Jeevan ka phool dhare, jag khuadi aage bhari
Sadho ki sangati, jagaati hai kaanta ki khari

Satguru ki harek baat, man ki nadi ko bekar
Phool vich do ulhaar, kaanta le flagan har

Sangat se man jale, dhool aakash dhula
Phool se behard maangi, kaanta bhi saam bhandula

Mandir ki baat, na koi dhool, na koi raso
Satguru ki dhun, phool pyaar se baaksho

Pran ki rida, satguru ke sang, dhosh se bhare
Phool se padhi, kaanta bhi, gyan ki lehar

Man ki vibhag, satgur ki baat se khul
Phool ke jhadu, kaanta se mil sunam gul

Sadhkār ke pyare sangati, phool ki aankhon mein lo
Kaanta bhi chhuta, darshan ki Ganga bhaj lo

Dekh vriksh ka phool, gaav ki dhool minghe
Satgur ki baat, kaanta bhi mil ma laaye

Raat ki shudh gagan, satguru se mile dhool
Phool ki barish, kaanta se lafz ful

Jab man ki basti udti, satguru ki pahchaan
Phool ke suneche, kaanta ki sair aasaan

Nadi ki dhul, satguru ki baat karaat
Phool ki lehr, kaanta ki kamal dharat

Sang me paise ka rang nahin, man ki sach me dharti
Phool se bhari, kaanta bhi pyaar ghoorti

Satguru ki baat me shanti, man ki dhool dhire noon
Phool ko chhoone, kaanta dhuli pe footon

Jab asli sangat ka rang, man me roshni jale
Phool bansi ke piche, kaanta bhi aabale

Sarali dhool aur satguru hai mil
Phool ki sukh se dhare, kaanta ka sil

Sangat ki svar, man ki chhaya mil jo
Phool ki bhakti, kaanta ki raj bhaj po

Dhoop aur chaand ki baat, sadhu ki drishti se
Phool ho jaaye, kaanta bhi mil sutri se

Satgur ki mithi baat, man ki saral dhool
Phool ki basy, kaanta ki raaj bhul

Man ki choti khilti, satgur ki antahi sang
Phool aur kaanta, sab rang bhari bang

Sang se dhool uda jaye, man ki sade ki bhanti
Phool ka dhvani, kaanta ki pant sween

Sant ki baat ho, man ki dhool chhu jaaye bright
Phool ki nadi, kaanta ki chirga sahr kalight

Jeevan ki dharti, satgur ke sahare palt
Phool se dhul, kaanta bhi mil ikat

Satguru ke milan me, man ke jam ke jhar
Phool ke gulshan, kaanta ki jhalar

Sang ke raag, man ki dhool ko bhaag le
Phool ki sukh, kaanta ki laabh me aag le

Saans ki zeher, satguru ki awaz thod
Phool ki bharm, kaanta shosh, gagan ode

Satguru ki baat se, man ka aatan dhool
Phool se maang, kaanta ki khatir shool

Mitti ke chilke, satguru ki mal jam
Phool ki umang, kaanta bhi jokha dhyan

Ras ki baat sang mein, man ki sach inhe jaye
Phool ki gol, kaanta ki antar le bhaye

Sadhu ki baat dhul, man ki jee jaye gan
Phool ki poori, kaanta se mil inki karan

Satguru ki panchhi, man ko leke aati
Phool ko rang, kaanta kare baati

Apne mann ki rait, satguru ki baat dhulan
Phool ke satra, kaanta bhi sahi sudhan

Sangat ki jhalak, man ka lehar ke bani
Phool ki bahar, kaanta ki titli bani

Satguru ke bhajan, mann ki shakti bhare
Phool ki mayur, kaanta ki gudiya tare

Jab man dharm ka dhool, satguru ki kanti
Phool ke phool, kaanta ki bhakti shanti

Man ki vatika, satgur ki baat aage
Phool ke sukhi, kaanta ke daagi naage

Satguru ki baat, vishwa ki khadi palm
Phool ki dana, kaanta ki harek dhoom

Har samay sangat milp, man ki dhool se posh
Phool ke rang se, kaanta ki dhara khoosh

Satguru ki baat se, man ki jeev lungi
Phool me khilna, kaanta se mil hues

Man ki zuqat, satguru ki baat se aadi
Phool ka nirmal, kaanta bhi rohn ki baadi

Sangat mil apne, man ki dhoop ki dhool
Phool bhi pyaara, kaanta ki saboot asool

Satguru ki chhanvi, man ki ptal se bhari
Phool ki dhara, kaanta ki preet sahi

Jab dhool se mann uchhal, satguru ka roop banta
Phool ki rekh, kaanta ka geet hota

Satguru ki baat, dhul jale man ki zindagi
Phool ka anurag, kaanta ki yan

Bhikhari ke haath mein sona na jata, jo bhakt ke roop se dhukhta hai
Kasauti se nahin, dil ki sachchai se shudhh hota, dharma ka rang dhukhta hai

Riti‑riwaz ki moorti, rang birangi phoolon ki mala
Jab tak mann mein na ho sada, woh bhi ek dhokha‑dala

Jat‑jati ke bhushan pehne log, man mein dhool ka avastha
Kothi ki chadri bina gyaan ke, ashri tapasya ka nasha

Mandir ke lohe ki ghanti, dil ke dhadkan se jab baat bhi na kare
Tabhi to bhakti ki jhalak, andhera hi andhera se bechare

Sona bechne wala bhi, kasauti ko bhool jaata hai
Jo bechta apni atma ko, uski kimat kabhi na aati

Rang‑birangi pooja‑pandal, khaali haath se bhare bhandar
Satya ki dhool hi rakhte, ghumraah sadiyon ka jahar

Khaas dharm‑guru ne jaise, dikhaye apna hi karat
Par aatma ki dhool machi, husn ko kiye har barat

Chadar ke piche chhupi, bhakti ki baat na kahna
Jab tak dhool bhari rahe, tasveer koi nayana

Dhan ki thali mein bhakton ko, bhagwan ka swad milta nahi
Jal‑jal sehri mein dharm ko, oonchi chadar ki padi

Kajal ki kankari hain jo, dharm ki ankahi kahani
Jab dard se bhara man, usko hi khabar nahi maani

Sona ki bhavya ghadi, dharam ki ghadi pe chhupi
Kasauti ka rang na jaane, patang se uttha koi gupi

Kapaas ki chadar dharan, dharti ko maange na shor
Kabira ke padhur rang, sahas ka hai manav dhoor

Dhoop ki chaudhri pe, bijli ki kaal ke beech
Jhog se nikli bhakti ko, dhoop nadi se milke

Nakli saiyaan ki dhun, dharm ki koi chaal na jaye
Satya ki bahar hi kahe, jab bhakti pyar se bhare

Kasauti ka sona, dharm ki sanghati pe nadi
Jab ishq kam ho to, rang ko dhoya na jake

Rang‑biraange ghunghat, aatma ki farmaa ko na lag
Sukoon ki manzil sirf shabd nahi, man ke ek bhaag

Mitti ke bartan mein, sabko bhakta ka kura
Jab se jalaate hain jeevan, ankaha hai use vura

Jai ho wo pujari, jo jhambhaadal ki poonch ho
Para mera bhool jaaye, bhakti ka rang khulne

Nadi ke kinare ka dal, dharm ki dhul ki chi
Kasauti ki silvat, kimat kam shor na laye

Mitti mein chaandni, kalaab ki fasal virodh
Jo roti ke bartan mein, bhakti ka maati pe thod

Kanpur ki galiyon mein, dharm ka balam na chheda
Ghum ki mitti mein raja, kasauti ki rakhe unka vega

Baat makin ki, jo rahe, bhakti ka soa hi jata
Dohra se pese bharte, dharm ki kashin satha

Jung ka balma, jo bhool jata, dharm ki bandook ki dhan
KHadi me baithi tadh ke to bhakti kheti, dharti dhona phir

Gajra ki surang, kendra me sab gyan ke neecha
Kasauti ki sikhi, vo tathe ki sindur ye tascha

Sona ke alaakhan, dharm ki jhappi ke patang
Jab jhali na bhakti, to dhulam na rakhna ganj

Sona ki chhap, mukht ka dhara, utna hi aanga kahin chupa
Jab dhun likhi jaaye dhir, to dharm ke kal se pooch

Bharta ki bhavya, jeevan ke phool jo bhari dhun
Kasauti kuch na kare, sadhna ki hoon chhanam

Riti‑riwaj ki dhool se, utte asur kis ke sikhne

Jab dhyaan ki gati, gali mein aise roome

Sut ka rahasya, milta nahi baat

Sut ke sang milke, milta sukh reet

Kumbhar kholta ghada, dharm na ho to bhakti bhai.

Jhoothi pooja ki dhuaan, in sab ko moshikal,

Jati ke patte fal, rama ke riti ki baar,
Kumbhar ki matti se, sab ka bhanwar bekaar.

Rang biranga vastra, dharm ki naazuk chadar,
Mitti ke ghaare mein hi, sach ka chashma mildar.

Jab charkha dhare dhula, to aatma ka rang ful.

Sapno ki rekhon ko tod, milti hai anka peala.

Aao mil kar sang sakho, jaisa shankh dhun sunaye,
Chakri pe jiya chalaye, man ki khopdi theke.

Jab sat sang milti hai, to jhooth ki palki girti,
Sut ka thread dhaage, maa ki baat dharne lagti.

Sadhu sang me bavrai, man ki chulha kata,
Charkha ki ghoor se, sukh ki dhool baata.

Mitti ki chakri ghume, to bhakti ka rang bhara,
Sang sang sab mile, anant gagan ka sahara.

Sang milan se jhooth na rahe, satya ki reet pakdi,
Charkha ki chaal se, mann ka rang khilti.

Guru ke aangan me, charkha chalti reh jaye,
Sut ki har ek dhaga, atma ko mukti daye.

Mitti ki murti ko, jaise sut se bundein,
Sadhu ki sangat me, khul jati sab gundain.

Charkha ki ghanti baje, jab sema mein milti hai,
Sang sang milke hum, apradh se biche chhati.

Sadhu ki baat ka sut, samay ka dhaga ghoome,
Jo sang dhare sat, wohi dhool se jhoome.

Mann ki chakri ghoome, jaise baazu ka ghoomn,
Sadhu ke sang se mil, sab rang milke jhoom.

Guru ki baat mein sut, dhoti ki gol chadar,
Sang milte hi dharti, badalti  asar.

Dehleez ka darwaza, jab gur ki sangat khuli,
Charkha roti milti, sukh ki roshni badi.

Gunj ki baat se tuti, sat ki reet banti,
Charkha ki dhaga se, andheriyaan nanti.

Paath ka sut aaj bhi, ghoome dharti par,
Sadhu ki sangat se, milti tapti manzar.

Sath chalne ki charkhi, jab ladhte hain dukh,
Guru ke rang me sab, nayi subah ko jhuk.

Mann ke taare khilte, jab sat rang bhata,
Sadhu ki sangat se, sukh ki baali kata.

Charkha ki chadar pe, dhadapteri milti,
Sat sang milne se, anand ka shashmi.

Mitti ka sut hai tu, charkha ki shakti,
Sadhu sang ki dhun me, man obh alangi.

Jo sut liya satta, man ki dhool se hata,
Sang milkar phirein, charkha ki taht bhata.

Guru ki aandhi chalti, sut dil ki hamesha,
Bhakti ki charkhi sang, aatma ko mil game.

Charkhi ka sut buniyaad, tatti ka andhera,
Sat sang mil to milti, prakash ki pahara.

Sang ke aangan me, charkha ka chalna,
Man ki dhoop se bhari, tan koi bhi bhula.

Guru ki baat se, sut ghoomti le,
Sang me sadhu ke, aashra milti the.

Aapno sang, charkha ghoomein, man ke gordh,
Shabd se satya ki, sut sadho ki pordh.

Jab bhikshuk sang milte, reet ki charkhi chalti,
Sut ke asmaan se, dhool ki leet badhati.

Sat sang ka sut, dhool ka pravah,
Guru ki shabdon se, man ki dhun majah.

Charkha ke ghumte, man ka niyom parha,
Sadhu ki dhun se, bhav ka sant aha.

Sab satra ki baat, charkha ki ghoor me,
Sadhu ki sangat se, anjaane milte roop.

Ghumna sut ka rasta, jab guru ki dhoop,
Man ki chaal sab, aphurti se thaap.

Guru ki baat ke sut, humro charkha keeja,
Sadhu sada sang se, khushboo josh mein aja.

Mann ki sut li tho, jogi ki charkhi,
Sat rang se bhari, jannat ki bhal.

Sadhu ki acar se, sadari ke sut chhod,
Charkhi ki matti me milti, param sitar.

Mitti ki rag satra, dhool ki charkhi,
Sat rang ki baat se, man ki khabar bhkhi.

Charkhi se chalti sab bhavana,
Sat sang milte hi dharti se anjana.

Guru ka sut baadal, man ki dhuniya,
Sadhu sang ki aaj bhi hamein jaha.

Charkhi ka zaam, noor ki reet,
Sat sang mil ke pha, roshni se bhweek.

Sang ke maidan me, charkh ki dhool,
Sat shabad se sukh ki baat dhool.

Mann ki dhool ghoometer, jab sut samajh,
Sadhu sang ka sath, kul mil raja.

Kavita ki dhool, charkh hi sut,
Sat sang mil ke, jannat ki fut.

Guru ki dhuno, sut jalti,
Sadhu sang se harka, roti pul

Charkha ghume man, sut ki gaari,
Sat rang sang ra, dhool se banti.

Mitti ka aakash, charkha ka dhool,
Sat sang mein adho, sukh ki aiful.

Guru ki baat ke sut, man raaj,
Sadhu sang ki baatein, charkha ko thaj.

Ankhon ki charkhi, sut ki barki,
Sat sang se mithas, sab raat ki ghoori.

Man ki sukhi aag, jab chutri ki charkha,
Sat sang ki mange, sukh se bhari akar.

Sadhu sang charkha, patang ki baaj,
Sat sut ki dhaar, mann ko bhal jilij.

Guru ke väda, sut se ki aank,
Sang ke josh se, charkh chal baja.

Aarti ki sut, charkha ke pan,
Sat sang mil kar, kalpathi ka man.

Mann ki bhadi nadi, jab dhar dhara dhar,
Saahil na dekh paga, dhoop se baras bar.

Jab mann ko rok le sooraj ki baat,
Toh jalti hui dhuaan, nadi me saath.

Mann se jab pyas bujhe, jal moti milti,
Gadar ki lehar tairti, dhalki na bhakti.

Mann ka talab sada, paani ka bhivandan,
Jo dhare to dekh le, oobha mein anand.

Gagan ki barish, mann ki toofaan,
Nadi behati shanti, jab pehchan daan.

Mann ka baraabar, taalupe ki leher,
Jab shant ho alag, samundar ho sunder.

Mann ki baat, dharti ki chhal,
Jab dhushk lauta, to pyaar ka sthal.

Mann ki tarah baher, jab sampati aankh,
Nadi ke sang milke, aangan milate dhakh.

Mann ke beej se, paani ki dharti,
Bina anand ke, koi bhi bandhi nahi.

Mann ko dhara dhoop, samundar ki dhun,
Sukh ki lehraye, jab mil jaye suntan.

Mann ki chhal, nadi ki lehar,
Milke bhajaye, bhav ko ubhar.

Mann ka sang, samundar ke base,
Jab dhare jhanjhat, tarka hota sahse.

Mann ko shaant kare, paani ki thorn,
Man ki ghan mehekti, baadal bhi jhoor.

Mann ki sanjeevani, nadi ke jhilmil,
Har dhadkan bajti, shunya se mil.

Mann ke visham, sahil ki tilak,
Jab samundar aata, jagat ki kimat.

Mann ki aankh, dhara ki shoonya,
Jab milti nadi, milti poornata.

Mann ki umang, paani ki mehka,
Mukt ho gaya gagan, khagola ke cheka.

Mann qudrat ki boond, nadi ki dor,
Jab dhar se bhare, milti poorn noor.

Mann ko bhool jao, samundar ki baat,
Jab badal rahe, aap hi raaz.

Mann ki dhara, ghode ka ram,
Mitti ka ghola, nadi se dhoom.

Mann ko sookhi samajh, paani ki chahi,
Mann ke sahare milte, nadi ke rang.

Mann ka baadal, nadi ka hal,
Jab dhulkap raat, to ghanti nahi dhare.

Mann ke gaane, sagar ke leher,
Sukh ki ladi, jhapti bhi jeher.

Mann ka pal, naram paani ka,
Jab beh gaana, na chhute jara.

Mann ki bhatti, sarovara ke chal,
Mitti aur paani, dono milte tal.

Mann ki raat, nadi ka pichla,
Jab manaye sukh, aayi yeh suprala.

Mann ki ghanti, samundar ki sog,
Jab suno dhar, na paye koi rog.

Mann ke ghan, nadi ka shehar,
Bheege har din, jeevan ke spar.

Mann ko path, paani ka dhur,
Jab milti adar, dikhe sahan.

Mann ki dhun, sahil ki thi,
Kajal ki dhara, milte aur rahi.

Mann pe bhari, paani ki dhir,
Jab milad har, sabhi ti sevir.

Mann ka kissa, sarovar ki bakshi,
Sukoon ki lehar, aankhon ki kheki.

Mann ki panka, tal ke kinare,
Jab dhundle chaman, snan hote kare.

Mann thakan, nadi ki dhipay,
Jab sahar jaawe, tab liye mai.

Mann ki kal, dera ki nadi,
Jung hi pare, sukh ki nadi.

Mann ki marj, sagar ki lehar,
Jab kalp sab, aage chhwere jahar.

Mann kara dhara, paani ki jhal,
Jab anand pane brahma, mil mil.

Mann ki baat, nadi ki sang,
Har pal ki dhul, nirvan ki rang.

Mann ka jahar, jheel ki boond,
Jab dhul nikle, jeevan ke char.

Mann ki dhara, samundar ki shok,
Jab bhakti dhadke, khushbu ko mok.

Mann ki chhod, deep ki lehar,
Mitti ki nibhi, paani ke sahar.

Mann ki ore, paani ka saaz,
Jab vivek tal, mitti se taas.

Mann ki bikri, nadi ki bhagan,
Jab samajh ho, jadar ke aga.

Mann ke aash, samundar ki katan,
Jab lagti dhara, pratthvi ka man.

Mann ki roti, nadi ki choti,
Dhar ke mile, dharti ki adhoti.

Mann ase kar, paani ki sargam,
Jab milke chale, anant ke rang.

Mann ho shant, tal of the nadi,
Jab milti preet, baadal ke chaadi.

Mann ka resa, samundar kee dharan,
Jo bujh jaave, nadi ka nirmaan.

Uthti savere man bana deep, jo andhakar ko mitla

Maya ki raat andheri, roshni se khelti,
Jab tak samajh na aaye, ankhon se andhera dhalte.

Savera jab aaye, maya ka dhuaan pichhe chhootê,
Jis dil mein Satya basa, uska man na dhootê.

Raat ki chadar odh ke, jagat ke rang pehlê,
Alag alag rang dikhte, asli rang sabko melê.

Maya ki chidiya, din ke dhoop mein pakadê,
Jab usko chodh dê, kundalini se baandhê.

Raat ka sikka maya, din ke upar tikê,
Jo na samjhe isko, bhool jayê apna dhikê.

Saawan ki barish maya, bhigoti har shair,
Jo isse na bhigê, uska dil sadai teer.

Maya ki dhool se, savera dhundhla ho jata,
Satguru ke charno mein, sab rang bikhar jata.

Raat ke deep jalte, maya ka jhalak dikhê,
Jab man shudh ho jaye, andhera rung hawê.

Maya ke jharna, din ki nadi se baha,
Jo isme dub jaye, vahi vyakul rahe savarâ.

Raat ka sahara maya, sabko bhoolê bhari,
Jab mukti ki roshni, uski deh pe kheri.

Maya ka chhalka, savera ki subah se milê,
Jo sarve vishw ko, apne charno me pîlê.

Raat ke ghumand mein, maya ka naksh hili,
Guru ki baat suni, to chira kal shash li.

Maya ki baadal, din ki kirno ko chhupây,
Satya ki jalti roshni, usko dekh kabhô nây.

Raat ke rang-hue, maya ki lagti haan,
Jab bhuul jaye bandhan, to aata naya gyaan.

Maya ki pirohan, savera ke sooraj se,
Jo samjhe na isko, phir namaz mein machhar.

Raat ki chhaap mein, maya ka rang bhara,
Jab gyaan ki roshni, mil jaye, to har sahara.

Maya ka totka, din ke dekhne se nirmal,
Jiska mann sthir ho, usko aage paayal.

Raat ki baat badi, maya ki chadar funda,
Guru ke sang, jagta, pravash hue yeh muda.

Maya ke baagh, savera ki dhool mein raat,
Jab dhyaan se dekho to, milta hai anant.

Raat bhari bhulawa, maya ke rang jage,
Satya ka sapna, peeth uthaye se jage.

Maya ka jharna, din ki noon mei sahara,
Jo usme dhop raha, uska mann bhara.

Raat ki jo dhul, maya ko bhi rang deti,
Jab buddhi uthi, to sab jagah chhantti.

Maya ki masti, savera ki shuruaat,
Jab man dharti par, dhyaan ki baat.

Raat ke sahare, maya ka phal gheta,
Satguru ki kirn se, tuta sab teta.

Maya ka pul, din ke rishte tod,
Satva ko khol ke, vidhioke se mod.

Raat ki dhoolon mein, maya ka rang bhara,
Mushkil raahon pe, dhyan se utha dhara.

Maya ki baat, savera ka beeth,
Jab man se utaar, to milti raat ki reet.

Raat ka gunja, maya ki chadpur,
Satya ki baat ho, to shunya mein murt.

Maya ki reet, din ki baalti se,
Jab dhairya se rukkhe, to naya roshni aave.

Raat ki silta, maya ka shabd chhupa,
Jab hum soch rahe, to uska pahra mufa.

Maya ke sang, savera ki rukh nayi,
Jise mil jaye vrat, to bhula bhakri bhayi.

Raat ka dhokha, maya ke rang chada,
Jo gyaan se jeeti, to dhul ho gaya nash.

Maya ka dhav, din ki baat se tukda,
Satguru ki nash se, palat hothi chitta.

Raat ko mita, maya ko mil paik,
Jab mulayam hi ho, wo dharti ki riy.

Maya ki chadi, savera ke vichaar,
Jab dhyan ki lai hoti, to sab dhup paare.

Raat ki ghadi, maya ka sandhan pichha,
Satya ka cheen, to haath mein jichha.

Maya ka saagar, din ki lehar ke bhitar,
Jab bhakti ho uddi, kehta aapji vitar.

Raat ka aab, maya ki chamak aisi,
Jab saans mein satva, to dur jahar ki bari.

Maya ki kujh, savera ki puja lathi,
Jab ankho se dekho, to roshni ka dhati.

Raat ke dhaga, maya ka bandhan jode,
Jab man dhule sat, to pithrai se bode.

Maya ki maali, din ki suraj se bhag,
Satjano dekh le, sankat har bhag.

Raat ka pashu, maya ke jaal me chipak,
Jab gyaan daurti, to josh bhi bhikshak.

Maya ki tasveer, savera ki chaap se,
Jab hridaya dhankar, to sidhi ho aap.

Raat ki duniya, maya ka kalpana,
Satyantra ko jhalki, mann dhyan ki sona.

Guru ki baat sun le, to dhoop kholdu.

Jab man ko laga, to sanjeevani maal.

Jab aasan se hat, to milti sharan.

Satya karta dhwar, man ki sojan.

Naav ko ghosh se tu chadhaa, par pahiye sabh dekhla
Jab tak aatmaa ka sahara, naav asit haath na chhukla

Sundar saanjh ki chaaon mein, naav baandhi khud ke ghum
Jab tak ahankaar ke pedh, uski paar na ho payi dhum

Mitti ka ghoda, naav ke paani mein, dhool se bhi dhola
Jab swabhimaan ki lehar uthe, to paar nikle na bhola

Jhoot ki ghadi mein naav chadh kar, sansar ka sahara
Satya ke kinare paar hoga, jab bhava bhool jaayega mara

Dan ki deewar ki baat, naav ko dhaar se chhune
Jab ahankaar ka dhokha, na pahunche uske ghune

Kali raat ke suraj mein, naav ka nishaan chhapa
Jab dil ka kamal khile, tab hi milti hai jaan ki chhapa

Mitti ki bhigni mirch, naav ko jaltiyaa patang
Jab ahankaar ki lehar, le jaaye paar ka rang

Paani ke beech se naav, thapke thaak saagar
Jab bhakti ki lehar aati, to aaavege pyaar ka aagar

Nadiyon ka raasta, naav ko baandha dheere
Jab mann ki kampan ko milti, dharti pe dhale theere

Mitti ki gachh, naav ko bheshe khel
Jab ahankaar ko dhaarya, unka than na chale mel

Reet ki thali, naav ko chalti hawaa
Jab dhyan ke deep jalte, ahankar ki baat bhulaa

Mitti ke jharne se naav, dhare ka sipahi
Jab sach ki dhun bajti, to bhava ka pariksha dihi

Tota ki bhavri, naav ki baat ka sang
Jab ahankar ki gaari, khula na ho ise rang

Loon ki roshni, naav ko dikhaye din
Jab bhakti ki talaash kaul, man milta hai kin

Pankh ki dhool se naav, aasman ki piroli
Jab ahankaar ke khoj, vishaal na ho doli

Mitti ki chadar, naav ki ganga
Jab shanti ke charna se, ahankaar pare bhanga

Umeed ki gauri, naav ki shikhar
Jab dhyaan ki dor chalti, ahankaar ko rikhsohar

Dhan ki chadar, naav ko tatha milan
Jab bhakti ki dhara samjhe, apna koi na rahan

Chaur ki dhar, naav ko padhara se
Jab mrit ka gyan kar, ahankaar ka na sahara se

Raat ki sheher, naav ko dhoyu chadar
Jab anand ki ratt mein, ahankaar hi aati udhar

Saawan ki baras, naav ko dhoop se bhar
Jab bhakti ke chadar tan, ahankar chhoot jaata jahar

Dharti ki dharin, naav ko rung paahat
Jab sadhe ka paal, ahankaar ke request jhoot

Jal ki baat, naav ko inju baadal
Jab satyavaan ke bhav se, ego ka pal vishaal

Gaon ki ghaas, naav ki bhavri nahi
Jab vishwa ki chhata se, ahankar chhota hi kafi

Mandir ki dhool, naav ki dhoop hai
Jab sannata ki dhwani, ahankar ko mitti banaye

Chirag ki roshni naav ko bhula de
Jab mann ki bhakti baandhe, apne hi dhoor ki gade

Murgi ki zindgi, naav ko desi basti
Jab ahankaar ka dhoop, ghoda ki par sikati

Bagal ki suraj, naav ki saidi
Jab gyaan ki diyayi, ahankar ko pehchaana

Kosa ki chadar, naav ke parinde ke neeche
Jab man ki vinash kshetra, ahankar ki dagdgi

Ras ki masti, naav ki bansi tan
Jab anant bhakta ke sang, ego ki pahadi mukt

Patang ki leher, naav ki dhaam dikhaye
Jab prem ki kitaab ho, ahankaar ki rang na rhay

Kavach ki dhool, naav behteya haun
Jab sahara ke charna ko, ego ki mirgi na chhaun

Nadi ki pallav, naav ki punya lehar
Jab sach ki yaad aati, ego ka andhakar

Pataka ki dhuni, naav ke vajra se
Jab aatma ke roshni, ahankaar ka roofa smesh

Bargad ki hansi, naav pe lagaudi sa
Jab man ki raah pakde, ahankaar ke milte te

Shakti ki gagan, naav oh khtaarna
Jab bhakti ke kannahe, ego ke jalti bagad

Mithaas ki bhanwar, naav sight ham
Jab bhola dhyaan se, asram apni nadiya

Paar ki chadar, naav chalti
Jab lallan ka kati, ahankaar na kisi mahar

Jab sadhgi ki paat, ahankaar ka gunj

Jab man ki dhuniya, ahankar ki asahra

Jab bhakti ki lehar, ahankar ka ghoomi khuli

Moti milti nahin pukaare, jo apni dhun pe bitta

Prem ki dhun sun ke baje, har khaal ko milti ar.

Dil ki ankho se dekh, aaina nahin koi dhoka;
Prem se milti hai ratan ki, jahan mile wo jhoor

Jab dil ki yatra mein aave, kabir ka paathar;

Maya ki chadar, dhundh se dhak le jaati,
Jab dwaar khulega, andar andhera hi chaati।

Ghar ki deewaaren toote, jab prem ka gyaan aata,
Maya ka kamra mita, sach ka deep jalta।

Dhoop se nahi, chhanv se dhokha milta,
Maya ka darwaza khula, bhool jata kalat।

Mitti ke ghode ki chaal, paaon mein dhool,
Maya ki gaadi aati, bina basool।

Chulha jalta, par roti na banti,
Maya ki roti poori, khwaab mein hi danti।

Saaya ki chhanv me, paani ka chaap,
Maya ka ghar chhupa, andhkaar ki paap।

Pankh nahi, palang par baith hai,
Maya ki udaan, dhool ki reet hai।

Maya ki chaal rahi, aaj bhi humsafar baata।

Maya ke grah ki dugni, sukh ka sahare।

Maya ki bhool se, zindagi bhas.

Maya ka raaz, duavan ke ghazal.

Maya ki jalti bei, roshni se bhil.

Maya ke aangan mein ghul gelfra.

Maya ki daali pe, gham ka mahal।

Maya ki pyari, aasha ki sang।

Maya ke darwaze, khulte hi dhala।

Sadiyon ka zevar, par raat se bhari,
Maya ka milap, roshni se dhari।

Maya ki pareshani, mann ka dara.

Maya ke pul se, na mile khaal।

Maya ki raat me, ankhen bhas.

Maya ke bandhan se, har ek koi.

Samay ke baadal chhaye, kal ki chhanv ka jhalak,
Jo samjhe usko milti, sukh ki ankhon ki badal.

Pal beet jaata hai jaise barish ki boondein,
Jise ginna na jaaye, wo hamesha sukh ki dhune.

Ghadi ke dhol ki taal, kabhi rukti nahin,
Jitni jaldi beh gayi, wo kshema ki raat.

Samay ki chakki ghoome, turant chakri mein,
Jis ne ghoda laga liya, ban gaye uske grah.

Badal ki chaadar dharti ko chhoote,
Ussi chadar mein bhatak jata hai jeevan ka rog.

Mitti se nikla phool, samay se tham ke,
Bhool jise samajh na paaye, wo khul jaye andhakar.

Barish ki boondein dhoop se mil jaye,
Aise samay ki baat, bhool na le koi bhola.

Samay ki meetha, khara aur kadwa,
Jo birha to aata, phir na aata samay.

Raat ka aangan, subah ki roshni,
Samay ko samajh, milega anand ki hi nishani.

Badalon ki chhaya mein ghoor, sapna dekhna,
Samay ke sang rang, melo jaisa badhkar.

Pal doob ke utre, har ghadi ki rehte,
Jo diya chhod de, vo dayal ka haath sahi.

Samay ki bagal me ghun ho ja, barish ki baat,
Jiska rogi balidaan de, mil jaati bat.

Ghud ki jaglo na ghadi, bhare reht hon,
Samay khichda jaaye, phone to kal ki rahti.

Jab barish aayi khali, sadiyo ki baat,
Samay ki bhanva hote waqt ki kshath.

Narak ki dhaar se puchho, samay aapki,
Jab jala wo aag aati, kabhi aaj jaaye.

Badal ghair ko dhool deta hai, tatka thakan,
Samay ki baat sukh ki roop ki ghan.

Ghadi jaisi bhari, basil anjaa,
Samay ke funsh ke baal saadha baajaye.

Barish ki dhara mein aati, akal ka yeh raaz,
Samay ke peeche aate, yarak badla ki aas.

Chhe janne caraje, baadal ka murjha raat,
Samay ka dikhaye rok , puja hai jhoot.

Kucch bhi utarna chalna, waqt ki dinodhai,
Bhutor nadiyon se, samajh kaadi bhai.

Samay ki vaani rasha, dhool se ubhri,
Tension ko bhar, phir samay ke banch.

Baadal se aati ki khushbu ki barg,
Samay ke jaane do judunde baag.

Chand ki ros ki ghal, raat manha guzar,
Samay chalata jaye freeze, duniya ko niwar.

Aandhi aati khin, samay ki chha sakti hai,
Phir bhi rishte katik, moh ki dillai kai.

Ghat ne ki dhare, barish abesha,
Samay ki tez bun, koi bhi nahin bhasha.

Badhusar ki zukhe, sadiyo parvan,
Samay chhootha dil se, bhookha acharya.

Samay ki ghat ja, gialo ajj, barish,
Par yaad ghal se, prakaas miraci.

Har baras at aane mein tum, samay ka lakın,
Mitti se bhool, pahsi mitti, agar avel.

Ghadi aakri saman hi raahein barobar,
Samay bhikht Allah ko, kaun ham bidaad.

Nadiyi ki dhori baadal, phusi samay ka~,
Kamal ko aapka phir pista jagdaya.

Samay ki khanasi, puri chalti,
Awur teedo ki, sabko lihazi rakhte.

Jab ahankar ki leher, nadi se udhar bahke,
Saagar ki gehrayi usko hi dhul jaye.

Nadi ke sang mil kar, ahankari patthar dhul,
Jab ghoor se dekhte hain, samundar rooth jaata.

Paani ka ek hi raaz, chhote se chhota boond,
Jo apna maane, usme sardari ka rang.

Mitti ki bhanwar mein, ego ka jaluhar,
Jab uthe samundar, to phir chhota pashu.

Nadi ke raaste, ahankar ko dhoye,
Jalti matti bhi dhul, jab dhara mil jaaye.

Jab dharti se milti, nadi ki sada,
Ahankar ka sahara, hawa ke jaisa sara.

Samundar ki leher, jhukti nahi kabhi,
Maan dhola poodh ki, ego ki chubhi.

Jal ki boond banti, samay ki mithi dhara,
Jab ahankar dhool bana, to jeevan mara.

Gadi ki mahasagar, paani ko sumaar,
Jab ahankar ko dhoye, roshni phir bar.

Nadi ke kinare, arkan ki khabar,
Jab khud ko vishva, to paani jhoor.

Jal ki lat, paani ki rang, ahankar ka ghoor,
Nadi par chhod de, samudr ki dor.

Kadam se kadam, paani ki dhara,
Ahankar ka paath, bhool na dhara.

Mitti ki lahri, nadi ki sharan,
Ego ka paani, aakri saazgari arman.

Jal ki dhara, ahankar ki makhan,
Samundar ki karwat, bhuli raahat.

Nadi ki lahar, ahankar ki asar,
Jab dhukaari jaye, shanti par.

Paani ka sahara, nadi ki kracht,
Ego ko dhoye to phir bina racht.

Samundar ke teer, ahankar ka sankat,
Jab bhukhe mar jaane, narm paani.

Pyaala mein paani, ahankar ka mach,
Jab paida na hove, toha kis baat.

Nadi ki baat, dil ki baat, ego ke dip,
Shanti ki lehar usme nadh ke sip.

Paani ka gunj, ahankar ka paat,
Jab shehar dhule, to karta naap.

Samudra ki aankhen, paani ke jode,
Jab yaad rakhe nein, ahankar ki chode.

Nadi ka rang, ahankar ka rang,
Jab koshish bhi na ho, shees ka sang.

Jal mein bikhar, ahankar ka lihaaz,
Jab mil jaye sabhi, to vishwa saaz.

Sagar ki aphim, ahankar ka prash,
Nadi ki lehar, usko chhod jaash.

Paani ki saans, ahankar ki paath,
Samundar ke kinara, manas kalaa.

Nadi ki ghad, ego ke patan,
Jab sade sab, to chhote ratna.

Jal ki ghat, ahankar ke nishaan,
Nadi ki basira, khulti aap ki shaan.

Samundar ka patta, ego ka drisht,
Jab bhanwar ho jaye, to phir shakt.

Paani ka sahara, ahnkar ki piyaas,
Nadi ke sang milkar, shanti ki vimaas.

Jal ki saans, egor ka daal,
Nadi ki bahaar, dil ki raat.

Samundar ki ghooms, ahankar ki lalkahi,
Jab aavashyak hove, to ghat ki bhogi.

Paani ki baat, ahankar ki taaz,
Nadi ke dhul pe, mann sabir naz.

Nadi ki rakh, ego ki rait,
Samudr se milkar, saagar se baat.

Jal ki baadal, ahankar ke paak,
Nadi ki mukti, milti mann ki bhook.

Samundar ke sahare, ego ka i-jan,
Rind ke dhula, nadi ki tjaan.

Paani ka ujala, ahankar roga,
Nadi ki lambi, hriday ki bhaja.

Sagar ki laḍ, ego ka nakh,
Nadi ke sang sang, milti aasha.

Jal ki dhara, ahankar ki vinas,
Nadi ke bharta, man ki hi bhava.

Samudr ke chaka, ahankar ki ghat,
Jal ka ghor, mann ki abad.

Paani ka sankalp, ego ki kharabi,
Nadi par noke, utpadhyad ke chaabi.

Jab nadi ka ishta, ahankar ka dhola,
Sagar ki bhola, alag se hi gola.

Pani ka raag, ahankar ki baat,
Nadi ke gagan, sundar roop.

Samundar ki dhool, egor ko bhay,
Jab syt vuj udh, to mach rach.

Jal ki sudhar, ego ke sahi,
Nadi ki dhar, sukh aate bin.

Samundar ki dhal, ahankar ki gai,
Paani ki shanti, dya tini.

Nadi ki ladi, ego ki javan,
Sagar ki jhooth, sab chhuta saran.

Paani ka sahara, ahankar ki baar,
Jab dikh rahi, to kul yeh dar.

Samudr ka pahar, ego ke roshni,
Nadi ke teri, dil ke bhan

Paani ka alam, ahankar ka arath,
Nadi ki sehan, man ke at.

Samundar ki baat, ego ki daur,
Jab raas na ho, toh jag ki chaur.

Jab antah se roshni aayi, raah sabke *saath* pund

Prem ka sagar gahra, patthar bhi doob jaata hai
Dil ke gehre tal par, heera bhi dhool ho jaata hai

Jab prem se dil bharta, kaante bhi ful jaate hain
Patthar ki dehleez pe, phoolon ka rang chha jaata hai

Lehen prem ko jala, patthar se nikle aag
Jitna roshni bhare, utna adhura raag

Heere ke jaise anmol, prem ki baat suno
Koi shithil dharti pe, na paaye iski chaan

Guru bina jeevan andhera, jaise patthar ki raat
Jab guru mile roshni, heere ka roop paat

Guru hi milta hai jise, man ki shakti milti
Patthar se bhi zyada, uski baat me gehri dhilti

Guru ki sharan mein, dukh ka sab kuch bhool
Heere jaise roz giri, hriday me phool

Guru ke charanon me, patthar bhi narm ho jaye
Jiski dhun suno, mann se baajhi veena bajaye

Guru hi so paimana, jiska darpan sacha
Patthar ki chuhi ke jaise, dhokha nahi kuch bhi acha

Guru ki bani se, patthar bhi ragini banta
Heere ki chamak se, bhul jaye sab ranta

Guru ki baat ko sune, chahe andhera ho bijli
Patthar ko pighla de, uski shabd ki bhul ki

Hans ki bhakti se milti, chidiya ki chah re man,
Sang sang jo sadhu milo, phir na rahe koi dhyan.

Mandir ki bhiti na bhare, jo padi hai man ki dhool,
Hans ki leela suno sang, sukh ka ho jaye pool.

Sang samundar jaisa gahra, shabd koi na samjhe,
Hans ki pehchan dikhaye, jo geet ko aaye.

Sadhu ki bani hai tasveer, kanvase ka rang bhari,
Pakshi ki chhalang se aata, dhyan ka dhoop nayi.

Hans ki awaz se uddta, jivan ka asmaan,
Sadhu ke sang ka sukh, milta hai anjaam.

Satsang ki dasan bhari, andhe ke liye roshni,
Hans ki paheli ko haath, lete hain ham daga.

Ghusna sa rang jhaag ka, jo dikhata na dharti,
Sadhu sang sab milke, toota hai gagan ke.

Hans ki pankh lagti par, vichlon ki hawa,
Sang sadhu milke padhte, dhool ka jadoo ba.

Man ki chaadar dhoti, hans ki dhun ke sang,
Sadangi safar se milti, aasha ka rang.

Hans ki jhad ke patte, sahara milta khil,
Sadhu ki kavita se, dhyaan ka rang mil.

Sang sadhu ki baadal, hans ki raah badi,
Bhadti hai dharti ko, shanti ke chedi.

Hans ki sudhi baatein, sahara dum ka gagan,
Sadhu ke qadam se, milti bhawan ki dhan.

Mitti mein roti, hans ki jhalak,
Sadhu ke sang hum, sahara mil lahek.

Mann ki dhajjan me, hans ki jalti urdu,
Sadhu ki juda jamana, satha ki chahat ko.

Hans dikhate hai, dhyaan ki koi nadi,
Sadhu sang sadiyon tak, dharti se yahi sodha.

Hans ki chaah ke sang, sadhu ki baat mil,
Doojon ke dhoop mein, aayenge sab mil.

Sadhi ki antari ki tord gaane sab,
Hans ki chonk mitti ke.

Hans ko sudhi ki choon, sadhu ki roshni haas,
Mann ko rahi mili mai ke phelya tha

Satsang ki pui, hans ke chhahi pankh dil,
Sadhu se milkar bhanwar ki haathon

Hans ke aashirvead, sadhu ki bhakti bhare,
Sikkon ki sahara milti aani chal.

Man ki dhara se hans, sadhu ke sang naye,
Roshni ki chashma kholta sath aakaash.

Seer ka dhoop sanguratan, hans ki chaad,
Saduni doodh se mil rahi mulya ki prad.

Hans ki hi liye code lhai rakh,
Sadhu ke hansur tol jata

Utpatti ki bhavyas, hans ke aakrit,
Sangan meno hi sahma hain vishvas ki.

Saat chhode savirri, hans ki bandhan,
Sadhu ke adeek samabta mil pa yeh.

Jab man ki nadi behkaye, toh dharam ki nagri dhundh
Paar lag jayegi shunya se, jab kabira ka naam ghoondh

Samundar ki leher se poochho, aansu ka kirana kyon chhuta

Guru ka aagman, nadi ki naav hai,
Jise dekh kar sab dar lagti sahara.

Jisne dikhaya paar ka raasta,
Woh hi to hai bhakti ka aashra.

Naav ko chhodi kar dikhaye jo dhyaan,
Guru ki baat mein milti praana.

Jal ki lehron se jo dar gye,
Guru ki shabd se milati rahat.

Jab guru na ho to paani bhari,
Naav tek nakki, kahin na chale bhari.

Sadhu ki padhai se chalti hai naav,
Har pal dharm ka deepak jagaye.

Sagar ke beech jahan koi na pakde,
Guru ki leela se milti raahein.

Jab man dhoran ka jata hai kangal,
Guru ka chehra hi hota sangalamat.

Guru ke charan chune to bhari.

Guru ki Mitrata se poori ho jaye.

Guru ki baat mein milti ujala.

Guru ke aashirvaad se dharti meethe.

Guru ke shabd hi hoti dharti ke rang.

Guru ki bhakti mein poori kalik.

Naav ke aatma se milti baat.

Guru ki baat hi bolta kam.

Bharpur karti, jivan ki gaye.

Jab man ki lau takraaye,
Guru ke sang, naav ki tulaaye.

Jo puja ki thali me roti, bhed bhar ke bhagwan ke naam lagaye,
Chaand bhi sharmaye, jab dharm ko dikhaya jaata hai pehlu ke parchaye.

Mitti ki jaat ka jhund, mandir ki deewar pe likhe apne aap,
Suraj ki roshni bhi pehchaan na sake, andhera jahan dikhaye dhap.

Chaand ki chaadar bhi ubhri, jab manushya andar se ho dhan.

Samaj ke andhar saans le, dharm ka rang khokar mil jaye.

Suraj ki roshni me aakhri ro 'tilash.

Chaand ke parde khul gaye, ki samata ki dhool kon.

Suraj ki dekhbhal, beda padh.

Pari ke puche, chalane ki ghati ki mein baat,
Aulad likhato musti, suraj ki aate.

Jal ke marleton, jaan lo, mastik ko roz,
Chaand ki reh, mann ki baat janun.

Tajiling mein rakhe haan demalah.

Jab tak na dekhe Rab, jhilmil na jaga.

Jo rah mein pyare, wohi to bas gaye.

Par sachcha saaksh, Pita ka anurag.

Jab khelo bhakti, to har pagaasa.

Jab khilti se karm ki saaj.

Jith pai mein vishva.

Rahiye anand kee matii.

Man ki deep ko jala, andhera chhuta hai pare,
Jab antarmann se dhua bhasha, to jagat roshan ho jaye.

Mitti se aaya hum, dhool se wapas milenge,
Jis tan mein sachchai ki roshni, vo kabhi na dhulenge.

Jab bhakti bin baat, to kaun sunega dhaar,
Antar ki kalpana hi aag ka sahara.

Sadhana ki ghanti bajti, jab man ko saaf kare,
Maya ki andhiyon ko, roshni se raas karta.

Jeevan ka paani, samundar se milta nahi,
Par jo deepak jalaye, uski roshni sabko paata.

Sukh ki dhoop mein, gyaan ka daana na bhoola,
Aandhera jab mil jaaye, to usse dhune ka shaula.

Raat ki chadar mein, jag magar jala hai,
Jab man ke deep tak dhyan, aati roshni ki kali.

Jab chaandni se bhi, zyada roshni ki ichchha,
To bhakti se jagat, phir bhi rah jata naach.

Mitti ki tarah saaf, mann ki baat,
Deepak ki roshni ka ahankar bhi aate.

Viraam ki ghadi mein, gyaan ka prahar,
Jab na manjhe maan ki dhoop, to khud hi dagar.

Saagar ki lehar mein, ek chhota sa deep,
Jab dhare pe dhwaj udhar, to sambhal jaye bhiksh.

Sookh ke baag me, jyoti se taal milti,
Dukh ka sang kyon, man ki chodiyaan hi milti.

Kavach jo dhatu ka, mann ki aasha,
Rahat ki roshni se, kabir ki dhara ghaz.

Guru ki baat suno, roop sikho na bhoola,
Antim din tak, deep jo jahaan se paala.

Deep ki subah ki roshni, se milti desh bhara.

Man ki roshni paribhit ghoori.

Aankher gati, ghulane ko.

Jadi jarnadri jaye mane se.

Vijayn ka gyaan dikhla.
