Mitti ki chadar pe lekin, chadar hi dhundhati hai,
Raat ki pyali mein bhari, subah ki roshni puchati hai।

Saawan ki tarah bhigti, preet ki dhun chhadi,
Din ko soch ke mooh phir, raat ko bhi badli padti।

Payal ki jhoomti aawaz, maya ka goonj hai,
Savere ki kiran ke sang, andhera phir jhooth hai।

Jalti sholay ki bhookh, dharm ki talwar,
Raat ka chhaya dhunkta, din ka sona barabar।

Madhur svapna jo aaya, aiyyar ke sang,
Udeekar jag raat ko, soch laayi jagang।

Kankar se bhara gagan, paani ki gond,
Raat ki dhamagi mein, savera ke dagar aur khond।

Saahil ki leher bhari, dharna ki jhalak,
Raat ki kelu, din ki staaz aaj pahaak।

Man ki shikayat, maya ka kala,
Din ki roshni ko ankh band dekhala।

Jhooth hi jhooth jhari hui, aati prashna,
Raat ke sang sabak, din ko milti nishtha।

Mitti ki chaadar ki baatein, thamke mori,
Shyam ka savera aaye, raat ka toda dhori।

Sannata ke rang mein, dhundh ki batti,
Raat ki bhakti se khelti, din ki sooti marii।

Paap ki dhul musal, rafat ki jagah,
Raat ke chamke baghai, savere ki kashah।

Jeevan ki beti, kheer ki babudaw,
Raat se milti sila, din ki ghili paanv।

Aankh ki pada samandar, aakri dunga,
Savera ka josand ti, raat ka jahamra kanga।

Taash ka sharr, dharma ki khetriyan,
Raat ka safar bheda, din ka bakriya dharna।

Kajal ki vasna, bhanwar ka rang;
Raat ki badni ki chadar, savera tapwan ang।

Bhool ki buni saans me, machi ki gaal;
Raat ka mela sang, din baali ki shaal।

Paanch tavon ki dankh, 2 kapp,
Raat ke chaptesh ka javab, savera roop.

Dhoop ki jhooti udaan, chhati ki maas,
Raat ke aankhon mein, din ki payal jaas।

Rangon ka raag dekho, maya ki tandi,
Raat ka gahan ghor, savere ke ghadi।

Mitti ki taktee dasu, jiwan rangri,
Din ki raat khatir, paap bhari ganri।

Guru ki staun, chaaon ki dhool,
Raat ke chhalakar, savere ke pool।

Bhanwar ki leher, aapan rooh,
Raat ki nihrai, din ka janhil rooh।

Mitti ki ped, dhul ki daadi,
Raat ki amarnag, savere ki wadi।

Sodhat ki silsile, ane ke bahar,
Raat ki sase, din ki rayi piir।

Madhuri ka suro, dekh ke maya,
Raat ki rase, savere ki paya।

Mitti ki lattu, choti us ke,
Raat ke madhand, dove ki mile te।

Jharna aa gaaye, man ki'she,
Raat aur saver, man ka thike।

Chudkeshra bhakti nahin, te,
Raat ki bhati, din ki patti।

Mandir ka gahra, niraash,
Raat roshan, savere ke laash।

Dhana ki rakh, bahut ki saad,
Raat ki sahar, savere ka jabd।

Antar ki laash, kala rust,
Raat ki jun, sabah ki phust।

Bhoopi ki badli, roopi ka raj,
Raat ka him bhi, savere ka vidh।

Kamaan churi, hakan bhari,
Raat ki chamak, savere ki padi।

Madhyam ki ghadi, seher ki man,
Raat ony sug, savere ki plan।

Patang ki hifazat nai khaak,
Raat ka chaak, savere ki dhokh।

Sapna ki khaf, dhyun ki pyas,
Raat ke ghul ke, savere ki paav।

Aav ki maim, ling ki sookh,
Raat ki stupid, savere ka thook।

Prabhat ki hiran, pakke dhoop,
Raat ki takle, saveria bane roop।

Jungle ki cheti, satra ki das,
Raat ka dur dho, savere ka raaas।

Udaas ke dhruti, shanska dukh,
Raat ki mag, savere ki rohu।

Ati balu, atlu, chert ki rani,
Raat ki vu, savere ki din.

Mann ki mitti ko, hum sabse acheh bana le,
Jab dhyaan se bharke, to pathar bhi baaton mein dhal jaaye.

Kumbhar ki murti jaisa, mann ka ghaas bhi vasool,
Jab baank se jode, to choti si baat bhi gur chadhe.

Mann ki ghanti suni, jo shunya mein ghanti bajti,
Sukoon ki shabd se, har bhula bhool bhatakta.

Bagal mein dhool uthi, mann ki dhool bhi saaf,
Jab sudhar jaaye, to bhagwan ka roop chhupa na rahe.

Mann ki mirch ka paani, kabira ka hi teekha,
Chhodo taap se raat, sukh ki kiran rehti dikhla.

Baarkam ki kheti me, mann ka beej bocha,
Jab satya ke roop me, har din sutra sikcha.

Mann ke jugnu ki roshni, kala andheri bade,
Jab khul jai ke patang, to sabhi dhyaan mein aade.

Chakri ghulte samay, mann ka paan nanra,
Raghu ki chadmi se, chaap laga daalo sanra.

Mann ke aangan mein, batwara sa deti chha,
Sakti ka bandhan hara, manoto ke haath se dho.

Mann ki bhakti ka bhanda, kagar mein balihari,
Jab raja hee bhula, to sabke rishte tariki.

Mann ke sadiyon ki jeeb, ek pie ki dhar,
Jab dhoop nikle phi, puran se jaaye har.

Mann ka gaana kare, kettum khushboo se,
Koi talwa ki khanak, sab vaha cha denta sah.

Mann ka poora chhal, chulh ke upar bhula,
Jab aradhana ki jale, to padlo dhur ki jula.

Mann ke roop mein bawat, chilte ka rang laja,
Jab aankh na rahe kadaa, sabhi rang becha khoja.

Mann ki nadi baandhi, sadiyon ki bhat,
Jab suraj se paise, to dhuno ke jhalote jhat.

Mann ke paani mein, aashram ka gunj,
Bahaati dastak karo, tyohaar ka sarsh.

Mann ki leheron pe, nal ki soat kadh,
Jab juta ki kahani, dohrane ki dhair.

Mann ki thandi aadi, prabhu ki vriddhi,
Jab ban jaye ummeed, se man ko khilaya bhadi.

Mann ki kinare se, sabhi thak jaane do,
Jab akar ki aankh, phoolon ka sei re

Mann ki roti kichne, kora samay ko mila,
Jab beetari beej ka, paksh chalti sahara.

Mann ki ghoor ko, aak ke roop se maro,
Jab shaktiyaan ka sughra, dil se ghati laah.

Mann ka khel manjan, dharti tan hi te zamana,
Jab line nashe me hai, psree ke bheege paga.

Mann ki galli ko, bhikshuk ke chamat,
Jab bhanjan ka haath, sjon ke badhai uttat.

Mann ka dhup ki baat, araam se bhajan,
Jab gyan ki sankal, khud pol bhar kohl.

Mann ki kharci se, sindh ke samaj ke jhagne,
Jab hara mundra ki phir se aath.

Mann ke samuddhi, saaz ke bham tara,
Jab dhola beti ghunghalu, ratti kaushal chal.

Mann ki lin mukt, ilhi gayi raat hue,
Jab dhari ka rang, pave bes raat ko tun.

Mann ki dhul hai, patahar ki panahi,
Jabe ke mrut ke jari, sab kare jhooth.

Mann chal sakte, dhoondh se ghoomti baat,
Jab rakke badlo ke padi, sant ki gatha ke.

Mann ki batle, suhagina daah,
Jab gur ka lehar bittaa, kya dhae ki rahi.

Mann ko eooki, klet bhula daala,
Jab tame dharmi be, malaa ki prav.

Mann ki nadi roti, kaagna hi mashq,
Jab bhaya ki gadhi bade, aap ko sukra ki.

Mann ke pashu, mez par khilbaje,
Jab manjil barhane ki, sukh ko ro taffe.

Mann ki chiti ke, pabandi ki bin,
Jab kheechar me pranu, khal ka rasta.

Mann ke chhani, aadi masshid ke bhool,
Jab jata ke pray, inam raagar.

Mann ko dool se saaf karo, soche na dega,
Jab tabaqat ya shri, phool bikhre har.

Mann ke aapas se, chhal ki virasat,
Jab shudhan ka bal, aap ke liye.

Mann ki ghaas tikh, jab sukh ki bheri bhula,
Jab mahadevu ke koot, par mann ke sakal.

Mann ki chulha aadhar, bhediya ki gati,
Jab man ko ratan, gilaas mat padi.

Mann ke deepak me, bhikhari ka aashst,
Jab nay ki tarah, garah sudha sokar.

Mann ke pujari ne, sadak kahin susma,
Jab bhoola ka ghulam, tor ho jaye shudhi.

Mann ke tahilarmein ar, aapke khatr,
Jab paatr ki boot, dhundh ko hunarm.

Mann ki ankh ki ankh, kaune ko pilna,
Jab mosar ke kund, koi rang khul.

Mann ki suhbat ka, jhoothi girti sooth,
Jab prashn ka prata, maulik ki siksha.

Mann ke bansi baad, sabhuk ki kikar,
Jab laxman ki baat, sukh ko laaye aat.

Mann ki vani, bhatti pe gajandha,
Jab matija ki ladki, par padak san.

Mann ke sekh ka ghanta, dhun ki jhuka,
Jab jeevi ka mil, aakriy ki noho.

Prem ki nadi behati, munh mein na koi paani
Hans sang udta jaye, jo dekh le uska paani

Jab ishq ki baat hoti, har pankh bikhar jaata hai
Hans ki shanti se, man ko jagah mil jaata hai

Dil se jo bolti hai, voh baat pakshi ka gungun
Dilon ka jhula hi, prem ki dor hai bun

Hans ka jhalak dekho, jahan se bhatke nahi
Prem ki dhundh mein, sab sanmaano ki barfi

Inkaar ki jhalak mein, sach ka rang na dikhaye
Hans ke puchh se hi, man ke ghoor se bhaye

Moh ke jhanjhat mein, prem ki tarah dhoop
Hans ki madhur dhun se, bhool jaane hoop

Dikhe jo andhera, usmein roshni ka pal
Hans ki sair se, milti hai prem ki dal

Kashmir ki nadi, kabhi nahi thame koi
Prem ki baat se, hans ka raja rahe koi

Mitti se paida prana, patang ki chaal chalti
Hans ka awaaz suna, mann ka jal diya palti

Mitti mein jogi ka dhool, upar aakash ke rang
Hans pakshi ke sang, prem ki saansung

Prem ki bhavani, dhoop aur chhaya dono
Hans ki udan ko, har kadam samjho shono

Mann ki teer se nikal, barish ka jhalak hi
Hans ki udan par, prem ki dhool chaakhi

Bhakti ki baat bhi, milti hai uitsa ki roshni
Hans ke sang, man ki har raat bolbadi

Ajab si dhoop, dharti pe baarish bhi
Prem ka jahar, hans ki udan bhi

Jo birha ke aag me jale, piya paave us paar

Jo piya prem se jude, hoye sada suhaana

Jisme piya ki talab lage, wah phire din raaye

Jo man ko ulata phire, piya dwar hoye aaye

Piya ke naam bin jeewan, jaise binu paani naav
Prem ki boond par rahe, piya le chala bhaav

Maaya Ka Bojh Mann Tyage, Bhavajale Se Paar

Gyaan Bina Sab Andhiyaara, Kaise Paar Padaaye
Antar Ke Deep Jagaale, Taap Sabe Mitaaye

Kagad Likhai Gyaan Naa Hoye, Paddhai Lakh Baraabar
Ek Palak Antar Dhyan Liye, Bheetar Hoye Nistar

Mann Mein Aankh Lagaye Jisne, Dekha Antar Paar
Gyaan Sagar Dubki Maari, Mile Amrit Bhandar

Shabd Gyaan Ki Ganga Baha, Manava Nirmal Hoyi
Jo Is Snan Nahi Kiyaa, Bheetar Mail Moi

Aate Paani Mein Haath Dhoye, Mail Kachhu Na Jaaye
Gyaan Bina Jo Jeewan Jiye, Janma Gavaya Jaaye

Chaudah Bhuvan Ke Malak Hain, Ek Hi Aatam Jyot
Gyaan Talvaari Chala Jabe, Kate Bharama Ki Jaal

Gyaan Bhakti Do Sath Chale, Ek Pair Na Dole
Paar Utare Naav Tabai, Jab Dil Gaya Khole

Bina Gyaan Jo Bhes Kare, Paar Ki Aas Naahi
Kahai Kabir Antar Jaan Le, Tab Lagi Piya Paaye

Bahar Khoja Paar Na Paaya, Antar Milai Samaadh
Kahai Kabir Gyaan Tab Hoye, Jab Tute Sab Saadh

Paar Ki Naav Gyaan Hi Janiye, Chadhe Jo Antar Jaan
Bhavajal Tare Hansi Hansi Kar, Maaya Ka Kachhu Maan

Maaya Andhi Hove Jagat Mein, Gyaan Deepak Chaaye
Jisne Aatam Deep Jiya, So Paar Utar Aaye

Paar Paana Ho Ta Gyaan Ki, Naav Chadho Bhai
Moh Ka Bojh Phenk Karke, Paar Utaro Jaaye

Gyaan Jaise Badhe Badhe, Man Neecha Hoi Jaaye
Paar Wohi Bhavajal Tare, Jo Aapaash Mitaaye

Mann Ko Math Kar Gyaan Ki, Madni Kadhi Jaaye
Jo Pee Gyaan Amrit Wohi, Paar Utar Aaye

Andar Ka Gyaan Nahin, Bahar Bharam Badhaaye
Paar Ki Naav Bhoje Bhari, Saamne Hi Dub Jaaye

Gyaan Ki Boond Bina Ye Jeevan, Sookha Sarv Sangaar
Paar Utare Naav Tabai, Jab Deep Antar Bhaar

Jhoothi Gyaan Ki Dukaan Kare, Bikai Kachhu Na Saar
Paar Na Pahunchaave Koi, Antar Se Hai Khaar

Aatam Gyaan Hi Asali Dhan, Aur Sab Dhana Jhoot
Paar Utare Jo Is Dhan Mein, Baaqi Sab Kachhu Chhoot

Gyaan Bina Jo Maan Bada, Aap Ko Maha Gyaani
Antar Andh Bahar Dikhave, Jhoothi Sab Badaani

Mann Bina Gyaan Na Kachhu, Mann Se Paar Pasaar
Mann Haraave So Paar Gaya, Mann Jeetya Sansaar

Kabira Gyaan Ki Naav Chali, Bheetar Ki Sidhi Raah
Paar Utare Tab Jaaniye, Jab Tute Sab Chaah

Jo Antar Paar Na Tare Kabhu, Bahar Dera Daare
Gyaan Ki Dolak Bina Kandhe, Kaal Unhe Nipaare

Maaya Ka Jaal Gyaan Hi Kaate, Paar Utare Bhaai
Jyot Jagaa Aatam Andar, Taare Andhera Jaai

Antar Deep Jab Jaga Hai, Sab Bahar Ki Laaj
Paar Ki Naav Chadhi Bheetar, Kachhu Na Laage Kaaj

Paar Ki Bhaat Bina Gyaan Ke, Kaun Paar Paaye
Jaise Andhera Deep Bina, Kachhu Dikhai Na Jaaye

Ek Gyaan Jo Antarman Mein, Laakh Satav Na Maane
Paar Utare Bhavajal Upar, Tan Mann Sukh Hoye

Gyaan Rashmi Ek Antarman, Bheetar Deep Jagaaye
Paar Utare Naav Bina Bhi, Jis Mann Mail Bhagaaye

Mann Ke Anek Raste Dekhe, Gyaan Ek Hi Raah
Paar Utare Jo Is Par Chadhe, Kahe Kabir Yeh Saar

Paar Ki Aas Gyaan Mein Hai, Naav Chadhe Chalaai
Maaya Ke Moorakh Dube Hai, Apna Aap Gavaai

Jo Gyaan Ki Naav Mein Baitha, Kabhu Na Hove Haar
Antar Manthan Kar Saanche Mein, Paar Kare Sansaar

Mann Ka Bojh Na Chadhe Naav, Maaya Karat Aneka
Gyaan Talvaari Chala Jisne, Paar Utare Eka

Aatam Gyaan Ki Roti Khaaye, Amrit Piye Pyala
Paar Utare Naav Jabhi, Tan Mann Hoye Ujala

Bahut Likhai Parhaai Kari, Gyaan Na Hoyi Hathaai
Paar Utare Naav Tabai, Jab Hriday Deep Jagaai

Gyaan Ki Baat Na Mukh Se Kar, Bheetar Kare Nihaar
Paar Utare Naav Jabhi, Jab Aaye Antar Saar

Antar Gyaan Sujhe Na Jisne, Bahar Bhatake Jaaye
Paar Ki Naav Bina Kevat, Bhavajal Phir Aaye

Ek Gyaan Ke Bina Kahun, Kachhu Naahi Thikaana
Paar Utare Naav Tabai, Jab Hove Aatam Jaana

Mann Ka Nagar Gyaan Bina, Sada Andhera Thaan
Paar Utare Jyot Jaga Kar, Dekhe Aatam Gyaan

Jo Antar Se Gyaan Pachhaane, Bahar Kachhu Na Bole
Paar Utare Naav Usike, Bheetar Amrit Ghole

Paar Utarne Ki Chinta Mein, Sab Jag Bharamaye
Gyaan Bina Jo Dhoondhata, So Antar Khoye Jaaye

Gyaan Bina Naav Kate Nahi, Bhavajal Gahra Bhaar
Aatam Jaan Bina Bhai, Kaal Kare Ati Vaar

Jhootha Gyaan Jo Maan Kare, Maaya Se Rahe Sanga
Paar Utare Naav Tabai, Jab Kate Yeh Phaansa

Aatam Jaan Bina Kachhu, Paar Na Laage Paar
Gyaan Ke Kinaare Jo Chadha, So Tare Sansaar

Bina Gyaan Ye Mann Murakh, Phansa Maaya Jaal
Antar Se Jo Jagaaya, Paar Utare Sakal

Ek Palak Mein Gyaan Pragate, Paar Hove Sujaan
Naav Bhavajal Tabhi Tare, Jab Mile Aatam Jaan

Antar Gyaan Ki Dhool Na Udi, Paar Ki Aas Naahi
Naav Bina Bhavajal Mein To, Kaal Ghere Taahi

Gyaan Loot Ke Par Ko Diya, Antar Dhan Laahi
Paar Utare Naav Tabai, Jab Aatam Deep Jagaahi

Ahankar so ganvaar hai, jo dehin ko khaaye
Jyu tilki hava lage, deepak bujhi jaaye.

Patthar base patthar hai, jab tak ghis na khaaye
Jab garava so chhoriye, tab heera kahlaaye.

Ahankari ka siru uchaa, jyu dariya ki ler
Jhuke bina samudra ko, kabahu na paawe gher.

Abhimaan ki bel gahi, chadhi akash uchaay
Jhuke jab phal lage, jhuke bina na chhaay.

Jharn ke jal nirmal hai, jab aapanu ghata jaaye
Milat sagar sukh raas mein, tab amar pad paaye.

Dhan dhaan ke ahankari, dehe ko bhari maan
Jyu sukhi bel akas so, phal kachhu nahi jaan.

Ahankar ka sagar gahan, sansaar sab dobaaye
Jab se naiya nich bani, tab lage paar aaye.

Ahankar ka phanda gahi, phanse sansaar apaar
Jyu machhli lalach lage, jaave kavari dwaar.

Ahankari ko saathi mili, bane satru samaan
Prem taj garava laage, ghar aangan mein aag.

Ahankari ko gur mile, gyaan kabahu na paaye
Jyu ghrit ki bhaandi mein, paani sang na aaye.

Ahankar se aankh dhundhli, sacha dars na hoye
Jyu andhakari ghar mein, mukha dikhai na koye.

Sab te nichahu bane so, aapa tyag vichaar
Param pada rahe so, jasu aanand apaara.

Ahankari ki dor bandhi, luya chauraasees
Jab phore to nirala bane, param pada mein sees.

Sab ke bich jo base so, kaha kahe bada
Jo sab se nichahu rahe, soi param pada chada.

Ahankar ka pahaar gahan, chadhat manu thakaaye
Jab se nichahu ur baise, tab saras sukh paaye.

Patthar sahe sahas maari, aapu na kachhu bole
Garava sab taje jab tab, heera jag bich jaane.

Abhimaan ki jad gahi, phale jahar aneh
Jab garava ur chhoriye, tab amrit ras beh.

Ahankari ko prem mile, jame nahin ek saath
Jyu paani me tail rakh, kabahu na ek saath.

Ahankar mein jo dekhe, laage mukh sohavaan
Jyu pani ke bubuula, phootat chhin mein jaan.

Ahankari ke shringaar mein, dehi ko sundar maan
Jyu chhachhundar sona jadhe, bheetar kahu na jaan.

Ahankar mein jo jap kare, hari naam rataye
Jyu kunwa chadhat akas, jal nichahu samaaye.

Ahankar mein jo jap kare, phal kachhu naahi
Jyu sukhi bel chadhi hai, jhapat tutat jaahi.

Ahankar bina jo bole, amrit baani baan
Jo aapanu mukh le chale, saba jahar samaan.

Ahankar bina seedha, raah dekhe sacha
Jo aapanu mukh liye, gahira bhool racha.

Garava mein prem laage, jaise aag mein taan
Jab se nirmal jhuke rahe, tab lahe sukh chaan.

Patthar sam jhuke rahe, sahe sab kai maar
Garava tyag jo chale, lah param pada saar.

Ahankar ko aag lagai, prem rasaan chaan
Jo bujhaye ur antar, so paave param thaan.

Ahankar ke darpan mein, mukh apu so dikhaaye
Jyu paani par jhag base, taale mail lukaaye.

Ahankar ka khajana bharat, jagat mein kachhu na paaye
Jab se aapanu chhor diye, tab amar sukh aaye.

Ahankar bina jo gur lahe, ek pal mein maan
Jab se aapanu haath diye, tab rahe sujaan.

Ahankar ke baadh tale, naam japat na jaaye
Jab se garava chhor diye, tab premi ras paaye.

Ahankar ke baans bane, ghar mein jhagra bhaar
Nirmal nich ghar base, prem paalak saar.

Ahankar ka pedh bada, chhayamhi andhkaar
Jhuka rahe jab jhadi so, tab ujiyaar apaara.

Ahankar so chor hai, jo gunaan ko khaaye
Jab se nich basa rahe, tab rahe bhagwaan.

Ahankar ka bhaar uthai, chale na paaye kaan
Jab se aapanu phenk diye, tab lage sukha thaan.

Ahankar ki laath lage, gir pade sansaar
Nirmal nichahu jo rahe, wah bhaye bhav paar.

Ahankar kahan bigaare, jo aapanu hi maare
Nirmal nichahu bane so, jag mein naam savaare.

Ahankar ka rassa kheench, luya barahin maas
Jab se rassa chhoot gaya, tab lahe ram nivaas.

Ahankar se saat janam, rahe bhatak bharamaaye
Jab se nichahu bane so, tab preetam raah samaaye.

Ahankar ke laaddu mein, kachhu meet na paaye
Jab se aapanu chhor diye, tab meetha har paaye.

Ahankar ke kuen mein, sada gaadha paani
Jab se kuen ko chhode, tab mile amrit khaani.

Ahankar ke ghoonghat mein, sove jag bechaar
Jab se ghoonghat khole diye, tab dekhe ram dwaar.

Ahankar ke aangan mein, barse aag anera
Jab se aangan chhode diye, tab base raam dera.

Ahankar se jo chale, wah kabahu na paar
Jab se aapanu chhor diye, tab gahire te taar.

Aapanu jo ur chhor de, so sarvagat samaaye
Jyu paani mein namak mile, sarvatra rasa paaye.

Ahankar se jo chalai, chalat na paaye paar
Jyu ghoorni ke bail so, kahu na paave paar.

Ahankari nindiya sove, sapane bhaari bhoj
Nirmal nichahu jaage, tab lahe ram ke oj.

Ahankar ka chatra bada, chhaye sabke sir
Jab se chhatra chhor diya, tab ujaas ghar bhar.

Nirmal jo nichahu rahe, wah lakhon mein ek
Ahankari sansaar mein, kahu na paaye tek.

Ahankar ke gahire kuen, doobe sab sansaar
Jab se nichahu gahai laga, tab lahe sansaar.

Mann Udyam Din Raat Kare, Kahu Na Chhode Soye
Kahe Kabira Surati Dhar, Tab Laage Naam Hoye

Raat Andheri Mann Bharmata, Din Bhi Bharmat Jaaye
Kahe Kabira Aapa Chhodo, Piya Paas Bulaaye

Bhor Bhai Uth Mann Ko Dhar, Pehle Naam Japaaye
Phir Din Bhar Ka Kaam Kare, Sab Kuchh Sukh Paaye

Mann Ke Andhiyaare Mein, Kahun Din Raat Samaan
Kahe Kabira Naam Binu, Kabahun Na Aave Gyaan

Mann Mrig Jyon Trishnaa Bhara, Din Raat Dhaavata Jaaye
Kahe Kabira Naam Rasa Piya, Mann Sukh Thikaane Paaye

Mann Ser Saanp Samaan Jyon, Din Raat Dushit Khaaye
Kahe Kabira Naam Ki Mani, Mann Amiya Ras Paaye

Mann Udar Jyon Taranga Bhara, Tik Na Paave Kaama
Kahe Kabira Naam Ka Ankus, Mann Hoya Param Dhaama

Mann Bina Vaanhi Hansa Samaan, Din Raat Bharmat Jaaye
Kahe Kabira Naam Ki Dor, Laave Thaam Samaaye

Saachu Savera Tab Jaaniye, Jab Mann Jagat Hai Jaage
Raat Sapna Din Bhi Sapna, Jab Tak Mann Na Laage

Mann Panchhi Udiye Mat Jaai, Raat Din Rakho Baandh
Kahe Kabira Naam Ki Dor, Lagaavo Pankh Mein Gaandh

Mann Shatru Aru Mitra Dono, Din Raat Sang Jaaye
Kahe Kabira Jaako Jeete, Sada Sukh Thikaane Paaye

Mann Aaine Par Daag Sa, Din Raat Dikhlaaye
Kahe Kabira Naam Ragaade, Nirmal Roop Paaye

Mann Bajaara Bharam Ka Bhaara, Din Raat Bikhat Soye
Kahe Kabira Naam Rasa Le, Bheetar Ujiyaara Hoye

Savere Savera Mann Jage, Tab Jaane Dayaal
Raat Raha Jo Bhram Mein Soya, Naam Bina Kaval Kaal

Madhye Din Mein Mann Thakaaya, Kaam Krodh Se Aag
Kahe Kabira Surat Laga, Mit Jaaye Sabhi Taap

Mann Ghoda Baingan Bina, Din Raat Kaude Jaaye
Kahe Kabira Naam Ki Lagam, Tab Sukh Thikaane Paaye

Mann Naav Khevaiya Bina, Saagar Mein Bharmat Jaaye
Kahe Kabira Naam Khanjar, Paar Utare Aaye

Mann Nagari Panch Chor Basat, Din Raat Lootat Koye
Kahe Kabira Naam Saty Ka, Taalaa Laga Soye

Mann Kuaan Bina Paani Ka, Din Raat Pyaas Jalaaye
Kahe Kabira Naam Ras Barsat, Mann Tript Sukh Paaye

Mann Upavan Jyon Banjara, Din Raat Ujar Jaaye
Kahe Kabira Naam Beej Boye, Phal Amiya Paaye

Mann Baazaar Bajat Bheri, Din Raat Shun Na Paaye
Kahe Kabira Naam Tatt Dhuni, Bheetar Anahat Gaaye

Mann Jhilonha Raat Sapna, Din Mein Bhi Dikhlaaye
Kahe Kabira Jaago Re Bhaai, Sachhu Surat Lagaaye

Mann Gaja Mast Jyon Nachata, Din Raat Sab Bhulaaye
Kahe Kabira Vivek Ka Ankus, Tab Shanti Bheetar Paaye

Mann Taula Jhuthe Bhaar, Din Raat Jhuke Jaaye
Kahe Kabira Naam Rasa Tol, Sadaa Satye Samaaye

Mann Deep Jyon Aandhiyaara, Din Raat Bujhata Jaaye
Kahe Kabira Naam Ki Baati, Jare Sada Ujaaye

Mann Agni Trishnaa Ka Tel, Din Raat Jalaaye
Kahe Kabira Naam Rasa Jal, Sab Taap Bujhaaye

Mann Aatithi Chanchal Jyon, Din Raat Bharmat Jaaye
Kahe Kabira Naam Ghar Basaay, Phir Laage Na Jaaye

Mann Aangan Jyon Jhaadhi Bina, Din Raat Mail Soye
Kahe Kabira Naam Ki Jhaadhi, Aangan Saaf Hoye

Mann Nadi Bina Kinara, Din Raat Bahata Jaaye
Kahe Kabira Naam Kinara, Sab Samudra Samaaye

Mann Hiran Jyon Ban Bina, Din Raat Bhatkat Jaaye
Kahe Kabira Naam Ka Ban, Nij Sukh Paaye

Mann Chaar Dishi Daude Andha, Din Raat Thakaaye
Kahe Kabira Naam Bina Disha, Kahu Na Thikaane Paaye

Mann Bhaari Bhar Bhrama Ka, Din Raat Kandhe Laaye
Kahe Kabira Naam Chhabi Lakhi, Sab Kuchh Nirmal Paaye

Raat Sapna Din Dhoka, Mann Chor Sab Khaaye
Kahe Kabira Jaagat Rahe, Naam Dharo Bachaaye

Mann Gahara Paani Bhinna, Din Raat Dubata Jaaye
Kahe Kabira Naam Ki Naai, Upara Utare Paaye

Mann Khet Jyon Patthar Ka, Din Raat Boe Jaaye
Kahe Kabira Naam Ki Joti, Amrit Fal Paaye

Mann Dhol Bajat Kusangat, Din Raat Shor Sunaaye
Kahe Kabira Naam Ki Taal, Bheetar Surat Gaaye

Mann Gaagar Chhed Bhara Jyon, Din Raat Ras Tapaaye
Kahe Kabira Naam Mrittika, Ras Ke Pot Banaaye

Mann Chhaayaa Saath Jab Laage, Din Raat Dukh Hoye
Kahe Kabira Naam Ujaala, Chhaayaa Durata Soye

Mann Rasnaa Trishnaa Bhari, Din Raat Bisaraaye
Kahe Kabira Naam Amiya, Sab Mitthas Paaye

Mann Latto Laath Bina, Din Raat Ghumat Jaaye
Kahe Kabira Naam Ki Laath, Tham Ke Thikaane Paaye

Mann Ka Chaadar Jhooth Se Buni, Din Raat Odhat Jaaye
Kahe Kabira Naam Ka Soot, Ek Taana Samaaye

Mann Kaag Jyon Kapat Bhara, Din Raat Kaal Udaaye
Kahe Kabira Naam Ka Paankh, Soham Aakaash Samaaye

Mann Niranja Jyon Paani Mein, Din Raat Mila Jaaye
Kahe Kabira Naam Tat Chakh, Apana Aapa Paaye

Mann Putli Door Ke Khaatir, Din Raat Naache Jaaye
Kahe Kabira Naam Khevaaiya, Chaahi Taraf Bachaaye

Mann Aalas Bharam Ka Bhara, Din Raat Sota Jaaye
Kahe Kabira Naam Ki Laat, Jaga Kar Gyaan Paaye

Mann Aandha Bail Jyon Bandha, Din Raat Chakkar Khaaye
Kahe Kabira Naam Ki Aankh, Saba Dishi Dekh Paaye

Mann Maanai Tab Kya Kahe, Raat Din Ek Samaaye
Kahe Kabira Chhod Chadke, Jag Jaag Sach Paaye

Mann Tuta Ghada Paani Ka, Din Raat Baras Jaaye
Kahe Kabira Naam Ki Mritt, Pot Purna Banaaye

Mann Makdi Jyon Jaal Buna, Din Raat Phasat Jaaye
Kahe Kabira Naam Ka Jhaadu, Saaf Mail Chhudaaye

Mann Afeem Nashe Bhara Jyon, Din Raat Baurhata Jaaye
Kahe Kabira Naam Ki Maala, Sab Bhranti Man Haraaye

Maya paani ke budbude, chhinate hi bujh jaaye
Hansa vivek vichaari, tatte paar chali jaaye

Sansaar sukh dekhike, manva bauraya hoye
Jaagte mein hi sapana, yahu jeevan saba hoye

Kahun Kabir maya ko, maanat sab sansaar
Jaise chhaya deha ki, aatam tatva saar

Sone chandi ke putale, moh liya man maay
Jaate samay haath na, laga kachhu saath na jaay

Mohini maaya rani ne, phansa jeev bichaara
Hansa jaane ansh hamara, aadi ka pukaara

Taante bune maya ko, jhoothi aash lagaye
Kaal aave jhapat mein, ek na taante paaye

Paani ke garte mein, jeevan dubaya hoye
Hansa bin gyaan ke, na paaya tatva hoye

Chaar diwari moh ki, jeev andar dasa
Maya ke kapat kutira, sab andhera disha

Parpaanch mohini nagari, basat sab anjaana
Hansa jaag vichaari ke, paawe param thikaana

Dhana dhaanya putra poutra, maay ke bandhan thaare
Ulat palat mein haariye, ek na paawe saare

Maaya sabun ki jhaag jyon, chhinate hi mit jaaye
Hansa gyaan bina sab, ant samay pachhitaaye

Maaya ki jhoothi chhaya, suraj doobe jaaye raat
Hansa chal det gyani, param gati ki baat

Jaaki laagi laagari, sansaar mein sukh soye
Woh birla nikase hai, maaya phaas na paaye

Moh ka paash badhat hai, ghar ghar bandh banaaye
Hansa mukta hona chahe, tatte paar chala jaaye

Daulat dekhi lalachiya, maya mohi basaaye
Antar aru baahar mile, tabhi gati sukh paaye

Tinke ka sahaara le, jeev bawandar bhaage
Maya ke jhooth panth mein, kabahu naahin laage

Sapne dekha raj mahal, prabhaate bhaya pachaar
Yahu sansaar maya hai, kahu kabeer vichaar

Trishna pet ki aag se, maaya mohi jaraaye
Hansa in durgandh tat, saada jal chaakhaaye

Chakachaundh mohini ki, aankh na pheranhaar
Kabahu na paawe thira, chanchal chit sansaar

Hansa gandha tyage jab, nirmal jal chaakhe
Maya ke bikh ras se, saadhu man hataaye

Maaya kaahe ko rate, din doobe jaaye raat
Gyaan deep jalaa le, paawe sacchi baat

Jyon megh garajat aawe, boond barsat bheer
Maya ke jhoothi aasha, jeev lahete teer

Kaanch ke khilaune jaise, maaya jhoothi chaaye
Hansa jaag vichaari ke, sacchi gati paaye

Mrig trishna ja dil ki, pipasa kabahu na jaaye
Maya ke jhooth jal mein, phir phir aaya paaye

Rang mahal bandh liye, maaya mohi pasaare
Bhramit huye na jaane, aatma dwar na taare

Hansa bina vivek ke, jehar ras chaakhaaye
Maaya ke madhu moh mein, param pad kabahu na paaye

Ek din ke rajya jaise, maaya sukh thira naahi
Chhute sapna jaanike, chala ja paar maahi

Maaya ke jhoothe dhan mein, sab laagat lagaav
Hansa vivek bina, phir na paawe thaav

Chaadar taant bune hai, maaya mohi samaaye
Ek taar toote kahun, poori chhata na paaye

Hansa kamal phool chaakhe, gandha jal tajaaye
Maya ke bikh ras se, saadhu man hataaye

Baawari laagi maaya mein, juthi aasha bhaari
Pakshi pinjar mein simat, phir na ude bichhaari

Hansa jaise jal tyagi, sarovar tat na chaaye
Maya taji sat sangat mein, param sukh sada paaye

Maaya ke andh kupe mein, gire sab anjaan
Hansa gyaan ke pankh mein, ude paar mahaan

Sansaar ki haar jeet ko, maaya mohi dikhlaaye
Hansa vairaag chhooTe, param pada paaye

Maaya ke sone ka pinjar, pakshi basat suhaaye
Hansa bin gyaan ke, ant samay pachhitaaye

Sapana dekhi sukh lahe, jaagat hi dukhaaye
Maaya ke jhooth nagari, santaap hi santaaye

Jaaki laagi laagari, maaya mohi gumaaye
Woh birla gyaani jan, param tatva paaye

Paani mein chabi dekhi, maya mohi lubhaaye
Hansa aapko jaanike, sada nij gati paaye

Maaya rani ke aage, jeev lutat khaaye
Hansa viraag vichaari, param pada paaye

Maaya aaina dikhaawe, jhoothi chabi dikhaaye
Hansa aapko jaanike, mukh phira le jaaye

Andhakar maaya jaal mein, sab jeev ulajhaaye
Hansa guru vachaana sun, tatte paar chala jaaye

Paapi pet ki laag se, maaya mohi badhaaye
Hansa saadhu sanga te, sada mukti paaye

Chakravyuh maya ka ghana, gheri hai charo khaan
Hansa viveki jaane, bachat nij jaan

Maaya ke madhu ras mein, bhaawar phansa bhaar
Hansa saadhu sang mein, gaya paar

Heere moti maaya ke, man lalachit laaye
Hansa tat gyaan paane, kachhu maangat na aaye

Deha bina na chhaya, maaya jhoothi bataaye
Hansa atma nija pehchaane, tatte tatva paaye

Hansa naam sumaran kari, ulat tatte jaaye

Aasha ka maaya kaagaz, paani par samaaye
Hansa viraag vichaari, nij naam paaye

Andh kup maaya nagari, mit gayi sab laaj
Hansa gyaan prakaas mein, lahe nija kaaj

Jhoothe prem maaya mein, jeev phansa bhaar
Hansa nij gyaan te, paawe paar

Sona Bina Kasauti Ke, Pehachanat Na Koye
Guru Bina Gyan Kahan, Kahun Milat Na Hoye

Dhundhat Phire Jagat Mein, Sir Chadhe Guraahi
Satguru Mile Tab Jaani, Dharti Aakaashi

Maaya Ki Jaal Sab Phanse, Bhool Gaye Param Thikaan
Guru Aankh Katari De, Kaate Bhava Paash

Pet Bhare Bhoonjan Lage, Man Bhookha Ye Rahiyo
Guru Shabad Ke Ann Bina, Kaal Ghata Chaayo

Path Padhai Kitabaan Ke, Agyan Na Ghat Jaave
Ek Updesh Guru Ka Laakh, Bhava Saagar Taare

Kaag Uddai Aakash Ko, Guru Pankh Lagaave
Guru Bina Surat Kabahu, Na Paar Utaraave

Andher Ghar Deep Bina, Kaise Gyan Ujaaro
Guru Deep Liye Aave, Saba Akshar Ujaaro

Maanas Janam Durlabh Hai, Guru Mile Bahu Naahi
Bina Guru Naam Na Koyi, Paavai Jag Mein Naahi

Kankar Kuvari Baahar Se, Chhupa Sona Hoi
Guru Kasauti Lagaave Tab, Param Tatv Hoi

Saat Samandar Paar Kare, Kaha Suna Na Bhai
Guru Eka Akshar Kahyo, Tahi Mann Laai

Baans Baje Ghughari Na, Guru Dhun Bhulaave
Shishya Naam Ki Taan Pakar, Nij Mein Layaave

Bin Gur Agni Bina Jyun, Kaath Na Kachhu Jala
Guru Agni Se Laag Kar, Tan Man Hoi Ujala

Maaya Paash Ulajh Ke, Raahi Bhule Raah
Guru Kaatari Haath Dhar, Kaate Sab Paash

Mitha Bolat Sab Bhala, Kadhat Na Koi Bhaave
Guru Neem Ki Paath Dai, Rog Shok Mit Jaave

Surat Nirat Bin Guru Ke, Bhatakhan Lage Kaanhi
Ek Guru Disha Dikhade, Paar Utara Jaahi

Pahiye Bin Gadi Chale Na, Gati Bina Na Janhi
Guru Pahiya Guru Gati Hai, Aap Aap Bakhaani

Maati Se Dev Uthaaro, Ujiyaara Ho Jis Ghaadi
Guru Chakshu Se Dekhiye, Maahi Brahm Samaadhi

Din Raat Beeti Gayi, Janam Beeti Gayi Bhaai
Guru Na Mila Jo De Sakaai, Phir Kaahat Aae Jaai

Laakhon Mein Khojat Phira, Kotik Kareen Upaay
Guru Mile Tinhi Ko Jaka, Bhaag Likha Hriday Maahi

Jaise Sona Kasauti Se, Bahaar Nikara Aave
Guru Se Shishya Gyanvat, Param Pada Paave

Bhramar Guna Phul Phule Na, Bin Surat Samaave
Guru Shabad Madhu Paani De, Amrit Ras Paave

Koti Pustak Padhai Phira, Jnana Na Ur Dhaar
Guru Eka Boond Ki Baat, Kare Ujaala Saar

Ganga Yamuna Jamuna Sab, Tirath Kare Nivaas
Guru Charan Kamal Dhove, Sab Te Uttam Aas

Bina Guru Naam Na Sangi, Kaal Kute Jaai
Satguru Ke Sang Rahiyo, Param Pada Paaee

Tel Deeve Baati Bina, Andher Rahat Chhah
Guru Baati Lagave Tab, Ghar Hoi Ujaala

Raat Gavai Din Gavai, Jaagat Naam Bichaaro
Guru Jab Se Sang Milyo, Bhaya Nisa Din Sukh Saaro

Maala Japio Tan Khinchin, Man Bhayo Na Thikaan
Guru Naam Laga Tin Ke, Bhayo Nij Pada Nidaan

Suraj Chanda Taare Chhode, Guru Te Nij Chet
Param Gati Paave Taahi, Jab Guru Sang Preet

Guru Bin Koi Saadh Naahi, Iha Para Ki Daan
Guru Ko Praan Sampeeye, Na Taje Seva Jaan

Hans Dudh Bichhur Khoje, Naam Bin Guru Khoye
Guru Keeval Naam Diyo, Taaki Param Hoye

Jaise Aag Loha Tapai, Kaantaare Ho Jaaye
Guru Aag Se Shishya Ko, Sona Bana Banaaye

Kagaj Ka Parda Ghat Mein, Andar Raha Chhipe
Guru Utha Pakad Udaare, Dijo Bharpur Diipe

Machhari Jaal Phans Gayi, Paani Se Bichhur Raai
Guru Jaal Kate Taahi, Paar Lagaai

Jyun Tej Bina Chandra Ko, Aankh Naahi Dikhayo
Guru Prakash Milat Hi, Param Pada Sukh Payo

Aapas Mein Jhagadat Rahe, Dharm Adharm Ki Baat
Guru Eka Samajh Dikhade, Param Gati Ki Raah

Bina Baadal Barse Na, Bina Guru Na Gyan
Guru Baadal Guru Barse, Bhare Bhandaar Gyan

Sabar Julha Julaiya, Guru Agan Bujhaave
Guru Shishya Ko Shital Kar, Param Shanti Paave

Akathic Katha Kab Kahu, Guru Mukha Se Aave
Adha Akshar Sunat Hi, Mann Paar Utar Jaave

Atak Gayi Nadiyaa Bech, Paar Karan Ko Dhaave
Guru Naav De Kevat Kar, Paar Utar Jaave

Mandir Masjid Dekhat, Dekhat Kitabe Aaye
Guru Dil Mein Basaave Jo, Tahi Saach Dikhlaaye

Sukh De Dukhat Dukh Raha, Mann Ke Duhayi Maan
Guru Duaar Par Jaai Ke, Mite Sab Vedana

Ghrit Katora Maatha Dhare, Diyan Deep Jalaaye
Guru Deepak Bina Sab, Andhera Hee Rah Jaaye

Nainon Mein Kodi Lagi, Sab Kachhu Dhaundhla Hoye
Guru Netra Se Dekhiye, Laakhon Mein Ek Hoye

Bandhe Huye Hath Hain Sab, Bandhan Mein Jag Naach
Guru Katar Se Kaat Ke, Kare Atam Ki Saaj

Hiran Samudra Pyasit, Samudra Ke Andar
Guru Boond Pilaave Jo, Bhave Param Amrit

Panchhi Bina Pankh Ke, Kaise Aakaash Jaai
Guru Pankh Lagaave Tab, Bhava Saagar Taai

Chauraasi Ke Beech Phire, Bhool Gaye Nij Naam
Guru Uddhaar Kare Jinki, Unka Achal Thikaan

Mool Na Jaani Baaunri, Patiyaan Se Hi Kaam
Guru Jad Se Pahichaan Kar, Phool Phal Bane Naam

Agni Bina Bhathi Mein, Kaise Bane Bhojan
Guru Agni Jagaave Tab, Pakat Saadhu Bhojan

Kahe Kabira Suno Bhaai, Guru Bina Bhram Na Jaaye
Guru Mile To Aap Liye, Param Pada Paaye

Kabira jhukna naa bhulo, jahan ahankar udaai
Jitna phal bhare ped, utni jhuki sarkaaee

Ahankar ki shikha oonchi, jeevan tel ghataye
Kahe Kabira nichu raha, tab andhera jaye

Khali bartan jab bajta, shor sunai de
Bhara hua jo chup hai, amrit usi ke haath

Nadiya le naam chali, jab talak alag bahaye
Samudra mein jo mili, phir paani paani ho paaye

Meethe paani mein goad, apna rang bhulaaye
Ahankar ko aise gholo, nirmal ras ho jaaye

Sui jo sidhi khadi hai, kapde ko na chhoo
Jhuki hui so chaliya, tan man ka dhaaga piroo

Oosa ki bund paat par, garbh se oonchi rahe
Suraj uge gir paadi, mitti mein hi mil jaaye

Roti jo tawe phoole, ahankar mein phat jaaye
Jhuki hui so pake sada, ras mein bhar jaaye

Chatri jo oonchi rahe, aakaas se takkar khaaye
Jhuki rahe to bachaawe, chaanv tale sukh paaye

Baans khokhla bheetar se, ooncha aakaas ghere
Kahe Kabira jhukna chahiye, jahan ahankar badere

Neeche ka sil tikaa rahe, ooper ki ghoom jaaye
Kahe Kabira samajh lijo, jo tikaa so raj paaye

Rassi jo jhuke litaawe, bhaari bojh uthaaye
Seedha hua na kucch kare, aap hi taan akad jaaye

Suraj ki kiran oonchi, taap sara bikhere
Jhuk kar saagar choo liya, phir badal ban ghume

Naiyya mein paani bhara, garbh se oonchi rahe
Wohi paani use dubo de, jab tak na jhuk jaaye

Deepak ki lau jhuki, tej bada bikhere
Ahankar mein lau oonchi, dhuan hi saath laaye

Darwaza jab jhuka rahe, andar ko raah de
Seedha khada jo rahe, koyi na andar aaye

Ooncha jo mahaal banaawe, neenv neechi rahe
Neev neechi na hoti to, dewaar kahan se aaye

Jo doosre ki aankh mein, dekhe dhul ka taan
Apni aankh mein jo na dekhe, wohi ahankar jaan

Fakeer jo maanga jhuk kar, daat pe bhikshaa paaye
Ahankar mein sir uthaawe, darwaaze se duraaye

Balti jab kuan mein jhuke, paani bhar laaye
Oonchi jo khadi rahe, khali hi palat aaye

Kaaya ka aakaar bada, ek din mitti khaaye
Kahe Kabira jhuk rahiyo, jis din kaaya jaaye

Sheesh jhukaawe jisko, aakaash mil jaaye
Ooncha jo sir uthaawe, dharati mein samaaye

Phal bhari shakh jhuke, panchhi aakar khaaye
Sookhi jhadi oonchi rahe, chhaya bhi na paaye

Kagad ki naav bana li, apna naam likh chaat
Paani par tairan lagi, to doobi wo ika baat

Ahankar ka pahad bana, charon ore ghira
Kahe Kabira jhuk ja bhai, tabhi paar utara

Mehnat ki jo roti hai, swaad usmein mitha rahe
Ahankar ki jad laage, phir wahi roti jeher bane

Bans jab jhuk jaay hai, tab bansuri bana
Ahankar mein jo sidha rahe, woh taan na suna

Bandar jo shaakhe ooncha, phal ko haath na laaye
Jhuk kar jo ghar aawe, baag ka phal chakhaaye

Ghada jab ghumaawe neeche, paani baahar aaye
Ahankar mein ooncha rahe, paani bhi na paaye

Patang oonchi jaave, maanjha haath mein rahe
Ahankar mein jo chhuda le, zameen pe wahi jaaye

Aaine mein jo dekhe, sar ooncha dikh jaaye
Jhuka diyo to duniya ki, thokar kahi na khaaye

Bojh uthawe jo kandha, jhukka hua badhaaye
Ahankar mein tan ubhraawe, kamar kahin dabaaye

Chhat pe jo baitha rahe, sabako neecha dekhe
Jhuka hua jo aankh rahe, aap hi ko pekhe

Jhoothi shaan se laade, jaisa hawa ka gubaara
Ek chhuri ke chhote se, phus ho jaaye saara

Jitna aap ko neecha kare, utna ooncha hoye
Kahe Kabira aisa sant, jagat mein koyi koye

Guru ke dar par jo aawe, sar jhukaawe maan
Ahankar se jo sir uthe, phir bhatakata jaan

Ant samay jo aawe, sab kachhu reh jaaye
Ahankar ka bojh saath, kaise paar jaaye

Jaise kumhara chak par, ghum ghum maanse maare
Aise maaya ke haath mein, ahankar ko pasaare

Koyal ki jab bolti, kanth lai piyaaye
Ahankar se jo bolti, kaan sabhi jalaaye

Dhanvaan ka bachva jo, khilone mein abhimaan
Tut gayi khilauni raat, phir roye nidaan

Jhuka hua jo hal hai, dharti chaak lagaaye
Seedha laat jo chale, kheti kaun chalaaye

Aadmi ka sar ooncha, guru se kaise mile
Jhuka hua jo sheesh diya, tab preetam ko chhule

Baarish ki boond aakaas, oonchi chalat aaye
Dharti mein jab samaawe, phir aapapan bhulaaye

Chhavi paani mein likhi, haath lage mitaaye
Ahankar ki chhavi aysi, jhuke bin na jaaye

Ahankar mein jo dhyaave, man kahin na rahe
Jhuka hua jo dhyaan lage, saat lok samaawe

Ahankar ka ek aadmi, sangi sabse bhaage
Vinamrata ka jo bhare, sang mein sab lagaaye

Chota sa diya aadmi, ahankar mein bujh jaaye
Jhuka hua jo deepak, saat ghar ujiyaare

Aisa koyi sant nahi, jo ooncha kahlaawe
Santo mein jo neecha rahe, so santo mein paawe

Tula ka paala jo neecha, bhaari bojh uthaaye
Ahankar mein paala ooncha, kewal haal dikhlaaye

Kahe Kabira suno bhai, ahankar ki maaya
Jhukna uska aant hai, ooncha chale na paaya

Prem Bina Ye Jeevan Hai, Jaise Bina Jal Meen
Piya Bina Ye Hriday Rahe, Soonapan Hi Cheen

Prem Ka Rang Jo Chale Tan Par, Rang Chhute Na Koy
Jaise Chakki Ka Loha Bhayo, Fir Alag Na Hoy

Viraha Agan Tan Jalave, Nain Barasat Neer
Piya Bina Sukh Kachhu Naahin, Bheetar Base Peer

Prem Bina Tirtha Vyarth Hai, Puja Bhi Hai Jhooth
Jahan Piya Ki Prit Na Lagi, Lakh Karam Ko Booth

Piya Ko Paane Ka Upay, Sumiran Din Raat
Jo Hiya Hin Rahata Man Mein, Kevat Jhuthi Baat

Premiya Ke Liye Jagat Mein, Koi Nahin Paraye
Jo Piya Ke Rang Rahe Ranga, So Jag Te Nyaare

Prem Ka Saagar Athah Hai, Taran Na Paave Kinar
Jo Doobat Jaat Gahire, Paawe Moti Bichar

Prem Ki Dhoti Tan Pari, Tan Man Dono Rang
Jo Piya Pritam Se Mil Gaye, Karat Na Koi Bhang

Piya Ke Bhajan Binu Ye Man, Bhatakat Dar Dar Jaaye
Jaise Bhavara Bina Phool Ke, Kahin Na Thehar Paaye

Prem Deewana Kabir Kahe, Apana Ho Gaya Bisaar
Jahan Piya Aan Basat Hai, Tahan Kaun Karat Vikar

Antar Piya Se Milat Rahe, To Bahar Kya Maang
Jaise Kuwa Andara Bhara, Baahar Chhai Aangaang

Nainan Mein Base Piya To, Kya Dekhoo Aur
Jab Andar Hi Mil Gaya Saajan, Toot Gaye Sab Dwar

Bina Guru Ke Shabd Pritam, Milaavat Nahi Hoyi
Jo Binu Naam Bhatakat Phire, Janam Janam Ki Khoyi

Jo Deh Mein Pritam Dekhat, So Bhrmiya Kho Jaaye
Deh Gehi To Sahej Basi, Piya Hridai Ko Aaye

Pritam Ka Milap Kya Kari, Jab Tak Haumai Bhari
Palak Mein Base Ahankar To, Piya Kahan Na Pari

Prem Ki Sejiya Piya Sang, Jo Rat Din Soye
Jo Binu Piya Ke Nind Laave, Janam Phal Sab Khoye

Piya Bina Ye Tan Hai Jaise, Diya Bina Baati
Ujiyaari Kahan Se Lage, Jab Nahin Hai Jyoti

Piya Ke Pyar Mein Jiyenge, Piya Ke Pyar Mein Maran
Jo Piya Bina Deh Rakhe, So Khele Janam Haaran

Prem Ki Dor Jo Bandhi Hai, Kabhu Na Woh Tute
Jo Piya Atal Sang Rahe, Janam Maran Te Chhute

Piya Ki Yaad Mein Beete Din, Piya Ki Yaad Me Raat
Jab Yaad Rahe Nirantar, Tab Nahin Kaal Ki Kaat

Pritam Ka Pyar Kya Hai, Mukh Se Kahat Na Jaaye
Jo Lekhat Paat Kagad Par, Piya Piya Keh Na Paaye

Prem Ki Ganga Gahri Hai, Snaan Kare Jo Koye
Tan Man Shuddha Ho Jaat Hai, Piya Milan Tab Hoye

Piya Ko Khojat Hiye Bhayo, Antar Hi Mein Aan
Jis Bheetar Base Pritam, Tako Bahar Kya Jaan

Prem Deewana Hoi Ke Phire, Dar Dar Jaane Jaaye
Antar Piya Milan Hoy Jaba, Ghar Aangan Laaye

Piya Ki Prit Jo Kare Koi, Lobh Moh Tyag Jaaye
Jaise Macchi Pani Se Prit, Taise Hi Piya Paaye

Antar Ki Jyoti Prem Ki, Koi Nahin Bujhaye
Andhera Saara Jab Mit Gaya, Piya Darshan Paaye

Piya Ke Roop Ko Dekhat Nahin, Ankhiyan Ke Andhe
Jo Prem Maarag Mein Chale, Wahi Nainon Ke Nidhe

Prem Ke Bhandar Gahire Hai, Moti Ginti Nahin
Jo Dubki Maare Gahire, Paawe Piya Waahin

Piya Ke Daras Ka Lobh Kahu, Jo Aur Lobh Dikhave
Jo Piya Darshan Lobhi Hai, So Janam Saphal Paave

Piya Ki Preet Asaadh Hai, Saadh Se Koi Na Paave
Saadh Tyag Kar Premiya, Jab Piya Antar Aave

Prem Ki Baat Koi Samjhe, Man Ka Taap Bujh Jaaye
Pritam Bina Jo Kachhu Bole, So Sab Jhuthi Laaye

Piya Ki Yaad Mein Tan Sukhat, Yaad Mein Man Ghabraaye
Yaad Bina Ik Chhin Kahu, Aaram Na Paaye

Piya Ko Paane Ki Aas Mein, Premi Sab Kuchh LuTaaye
Deh Dhari Ka Sab Kachhu Jare, Tab Prem Ke Rang Aaye

Prem Ki Aag Tan Jalave, Koni Bacha Paave
Jis Tan Mein Prem Ki Aag Nahin, Piya Us Ghar Na Paave

Prem Mein Doobat Jaat Hai, Piya Milan Ki Aash
Baras Baras Beet Gaye Re, Nain Base Udaash

Piya Bina Jo Sukh Paavat, To Sukh Nahin Vikaar
Jaise Hans Bina Sarovar, Kaise Kare Singaar

Prem Ki Raah Jo Chalat Hai, Na Rakhe Or Ko Dhyan
Jo Piya Ka Chit Mein Chinhat, Nahin Kachhu Durgam Maan

Piya Ki Prit Jo Maan Liyo, Lobh Moh Sab Jaaye
Jaise Chandan Ka Van Basat, Ta Tah Kaun Chhupaaye

Piya Ke Pyar Mein Jo Rahe, Taake Jag Ki Kaun Chint
Jahan Prem Ki Jyoti Jage, Taahin Andhiyara Mint

Piya Ke Bina Hriday Soon, Jaise Ghat Bina Chand
Jo Piya Aan Base Hriday, Taake Poora Anand

Piya Ki Prem Agan Mein, Jo Jarat Tan Hoye
Us Tan Ki Kushboo Chhaavat, Lok Sab Rang Doye

Prem Ki Dor Atal Hai, Jor Se Chhute Na Koye
Jab Piya Antar Aan Base, Tab Maran Na Hoye

Piya Ko Paane Ke Kaaran, Premi Kachhu Na Chhod
Dhana Dhaanya Kul Kutamb Sab, Pritam Prem Mein Tod

Piya Ke Naam Ki Dhun Mein, Jo Man Ko Hi Lagaaye
Us Man Ko Kaal Na Chhoo Sake, Nahin Antar Jaaye

Piya Ki Oat Kabir Kahe, Binu Gur Koyi Na Paave
Guru Kripa Bina Pritam Ke, Kahin Na Kahu Aave

Piya Ki Yaad Mein Roihat, Nainan Mein Neer
Piya Binu Ve Prit Rahat, Sakal Hoye Adheer

Piya Ki Baani Sunat Hiye, Lagat Prem Ki Aag
Pritam Baani Jo Na Sunat, Taake Jeevan Bhaag

Piya Ke Bina Tan Soon, Jaise Sangeet Bina Taan
Jo Piya Mein Hi Sada Basat, Paawe Param Gyaan

Prem Ka Saagar Gahira Hai, Naave Ke Na Kinar
Jo Doobat Doobat Jaat Hai, Paawe Piya Adhar

Piya Ke Pritam Ki Gaath Hai, Antar Ke Sab Taar
Jo Akhand Prem Se Rahe, Paawe Piya Paar
